akhila-rasāmṛta-mūrtiḥ prasṛmara-ruci-ruddha-tārakā-pāliḥ । kalita-śyāmā-lalito rādhā-preyān vidhur jayati ।। hṛdi yasya preraṇayā pravartito ahaṃ varāka-rūpo api । tasya hareḥ pada-kamalaṃ vande caitanya-devasya ।।
viśrāma-mandiratyā tasya sanātana-tanor mad-īśasya । bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhur bhavatu sadāyam pramodāya ।। bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhau carataḥ paribhūta-kāla-jāla-bhiyaḥ । bhakta-makarān aśīlita-mukti-nadīkān namasāmi ।।
mīmāṃsaka-baḍavāgneḥ kaṭhinām api kuṇṭhayann asau । sphuratu sanātana suciraṃ tava bhakti-rasāmṛtāmbhodhiḥ ।। bhakti-rasasya prastutir akhila-jagaṅ-maṅgala-prasaṅgasya । ajñenāpi mayāsya kriyate suhṛdām pramodāya ।।
etasya bhagavad-bhakti-rasāmṛta-payonidheḥ । catvārah khalu vakṣyante bhāgāḥ pūrvādayaḥ kramāt ।। tatra pūrve vibhāge asmin bhakti-bheda-nirūpake । anukrameṇa vaktavyaṃ laharīṇāṃ catuṣṭayam ।।
ādyā sāmānya-bhakty-āḍhyā dvitīyā sādhanānvitā । bhāvāśritā tṛtīyā ca turyā prema-nirūpikā ।। tatrādau suṣṭhu vaiśiṣṭyam asyāḥ kathayituṃ sphuṭam । lakṣaṇaṃ kriyate bhakter uttamāyāḥ satāṃ matam ।।
anyābhilāṣitā-śūnyaṃ jñāna-karmādy-anāvṛtam । ānukūlyena kṛṣṇānuśīlanaṃ bhaktir uttamā ।। sarvopādhi-vinirmuktaṃ tat-paratvena nirmalam । hṛṣīkeṇa hṛṣīkeśa-sevanaṃ bhaktir ucyate ।।
śrī-bhāgavatasya tṛtīya-skandhe ca ahaituky avyavahitā yā bhaktiḥ puruṣottame ।। sālokya-sārṣṭi-sāmīpya-sārūpyaikatvam apy uta । dīyamānaṃ na gṛhṇanti vinā mat-sevanaṃ janāḥ ।। sa eva bhakti-yogākhya ātyantika udāhṛtaḥ ।।
sālokyetyādi-padyastha-bhaktotkarṣa-ṇirūpaṇam । bhakter viśuddhatā-vyaktyā lakṣaṇe paryavasyati ।। kleśa-ghnī śubhadā mokṣa-laghutā-kṛt sudurlabhā । sāndrānanda-viśeṣātmā śrī-kṛṣṇākarṣiṇī ca sā ।।
tatrāsyāḥ kleśaghnatvam - kleśās tu pāpaṃ tad-bījam avidyā ceti te tridhā ।। tatra pāpam aprārabdhaṃ bhavet pāpaṃ prārabdhaṃ ceti tad dvidhā ।। yathāgniḥ susamiddhārciḥ karoty edhāṃsi bhasmasāt । tathā mad-viṣayā-bhaktir uddhavaināṃsi kṛtsnaśaḥ ।।
yat-prahvaṇad yat-smaraṇād api kvacit । kutaḥ punas te bhagavan nu darśanāt ।। durjātir eva savanāyogyatve kāraṇam matam । durjāty-ārambhakaṃ pāpaṃ yat syāt prārabdham eva tat ।।
aprārabdha-phalaṃ pāpaṃ kūṭaṃ bījaṃ phalonmukham । krameṇaiva pralīyeta viṣṇu-bhakti-ratātmanām ।। tais tāny aghāni pūyante tapo-dāna-vratādibhiḥ । nādharmajaṃ tad-hṛdayaṃ tad apīśāṅghri-sevayā ।।
karmāśayaṃ grathitam udgrathayanti santaḥ । sroto-gaṇās tam araṇaṃ bhaja vāsudevam ।। kṛtānuyātrā-vidyābhir hari-bhaktir anuttamā । avidyāṃ nirdahaty āśu dāva-jvāleva pannagīm ।।
śubhāni prīṇanaṃ sarva-jagatām anuraktatā । sadguṇāḥ sukham ity-ādīny ākhyātāni manīṣibhiḥ ।। yenārcito haris tena tarpitāni jaganty api । rajyanti jantavas tatra jangamāḥ sthāvarā api ।।
sarvair guṇais tatra samāsate surāḥ । manorathenāsati dhāvato bahiḥ ।। sukha-pradatvam sukhaṃ vaiṣayikaṃ brāhmam aiśvaraṃ ceti tat tridhā ।। siddhayaḥ paramāścaryā bhuktir muktiś ca śāśvatī ।
nityaṃ ca paramānando bhaved govinda-bhaktitaḥ ।। bhūyo api yāce deveśa tvayi bhaktir dṛḍhāstu me । yā mokṣānta-caturvarga phaladā sukhadā latā ।। manāg eva prarūḍhāyāṃ hṛdaye bhagavād-ratau ।
puruṣārthās tu catvārās tṛṇāyante samantataḥ ।। yathā śrī-nārada-pañcarātre hari-bhakti-mahā-devyāḥ sarvā mukty-ādi-siddhayaḥ । bhuktyaś cādbhutās tasyāś ceṭikāvad anuvratāḥ ।। iti । sādhanaughair anāsangair alabhyā sucirād api । hariṇā cāśvadeyeti dvidhā sā syāt sudurlabhā ।।
jñānataḥ sulabhā muktir bhuktir yajñādi-puṇyataḥ । seyaṃ sādhana-sāhasrair hari-bhaktiḥ sudurlabhā ।। daivaṃ priyaḥ kula-patiḥ kva ca kiṅkaro vaḥ । muktiṃ dadāti karhicit sma na bhakti-yogam ।।
brahmānando bhaved eṣa cet parārddha-guṇīkṛtaḥ । naiti bhakti-sukhāmbhodheḥ paramāṇu-tulām api ।। tvat-sākṣāt-karaṇāhlāda-viśuddhābdhi-sthitasya me । sukhāni goṣpadāyante brāhmāṇy api jagad-guro ।।
tvat-kathāmṛta-pāthodhau viharanto mahā-mudaḥ । kurvanti kṛtinaḥ kecit catur-vargaṃ tṛṇopamam ।। kṛtvā hariṃ prema-bhājaṃ priya-varga-samanvitam । bhaktir vaśīkarotīti śrī-kṛṣṇākarṣiṇī matā ।।
na sādhyati mām yogo na sāṅkhyaṃ dharma uddhava । na svādhyāyas tapas tyāgo yathā bhaktir mamorjitā ।। lokaṃ punānā munayo abhiyanti । guḍhaṃ paraṃ brahma manuṣya-liṅgam ।।
agrato vakṣyamāṇāyās tridhā bhakter anukramāt । dviśaḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ padair etan māhātyaṃ parikīrtitam ।। svalpāpi rucir eva syād bhakti-tattvāvabodhikā । yuktis tu kevalā naiva yad asyā apratiṣṭhatā ।।
yatnenāpādito apy arthaḥ kuśalair anumātṛbhiḥ । abhiyuktatarair anyair anyathaivopapādyate ।। sā bhaktiḥ sādhanaṃ bhāvaḥ premā ceti tridhoditā ।। kṛti-sādhyā bhavet sādhya-bhāvā sā sādhanābhidhā ।
nitya-siddhasya bhāvasya prākaṭyaṃ hṛdi sādhyatā ।। sā bhaktiḥ saptama-skandhe bhaṅgyā devarṣiṇoditā ।। yathā saptame tasmāt kenāpy upāyena manaḥ kṛṣṇe niveśayet ।। iti । vaidhī rāgānugā ceti sā dvidhā sādhanābhidhā ।।
yatra rāgānavāptatvāt pravṛttir upajāyate । śāsanenaiva śāstrasya sā vaidhī bhaktir ucyate ।। tasmād bhārata sarvātmā bhagavān īśvaro hariḥ । śrotavyaḥ kīrtitavyaś ca smartavyaś cecchatābhayam ।।
smartavyaḥ satataṃ viṣṇur vismartavyo na jātucit । sarve vidhi-niṣedhāḥ syur etayor eva kiṅkarāḥ ।। ity asau syād vidhir nityaḥ sarva-varṇāśramādiṣu । nityatve apy asya nirṇītam ekādaśy-ādivat-phalam ।।
mukha bāhūru-pādebhyaḥ puruṣasyāśramaiḥ saha । catvāro jajñire varṇā guṇair viprādayaḥ pṛthak ।। ya eṣāṃ puruṣaṃ sākṣād ātma-prabhavam īśvaram । na bhajanty avajānanti sthānād bhraṣṭāḥ patanty adhaḥ ।।
evaṃ kriyā-yoga-pathaiḥ pumān vaidika-tāntrikaiḥ । arcann ubhyataḥ siddhiṃ matto vindaty abhīpsitām ।। surarṣe vihitā śāstre harim uddiśya yā kriyā । saiva bhaktir iti proktā tayā bhaktiḥ parā bhavet ।।
yaḥ kenāpy atibhāgyena jāta-śraddho asya sevane । nātisakto na vairāgya-bhāg asyām adhikāry asau ।। yadṛcchayā mat-kathādau jāta-śraddho astu yaḥ pumān । na nirviṇṇo nātisakto bhakti-yogo asya siddhidaḥ ।।
uttamo madhyamaś ca syāt kaniṣṭhaś ceti sa tridhā ।। śāstre yuktau ca nipuṇaḥ sarvathā dṛḍha-niścayaḥ । prauḍha-śraddho adhikārī yaḥ sa bhaktāv uttamo mataḥ ।। tatra madhyamaḥ yaḥ śāstrādiṣv anipuṇaḥ śraddhāvān sa tu madhyamaḥ ।।
tatra kaniṣṭhaḥ yo bhavet komala-śraddhaḥ sa kaniṣṭho nigadyate ।। tatra gītādiṣūktānāṃ caturṇām adhikāriṇām । madhye yasmin bhagavatah kṛpā syāt tat-priyasya vā ।। sa kṣīṇa-tat-tad-bhāvaḥ syāc chuddha-bhakty-adhikāravān ।
yathebhaḥ śaunakādiś ca dhruvaḥ sa ca catuḥsanaḥ ।। bhukti-mukti-spṛhā yāvat piśācī hṛdi vartate । tāvad bhakti-sukhasyātra katham abhyudayo bhavet ।। tatrāpi ca viśeṣeṇa gatim aṇvīm anicchataḥ ।
bhaktir hṛta-manaḥ-prāṇān premṇā tān kurute janān ।। vilāsa-hāsekṣita-vāma-sūktaiḥ । anicchato me gatim aṇvīṃ prayuṅkte ।। śrī kṛṣṇa-caraṇāmbhoja-sevā-nirvṛta-cetasām ।
eṣāṃ mokṣāya bhaktānāṃ na kadācit spṛhā bhavet ।। sudurlabho artheṣu caturṣv apīha । bhavat-padāmbhoja-niṣevaṇotsukaḥ ।। mat-pāda-sevābhiratā mad-īhāḥ ।
sabhājayante mama pauruṣāṇi ।। sālokya-sārṣṭi-sāmīpya- sārūpyaikatvam apy uta । dīyamānaṃ na gṛhṇanti vinā mat-sevanaṃ janāḥ ।। dhyānād bhavaj-jana-kathā-śravaṇena vā syāt ।
kiṃ tv antakāsi-lulitāt patatāṃ vimānāt ।। na yatra yuṣmac-caraṇāmbujāsavaḥ । vidhatsva karṇāyutam eṣa me varaḥ ।। prārthyāṃ śriyaṃ sura-varaiḥ sadayāvalokām ।
sevānurakta-manasām abhavo api phalguḥ ।। na sārva-bhaumaṃ na rasādhipatyam । samañjasa tvā virahayya kāṅkṣe ।। nārāyaṇa-parāḥ sarve na kutaścana bibhyati ।
svargāpavarga-narakeṣv api tulyārtha-darśinaḥ ।। ārādhanaṃ bhagavata īhamānā nirāśiṣaḥ । ye tu necchanty api paraṃ te svārtha-kuśalāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। kiṃ tair guṇa-vyatikarād iha ye sva-siddhāḥ ।
sāraṃ juṣāṃ caraṇayor upagāyatāṃ naḥ ।। daityākrāntaṃ hṛdaya-kamalaṃ tad-gṛhaṃ pratyabodhi । muktis teṣāṃ na hi bahumatā nārasiṃhāparaiḥ kim ।। vāñchanti ye vai bhagavat-prapannāḥ ।
gāyanta ānanda-samudra-magnāḥ ।। mat-sevayā pratītaṃ te sālokyādi-catuṣṭayam । necchanti sevayā pūrṇāḥ kuto anyat kāla-viplutam ।। na pārameṣṭhyaṃ na rasādhipatyam ।
vāñchanti yat-pāda-rajaḥ-prapannāḥ ।। carita-mahāmṛtābdhi-parivarta-pariśramaṇāḥ । caraṇa-saroja-haṃsa-kula-saṅga-visṛṣṭa-gṛhāḥ ।। na kiñcit sādhavo dhīrā bhaktā hy ekāntino mama ।
vāñchanty api mayā dattaṃ kaivalyam apunar-bhavam ।। na sārvabhaumaṃ na rasādhipatyam । mayy arpitātmecchati mad vinānyat ।। naivecchaty āśiṣaḥ kvāpi brahmarṣir mokṣam apy uta ।
bhaktiṃ parāṃ bhagavati labdhavān puruṣe avyaye ।। na cānyaṃ vṛṇe ahaṃ vareśād apīha । sadā me manasy avirāstāṃ kim anyaiḥ ।। tvayā mocitau bhakti-baddhau kṛtau ca ।
na mokṣe graho me asti dāmodareha ।। na dharma kāmam arthaṃ vā mokṣaṃ vā varadeśvara । prārthaye tava pādābje dāsyam evābhikāmaye ।। punaḥ punar varān ditsur viṣṇur muktiṃ na yācitaḥ ।
bhaktir eva vṛtā yena prahlādaṃ taṃ namāmy ahaṃ ।। yadṛcchayā labdham api viṣṇor dāśarathes tu yaḥ । naicchan mokṣaṃ vinā dāsyaṃ tasmai hanumate namaḥ ।। bhava-bandha-cchide tasyai spṛhayāmi na muktaye ।
bhavān prabhur ahaṃ dāsa iti yatra vilupyate ।। dharmārtha-kāma-mokṣeṣu necchā mama kadācana । tvat-pāda-pañkajasyādho jīvitaṃ dīyataṃ mama ।। mokṣa-sālokya-sārūpyān prārthaye na dharādhara ।
icchāmi hi mahābhāga kāruṇyaṃ tava suvrata ।। muktānām api siddhānāṃ nārāyaṇa-parāyaṇaḥ । sudurlabhaḥ praśāntātmā koṭiṣv api mahā-mune ।। tathā paramahaṃsānāṃ munīnām amalātmanām ।
bhakti-yoga-vidhānārthaṃ kathaṃ paśyema hi striyaḥ ।। ātmārāmāś ca munayo nirgranthā apy urukrame । kurvanty ahaitukīṃ bhaktim ittham-bhūta-guṇo hariḥ ।। atra tyājyatayaivoktā muktiḥ pañca-vidhāpi cet ।
sālokyādis tathāpy atra bhaktyā nātivirudhyate ।। sukhaiśvaryottarā seyaṃ prema-sevottarety api । sālokyādir dvidhā tatra nādyā sevā-juṣaṃ matā ।। kintu premaika-mādhurya-juṣa ekāntino harau ।
naivāṅgīkurvate jātu muktiṃ pañca-vidhām api ।। tatrāpy ekāntināṃ śreṣthā govinda-hṛta-mānasāḥ । yeṣāṃ śrīśa-prasādo api mano hartuṃ na śaknuyāt ।। siddhāntatas tv abhede api śrīśa-kṛṣṇa-svarūpayoḥ ।
rasenotkṛṣyate kṛṣṇa-rūpam eṣā rasa-sthitiḥ ।। śāstrataḥ śrūyate bhaktau nṛ-mātrasyādhikāritā । sarvādhikāritāṃ māgha-snānasya bruvatā yataḥ । dṛṣtāntitā vaśiṣṭhena hari-bhaktir nṛpaṃ prati ।।
yathā pādme - sarve adhikāriṇo hy atra hari-bhaktau yathā nṛpa ।। antyajā api tad-rāṣṭre śaṅkha-cakrāṅka-dhāriṇaḥ । samprāpya vaiṣṇavīṃ dīkṣāṃ dīkṣitā iva sambabhuḥ ।। ananuṣṭhānato doṣo bhakty-aṅgānāṃ prajāyate ।
na karmaṇām akaraṇād eṣa bhakty-adhikāriṇām ।। niṣiddhācārato daivāt prāyaścittaṃ tu nocitam । iti vaiṣṇava-śāstrāṇāṃ rahasyaṃ tad-vidāṃ matam ।। sve sve adhikāre yā niṣṭhā sā guṇaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।
viparyayas tu doṣaḥ syād ubhayor eṣa niścayaḥ ।। bhajann apakvo atha patet tato yadi । ko vārtha āpto abhajatāṃ sva-dharmataḥ ।। ājñāyaiva guṇān doṣān mayādiṣṭān api svakān ।
dharmān santyajya yaḥ sarvān māṃ bhajet sa ca sattamaḥ ।। na kiṅkaro nāyam ṛṇī ca rājan । gato mukundaṃ parihṛtya kartam ।। sarva-dharman parityājya mām ekaṃ śaraṇaṃ vraja ।
ahaṃ tvāṃ sarva-pāpebhyo mokṣayiṣyāmi mā sucaḥ ।। yathā vidhi-niṣedhau tu muktaṃ naivopasarpataḥ । tathā na spṛśato rāmopāsakaṃ vidhi-pūrvakam ।। tyaktāny abhāvasya hariḥ pareśaḥ ।
dhunoti sarvaṃ hṛdi sanniviṣṭaḥ ।। hari-bhakti-vilāse asyā bhakter aṅgāni lakṣaśaḥ । kintu tāni prasiddhāni nirdiśyante yathāmati ।। āśritāvāntarāneka-bhedaṃ kevalam eva vā ।
ekaṃ karmātra vidvadbhir ekaṃ bhakty-aṅgam ucyate ।। guru-pādāśrayas tasmāt kṛṣṇa-dīkṣādi-śikṣaṇam । viśrambheṇa guroḥ sevā sādhu-vartmānuvartanam ।। sad-dharma-pṛcchā bhogādi-tyāgaḥ kṛṣṇasya hetave ।
nivāso dvārakādau ca gaṅgāder api sannidhau ।। vyāvahāreṣu sarveṣu yāvad-arthānuvartitā । hari-vāsara-sammāno dhātry-aśvatthādi-gauravam ।। eṣām atra daśāṅgānāṃ bhavet prārambha-rupatā ।।
saṅga-tyāgo vidūreṇa bhagavad-vimukhair janaiḥ । śiṣyādy-ananubandhitvaṃ mahārambhādy-anudyamaḥ ।। bahu-grantha-kalābhyāsa-vyākhyā-vāda-vivarjanam ।।vyāvahāre apy akārpaṇyaṃ śokādy-avaśa-vartitā ।। anya-devān avajñā ca bhūtānudvega-dāyitā ।
sevā-nāmāparādhānām udbhavābhāva-kāritā ।। kṛṣṇa-tad-bhakta-vidveṣa-vinindādy-asahiṣṇutā । vyatirekatayāmīṣāṃ daśānāṃ syād anuṣṭhitīḥ ।। asyās tatra praveśāya dvāratve apy aṅga-viṃśateḥ ।
trayāṃ pradhānam evoktaṃ guru-pādāśrayādikam ।। dhṛtir vaiṣṇava-cihṇānāṃ harer nāmākṣarasya ca । nirmālyādeś ca tasyāgre tāṇḍavaṃ daṇḍavan-natiḥ ।। abhyutthānam anuvrajyā gatiḥ sthāne parikramaḥ ।
arcanaṃ paricaryā ca gītaṃ saṅkīrtanaṃ japaḥ ।। vijñaptiḥ stava-pāṭhaś ca svādo naivedya-pādyayoḥ । dhūpa-mālyādi-saurabhyaṃ śrī-mūrteḥ spṛṣṭir īkṣaṇam ।। ārātrikotsavādeś ca śravaṇaṃ tat-kṛpekṣaṇam ।
smṛtir dhyānaṃ tathā dāsyaṃ sakhyam ātma-nivedanam ।। nija-priyopaharaṇaṃ tad-arthe akhila-ceṣṭitam । sarvathā śaraṇāpattis tadīyānāṃ ca sevanam ।। tadīyās tulasī-śāstra-mathurā-vaiṣṇavādayaḥ ।
yathā-vaibhava-sāmagrī sad-goṣṭhībhir mahotsavaḥ ।। ūrjādaro viśeṣeṇa yātrā janma-dinādiṣu । śraddhā viśeṣataḥ prītiḥ śrī-mūrter aṅghri-sevane ।। śrīmad-bhāgavatārthānām āsvādo rasikaiḥ saha ।
sajātīyāśaye snigdhe sādhau saṅgaḥ svato vare ।। nāma-saṅkīrtanaṃ śrī-mathurā-maṇḍale sthitiḥ ।। aṅgānāṃ pañcakasyāsya pūrvaṃ vilikhitasya ca । nikhila-śraiṣṭhya-bodhāya punar apy atra kīrtanam ।।
iti kāya-hṛṣīkāntaḥ-karaṇānām upāsanāḥ ।।catuḥṣaṣṭiḥ pṛthak sāṅghātika-bhedāt kramādināḥ ।।athārṣānumatenaiṣām udāharaṇam īryate ।। tasmād guruṃ prapadyeta jijñāsuḥ śreya uttamam । śābde pare ca niṣṇātaṃ brahmaṇy upaśamāśrayam ।। tatra bhāgavatān dharmān śikṣed gurv-ātma-daivataḥ ।
amāyayānuvṛttyā yais tuṣyed ātmātma-do hariḥ ।। ācāryaṃ māṃ vijānīyān nāvamanyeta karhicit । na martya-buddhyāsūyeta sarva-deva-mayo guruḥ ।। sa mṛgyaḥ śreyasāṃ hetuḥ panthāḥ santāpa-varjitaḥ ।
anvāpta-śramaṃ pūrve yena santaḥ pratasthire ।। śruti-smṛti-purāṇādi-pañcarātra-vidhiṃ vinā । aikāntikī harer bhaktir utpātāyaiva kalpate ।। bhaktir aikāntikī veyam avicārāt pratīyate ।
vastutas tu tathā naiva yad aśāstrīyatekṣyate ।। acirād eva sarvārthaḥ sidhyaty eṣām abhīpsitaḥ । sad-dharmasyāvabodhāya yeṣāṃ nirbandhinī matiḥ ।। harim uddiśya bhogāni kāle tyaktavatas tava ।
viṣṇu-loka-sthitā sampad-alolā sā pratīkṣate ।। saṃvatsaraṃ vā ṣaṇmāsān māsaṃ māsārdham eva vā । dvārakā-vāsinaḥ sarve narā nāryaś caturbhujāḥ ।। aho kṣetrasya māhātmyaṃ samantād daśa-yojanam ।
diviṣṭhā yatra paśyanti sarvān eva caturbhujān ।। kṛṣṇāṅghri-reṇv-abhyadhikāmbu-netrī । kas tāṃ na seveta mariṣyamāṇaḥ ।। yāvatā syāt sva-nirvāhaḥ svīkuryāt tāvad artha-vit ।
ādhikye nyūnatāyāṃ ca cyavate paramārthataḥ ।। sarva-pāpa-praśamanaṃ puṇyam ātyantikaṃ tathā । govinda-smāraṇaṃ nṝṇām ekadaśyām upoṣaṇam ।। aśvattha-tulasī-dhātrī-go-bhūmisura-vaiṣṇavāḥ ।
pūjitāḥ praṇatāḥ dhyātāḥ kṣapayanti nṝṇām agham ।। varaṃ huta-vaha-jvālā-pañjarāntar-vyavasthitiḥ । na śauri-cintā-vimukha-jana-saṃvāsa-vaiśasam ।। āliṅganaṃ varaṃ manye vyāla-vyāghra-jalaukasām ।
na saṅgaḥ śalya-yuktānāṃ nānā-devaika-sevinām ।। na śiṣyān anubadhnīta granthān naivābhyased bahūn । na vyākhyām upayuñjīta nārambhān ārabhet kvacit ।। alabdhe vā vinaṣṭe vā bhakṣyācchādana-sādhane ।
aviklava-matir bhūtvā harim eva dhiyā smaret ।। śokādy-avaśa-vartitā, yathā tatraiva śokāmarṣādibhir bhāvair ākrāntaṃ yasya mānasam । kathaṃ tatra mukundasya sphūrti-sambhāvanā bhavet ।। harir eva sadārādhyaḥ sarva-deveśvareśvaraḥ । itare brahma-rudrādyā nāvajñeyāḥ kadācana ।।
piteva putraṃ karuṇo nodvejayati yo janam । viśuddhasya hṛṣīkeśas tūrṇaṃ tasya prasīdati ।। mamārcanāparādhā ye kīrtyante vasudhe mayā । vaiṣṇavena sadā te tu varjanīyāḥ prayatnataḥ ।।
sarvāparādha-kṛd api mucyate hari-saṃśrayaḥ । harer apy aparādhān yaḥ kuryād dvipadapāṃśulaḥ ।। nāmāśrayaḥ kadācit syāt taraty eva sa nāmataḥ । nāmno hi sarva-suhṛdo hy aparādhāt pataty adhaḥ ।।
nindāṃ bhagavataḥ śrṇvaṃs tat-parasya janasya vā । tato nāpaiti yaḥ so api yāty adhaḥ sukṛtāc cyutaḥ ।। ye bāhu-mūla-paricihṇita-śaṅkha-cakrāḥ । te vaiṣṇavā bhuvanam āśu pavitrayanti ।।
hari-nāmākṣara-yutaṃ bhāle gopī-mṛḍaṅkitam । tulasī-mālikoraskaṃ spṛśeyur na yamodbhaṭāḥ ।। kṛṣṇa-nāmākṣarair gātram aṅkayec candanādinā । sa loka-pāvano bhutvā tasya lokam avāpnuyāt ।।
tvayopayukta-srag-gandha-vāso alaṅkāra-carcitāḥ । ucchiṣṭa-bhojino dāsās tava māyāṃ jayemahi ।। kṛṣṇottīrṇaṃ tu nirmālyaṃ yasyāṅgaṃ spṛśate mune । sarva-rogais tathā pāpair mukto bhavati nārada ।।
yo nṛtyati prahṛṣṭātmā bhāvair bahuṣu bhaktitaḥ । sa nirdahati pāpāni manvantara-śateṣv api ।। nṛtyatāṃ śrī-pater agre tālikā-vādanair bhṛśam । uḍḍīyante śarīra-sthāḥ sarve pātaka-pakṣiṇaḥ ।।
daśāśvamedhāvabhṛthair na tulyaḥ । kṛṣṇa-praṇāmī na punar-bhavāya ।। yān ārūḍhaṃ puraḥ prekṣya samāyāntaṃ janārdanam । abhyutthānaṃ naraḥ kurvan pātayet sarva-kilbiṣam ।।
rathena saha gacchanti pārśvataḥ pṛṣṭhato agrataḥ । viṣṇunaiva samāḥ sarve bhavanti śvapadādayaḥ ।। - sthāne gatiḥ sthānaṃ tīrthaṃ gṛhaṃ cāsya tatra tīrthe gatir yathā ।। saṃsāra-maru-kāntāra-nistāra-karaṇa-kṣamau ।
slāghyau tāv eva caraṇau yau hares tīrtha-gāminau ।। pravīśann ālayaṃ viṣṇor darśanārthaṃ subhaktimān । na bhūyaḥ praviśen mātuḥ kukṣi-kārāgṛhaṃ sudhīḥ ।। viṣṇuṃ pradakṣinī-kurvan yas tatrāvartate punaḥ ।
tad evāvartanaṃ tasya punar nāvartate bhave ।। catur-vāraṃ bhramībhis tu jagat sarvaṃ carācaram । krāntaṃ bhavati viprāgrya tat-tīrtha-gamanādikam ।। śuddhi-nyāsādi-pūrvāṅga-karma-nirvāha-pūrvakam ।
arcanam tūpacārāṇāṃ syān mantreṇopapādanam ।। svargāpavargayoḥ puṃsāṃ rasāyāṃ bhuvi sampadām । sarvāsām api siddhīnāṃ mūlaṃ tāc-caraṇārcanaṃ ।। śrī-viṣṇor arcanaṃ ye tu prakurvanti narā bhuvi ।
te yānti śāśvataṃ viṣṇor ānandaṃ paramaṃ padam ।। paricaryā tu sevopakaraṇādi-pariṣkriyā । tathā prakīrṇaka-cchatra-vāditrādyair upāsanā ।। muhūrtaṃ vā muhūrtārdhaṃ yas tiṣṭhed dhari-mandire ।
sa yāti paramaṃ sthānaṃ kim u śuśrūṣaṇe ratāḥ ।। aśeṣa-janmopacitaṃ malaṃ dhiyaḥ । yathā padāṅguṣṭha-viniḥsṛtā sarit ।। aṅgāni vividhāny eva syuḥ pūjā-paricaryayoḥ ।
na tāni likhitāny atra grantha-bāhulya-bhītitaḥ ।। brāhmaṇo vāsudevākhyaṃ gāyamāno aniśaṃ param । hareḥ sālokyam āpnoti rudra-gānādhikaṃ bhavet ।। - atha saṃkīrtanam nāma-līlā-guṇadīnām uccair-bhāṣā tu kīrtanam ।।
kṛṣṇeti maṅgalaṃ nāma yasya vāci pravartate । bhasmībhavanti rājendra mahā-pātaka-koṭayaḥ ।। līlā-kathās tava nṛsiṃha viriñca-gītāḥ । durgāṇi te pada-yugālaya-haṃsa-saṅgaḥ ।।
sviṣṭasya sūktasya ca buddhi-dattayoḥ । yad uttamaḥśloka-guṇānuvarṇanam ।। - atha japaḥ mantrasya sulaghūccāro japa ity abhidhīyate ।। kṛṣṇāya nama ity eṣa mantraḥ sarvārtha-sādhakaḥ ।
bhaktānāṃ japatāṃ bhūpa svarga-mokṣa-phala-pradaḥ ।। harim uddiśya yat kiñcit kṛtaṃ vijñāpanaṃ girā । mokṣa-dvārārgalān mokṣas tenaiva vihitas tava ।। samprārthanātmikā dainya-bodhikā lālasāmayī ।
ity ādir vividhā dhīraiḥ kṛṣṇe vijñaptir īritā ।। yuvatīnāṃ yathā yūni yūnāṃ ca yuvatau yathā । mano abhiramate tadvan mano abhiramatāṃ tvayi ।। mat-tulyo nāsti pāpātmā nāparādhī ca kaścana ।
parihāre api lajjā me kiṃ brūve puruṣottama ।। kadā gambhīrayā vācā śriyā yukto jagat-pate । cāmara-vyagra-hastaṃ mām evaṃ kurv iti vakṣyasi ।। kadāhaṃ yamunā-tīre nāmāni tava kīrtayan ।
udbāṣpaḥ puṇḍarīkākṣa racayiṣyāmi tāṇḍavam ।। - atha stava-pāṭhaḥ proktā manīṣibhir gītā-stava-rājādayaḥ stavāḥ ।। śrī-kṛṣṇa-stava-ratnaughair yeṣāṃ jihvā tv alaṅkṛtā । namasyā muni-siddhānāṃ vandanīyā divaukasām ।।
stotraiḥ stavaś ca devāgre yaḥ stauti madhusūdanam । sarva-pāpa-vinirmukto viṣṇu-lokam avāpnuyāt ।। vīśeṣataḥ pāda-jalena siktam । prāpṇoti yajñāyuta-koṭi-puṇyam ।।
na dānaṃ na havir yeṣāṃ svādhyāyo na surārcanam । te api pādodakaṃ pītvā prayānti paramāṃ gatim ।। āghrāṇaṃ yad dharer datta-dhūpocchiṣṭasya sarvataḥ । tad-bhava-vyāla-daṣṭānāṃ nasyaṃ karma viṣāpaham ।।
praviṣṭe nāsikā-randhre harer nirmālya-saurabhe । sadyo vilayam āyāti pāpa-pañjara-bandhanam ।। āghrāṇaṃ gandha-puṣpāder arcitasya tapodhana । viśuddhiḥ syād anantasya ghrāṇasyehābhidhīyate ।।
spṛsṭvā viṣṇor adhiṣṭhānaṃ pavitraḥ śraddhayānvitaḥ । pāpa-bandhair vinirmuktaḥ sarvān kāmān avāpnuyāt ।। vṛndāvane tu govindaṃ ye paśyanti vasundhare । na te yama-puraṃ yānti yānti puṇya-kṛtāṃ gatim ।।
koṭayo brahma-hatyānām agamyāgama-koṭayaḥ । dahaty āloka-mātreṇa viṣṇoḥ sārātrikaṃ mukham ।। ratha-sthaṃ ye nirīkṣante kautikenāpi keśavam । devatānāṃ gaṇāḥ sarve bhavanti śvapacādayaḥ ।।
ādi-śabdena pūjā-darśanaṃ, yathāgneye pūjitaṃ pūjyamānaṃ vā yaḥ paśyed bhaktito harim ।। - atha śravaṇam śravaṇaṃ nāma-carita-guṇādīnāṃ śrutir bhavet ।। saṃsāra-sarpa-daṣṭa-naṣṭa-ceṣṭaika-bheṣajam । kṛṣṇeti vaiṣṇavaṃ mantraṃ śrutvā mukto bhaven naraḥ ।।
pīyūṣa-śeṣa-saritaḥ paritaḥ sravanti । tān na spṛśanty aśana-tṛḍ-bhaya-śoka-mohāḥ ।। saṅgīyate abhīkṣṇam amaṅgala-ghnaḥ । kṛṣṇe amalāṃ bhaktim abhīpsamānaḥ ।।
bhuñjāna evātma-kṛtaṃ vipākam । jīveta yo mukti-pade sa dāya-bhāk ।। atha smṛtiḥ yathā kathaṃ cin-manasā sambandhaḥ smṛtir ucyate ।। smṛte sakala-kalyāṇa-bhājanaṃ yatra jāyate ।
puruṣaṃ tam ajaṃ nityaṃ vrajāmi śaraṇaṃ harim ।। prayāṇe cāprayāṇe ca yan-nāma smaratāṃ nṝṇām । sadyo naśyati pāpaugho namas tasmai cid-ātmane ।। atha dhyānam dhyānam rupa-guṇa-krīḍā-sevādeḥ suṣṭhu cintanam ।।
bhagavac-caraṇa-dvandva-dhyānaṃ nirdvandvam īritam । pāpino api prasaṅgena vihitaṃ suhitaṃ param ।। ye kurvanti sadā bhaktyā guṇānusmaraṇaṃ hareḥ । prakṣīṇa-kaluṣaughās te praviśanti hareḥ padam ।।
sarva-mādhurya-sārāṇi sarvādbhutamayāni ca । dhyāyan hareś caritrāṇi lalitāni vimucyate ।। mānasenopacārena paricarya hariṃ sadā । pare vāṅ-manasā'gamyaṃ taṃ sākṣāt pratipedire ।।
atha dāsyam dāsyaṃ karmārpaṇaṃ tasya kaiṅkaryam api sarvathā ।। tasmin samarpitaṃ karma svābhāvikam apīśvare । bhaved bhāgavato dharmas tat-karma kimutārpitam ।। karma svābhāvikaṃ bhadraṃ japa-dhyānārcanādi ca ।
itīdaṃ dvividhaṃ kṛṣṇe vaiṣṇavair dāsyam arpitam ।। mṛdu-śraddhasya kathitā svalpā karmādhikāritā । tad-arpitaṃ harau dāsyam iti kaiścid udīryate ।। īhā yasya harer dāsye karmaṇā manasā girā ।
nikhilāsv apy avasthāsu jīvan-muktaḥ sa ucyate ।। atha sakhyam viśvāso mitra-vṛttiś ca sakhyaṃ dvividham īritam ।। pratijñā tava govinda na me bhaktaḥ praṇaśyati । iti saṃsmṛtya saṃsmṛtya prāṇān saṃdhārayāmy aham ।।
smṛtir ajitātma-surādibhir vimṛgyāt । lava-nimiṣārdham api yaḥ sa vaiṣṇavāgryaḥ ।। śraddhā-mātrasya tad-bhaktāv adhikāritva-hetutā । aṅgatvam asya viśvāsa-viśeṣasya tu keśave ।।
paricaryā parāḥ kecit prāsādeṣu ca śerate । manuṣyam iva taṃ draṣṭuṃ vyāvahartuṃ ca bandhuvat ।। rāgānugāṅgatāsya syād vidhi-mārgānapekṣatvāt । mārga-dvayena caitena sādhyā sakhya-ratir matā ।।
niveditātmā vicikīrṣito me । mayātma-bhuūyāyā ca kalpate vai ।। artho dvidhātma-śabdasya paṇḍitair upapāyate । dehy-ahantāspadaṃ kaiścid dehaḥ kaiścin mamatva-bhāk ।।
guṇato asāni yathā tathā-vidhaḥ । aham adyaiva mayā samarpitaḥ ।। cintāṃ kuryān na rakṣāyai vikrītasya yathā paśoḥ । tathārpayan harau dehaṃ viramed asya rakṣanāt ।।
duṣkaratvena virale dve sakhyātma-nivedane । keṣāṃcid eva dhīrāṇāṃ labhate sādhanārhatām ।। yad yad iṣṭatamaṃ loke yac cāti-priyam ātmanaḥ । tat tan nivedayen mahyaṃ tad ānantyāya kalpate ।।
laukikī vaidikī vāpi yā kriyā kriyate mune । hari-sevānukūlaiva sā kāryā bhaktim icchatā ।। tavāsmīti vadan vācā tathaiva manasā vidan । tat-sthānam āśritas tanvā modate śaraṇāgataḥ ।।
tvāṃ prapanno asmi śaraṇaṃ deva-deva janārdana । iti yaḥ śaraṇaṃ prāptas taṃ kleśād uddharāmy aham ।। atha tadīyānāṃ sevanam । tulāsyaḥ, yathā skānde rogāṇām abhivanditā nirasanī siktāntaka-trāsinī ।
nyastā tac-caraṇe vimukti-phaladā tasyai tulasyai namaḥ ।। dṛṣtā spṛṣṭā tathā dhyātā kīrtitā namitā stutā । ropitā sevitā nityaṃ pūjitā tulasī śubhā ।। navadhā tulasīṃ devīṃ ye bhajanti dine dine ।
yuga-koṭi-sahasrāṇi te vasanti harer gṛhe ।। atha śāstrasya, śāstram atra samākhyātaṃ yad bhakti-pratipādakam ।। vaiṣṇavāni tu śāstrāṇī ye śṛṇvanti paṭhanti ca । dhanyās te mānavā loke tesāṃ kṛṣṇaḥ prasīdati ।।
vaiṣṇavāni tu śāstrāṇī ye arcayanti gṛhe narāḥ । sarva-pāpa-vinirmuktā bhavanti sura-vanditāḥ ।। tiṣṭhate vaiṣṇavaṃ śāstraṃ likhitaṃ yasya mandire । tatra nārāyaṇo devaḥ svayaṃ vasati nārada ।।
sarva-vedānta-sāraṃ hi śrī-bhāgavatam iṣyate । tad-rasāmṛta-tṛptasya nānyatra syād ratiḥ kvacit ।। mathurāṃ ca parityajya yo anyatra kurute ratim । mūḍho bhramati saṃsāre mohitā mama māyayā ।।
trailokya-varti-tīrthānāṃ sevanād durlabhā hi yā । parānanda-mayī siddhir mathurā-sparṣa-mātrataḥ ।। śrutā smṛtā kīrtitā ca vāñchitā prekṣitā gatā । spṛṣṭā śritā sevitā ca mathurābhīṣṭadā nṛṇām ।
iti khyātaṃ purāṇeṣu na vistāra-bhiyocyate ।। ārādhanānāṃ sarveṣāṃ viṣṇor ārādhanaṃ param । tasmāt parataraṃ devi tadīyānāṃ samarcanam ।। yat-sevayā bhagavataḥ kūṭa-sthasya madhu-dviṣaḥ ।
rati-rāso bhavet tīvraḥ pādayor vyasanārdanaḥ ।। śaṅkha-cakrāṅkita-tanuḥ śirasā mañjarī-dharaḥ । gopī-candana-liptāṅgo dṛṣtaś cet tad-aghaṃ kutaḥ ।। yeṣāṃ saṃsmaraṇāt puṃsāṃ sadyaḥ śuddhyanti vai gṛhāḥ ।
kiṃ punar darśana-sparśa-pāda-śaucāsanādibhiḥ ।। ye me bhakta-janāḥ pārtha na me bhaktāś ca te janāḥ । mad-bhaktānāṃ ca ye bhaktās te me bhaktatamā matāḥ ।। yāvanti bhagavad-bhakter aṅgāni kathitānīha ।
prāyas tāvanti tad-bhakta-bhakter api budhā viduḥ ।। yaḥ karoti mahīpāla harer gehe mahotsavam । tasyāpi bhavati nityaṃ hari-loke mahotsava ।। yathā dāmodaro bhakta-vatsalo vidito janaiḥ ।
tasyāyaṃ tādṛśo māsaḥ svalpam apy uru-kārakaḥ ।। bhuktiṃ muktiṃ harir dadyād arcito anyatra sevinām । bhaktiṃ tu na dadāty eva yato vaśyakarī hareḥ ।। sā tv añjasā harer bhaktir labhyate kārttike naraiḥ ।
mathurāyāṃ sakṛd api śrī-dāmodara-sevanāt ।। yasmin dine prasūteyaṃ devakī tvāṃ janārdana । tad-dinaṃ brūhi vaikuṇṭha kurmas te tatra cotsavam । tena samyak-prapannānāṃ prasādaṃ kuru keśavaḥ ।।
mama nāma-sadāgrāhī mama sevā-priyaḥ sadā । bhaktis tasmai pradātavyā na tu muktiḥ kadācana ।। śuka-mukhād amṛta-drava-saṃyutam । muhur aho rasikā bhuvi bhāvukāḥ ।।
pariniṣṭhito api nairguṇye uttamaḥśloka-līlayā । gṛhita-cetā rājarṣe ākhyānaṃ yad adhītavān ।। tulayāma lavenāpi na svargaṃ nāpunar-bhavam । bhagavat-saṅgi-saṅgasya martyānāṃ kimutāśiṣaḥ ।।
yasya yat-saṅgatiḥ puṃso maṇivat syāt sa tad-guṇaḥ । sva-kūlarddhyai tato dhīmān sva-yūthyān eva saṃśrayet ।। etan nirvidyamānānām icchatām akuto-bhayam । yogināṃ nṛpa nirṇītaṃ harer nāmānukīrtanaṃ ।।
gītvā ca mama nāmāni vicaren mama sannidhau । iti bravīmi te satyaṃ krīto ahaṃ tasya cārjuna ।। yena janma-sahasrāṇi vāsudevo niṣevitaḥ । tan-mukhe hari-nāmāni sadā tiṣṭhanti bhārata ।।
nāma cintāmaṇiḥ kṛṣṇaś caitanya-rasa-vigrahaḥ । pūrṇaḥ śuddho nitya-mukto abhinnatvān nāma-nāminoḥ ।। ataḥ śrī-kṛṣṇa-nāmādi na bhaved grāhyaṃ indriyaiḥ । sevonmukhe hi jihvādau svayam eva sphuraty adaḥ ।।
anyeṣu puṇya-tīrtheṣu muktir eva mahā-phalam । muktaiḥ prārthyā harer bhaktir mathurāyāṃ tu labhyate ।। tri-vargadā kāmināṃ yā mumukṣūṇāṃ ca mokṣadā । bhaktīcchor bhaktidā kas tāṃ mathurāṃ nāśrayed budhaḥ ।।
aho madhu-purī dhanyā vaikuṇṭhāc ca garīyasī । dinam ekaṃ nivāsena harau bhaktiḥ prajāyate ।। durūhādbhuta-vīrye asmin śraddhā dūre astu pañcake । yatra svalpo api sambandhaḥ sad-dhiyāṃ bhāva-janmane ।।
vaṃśī-nyastādhara-kiśalayām ujjvalāṃ candrakeṇa । mā prekṣiṣṭhās tava yadi sakhe bandhu-sange asti raṅgaḥ ।। varṇāḥ karṇādhvani pathi katāmānupurvyād bhavadbhiḥ । yad garhantaḥ sukhamayam amī mokṣam apy ākṣipanti ।।
skhalann antaḥ-phullo dadhad atipṛthuṃ vepathum api । na jāte kiṃ tāvan matir iha gṛhe nābhiramate ।। śruti-patham agha-śatror nāmā-gāthā prayātā । tadavadhi dadhad-antar-mānasaṃ śāmyatīva ।।
sphuṭita-nava-kadambālambi-kūjad-dvirephā । manasi kam api bhāvaṃ kānana-śrīs tanoti ।। alaukika-padārthānām acintyā śaktir īdṛśī । bhāvaṃ tad-viṣayaṃ cāpi yā sahaiva prakāśayet ।।
keṣāṃcit kvacid aṅgānāṃ yat kṣudraṃ śrūyate phalaṃ । bahir-mukha-pravṛttyaitat kintu mukhyaṃ phalaṃ ratiḥ ।। saṃmataṃ bhakti-vijñānāṃ bhakty-aṅgatvaṃ na karmaṇām ।। tāvat karmāṇi kurvīta na nirvidyeta yāvatā ।
mat-kathā-śravaṇādau vā śraddhā yāvan na jāyate ।। jñāna-vairāgyayor bhakti-praveśāyopayogitā । īṣat prathamam eveti nāṅgatvam ucitaṃ tayoḥ ।। yad ubhe citta-kāṭhinya-hetū prāyaḥ satāṃ mate ।
sukumāra-svabhāveyaṃ bhaktis tad-dhetur īritā ।। tasmān mad-bhakti-yuktasya yogino vai mad-ātmanaḥ । na jñānaṃ na ca vairāgyaṃ prāyaḥ śreyo bhaved iha ।। kintu jñāna-virakty-ādi-sādhyaṃ bhaktyaiva sidhyati ।।
yat karmabhir yat tapasā jñāna-vairāgya taś ca yat । yogena dāna dharmeṇa śreyobhir itarair api ।। sarvaṃ mad-bhakti-yogena mad-bhakto labhate anjasā । svargāpavargaṃ mad-dhāma kathañcid yadi vāñchati ।।
rucim udvahatas tatra janasya bhajane hareḥ । viṣayeṣu gariṣṭho api rāgaḥ prāyo vilīyate ।। anāsaktasya viṣayān yathārham upayuñjataḥ । nirbandhaḥ kṛṣṇa-sambandhe yuktaṃ vairāgyam ucyate ।।
prāpañcikatayā buddhyā hari-sambandhi-vastunaḥ । mumukṣubhiḥ parityāgo vairāgyaṃ phalgu kathyate ।। proktena lakṣaṇenaiva bhaktir adhikṛtasya ca । aṅgatve suniraste api nityādy-akhila-karmaṇāṃ ।।
jnānasyādhyātmikasyāpi vairagyasya ca phalgunaḥ । spaṣṭatārthaṃ punar api tad evedaṃ nirākṛtaṃ ।। dhana-śiṣyādibhir dvārair yā bhaktir upapādyate । vidūratvād uttamatā-hānyā tasyāś ca nāṅgatā ।।
viśeṣaṇatvam evaiṣāṃ saṃśrayanty adhikāriṇām । vivekādīny ato amīṣām api nāṅgatvam ucyate ।। kṛṣṇonmukhaṃ svayaṃ yānti yamāḥ śaucādayas tathā । ity eṣāṃ ca na yuktā syād bhakty-aṅgāntara-pātitā ।।
ete na hy adbhutā vyādha tavāhiṃsādayo guṇāḥ । hari-bhaktau pravṛttā ye na te syuḥ para-tāpinaḥ ।। antaḥ-śuddhir bahiḥ-śuddhis tapaḥ-śānty-adayas tathā । amī guṇāḥ prapadyante hari-sevābhikāminām ।।
sā bhaktir eka-mukhyāṇgāśritānaikāṅgi kātha vā । svavāsanānusāreṇa niṣṭhātaḥ siddhi-kṛd bhavet ।। prahlādaḥ smaraṇe tad-aṅghri-bhajane lakṣmīḥ pṛthuḥ pūjane । sarvasvātma-nivedane balir abhūt kṛṣṇāptir eṣāṃ parā ।।
vacāṃsi vaikuṇṭha-guṇānuvarṇane । śrutiṃ cakārācyuta-sat-kathodaye ।। tad-bhṛtya-gātra-sparśe aṅga-saṅgamam । śrīmat-tulasyā rasanāṃ tad-arpite ।।
śiro hṛṣīkeśa-padābhivandane । yathottamaḥśloka-janāśraya ratiḥ ।। śāstroktayā prabalayā tat-tan-maryādayānvitā । vaidhi bhaktir iyaṃ kaiścan maryādā-mārga ucyate ।।
virājantīm abhivyaktāṃ vraja-vāsī janādiṣu । rāgātmikām anusṛtā yā sā rāgānugocyate ।। rāgānugā-vivekārtham ādau rāgātmikocyate ।। iṣṭe svārasikī rāgaḥ paramāviṣṭatā bhavet ।
tan-mayī yā bhaved bhaktiḥ sātra rāgātmikoditā ।। sā kāmarūpā sambandha-rūpā ceti bhaved dvidhā ।। kāmād dveṣād bhayāt snehād yathā bhaktyeśvare manaḥ । āveśya tad aghaṃ hitvā bahavas tad-gatiṃ gatāḥ ।।
gopyaḥ kāmād bhayāt kaṃso dveṣāc caidyādayo nṛpāḥ । sambandhād vṛṣṇayaḥ snehād yūyaṃ bhaktyā vayaṃ vibho ।। iti ।। ānukūlya-viparyāsād bhīti-dveṣau parāhatau ।
snehasya sakhya-vācitvād vaidha-bhakty-anuvartitā ।। kiṃ vā premābhidhāyitvān nopayogo atra sādhane । bhaktyā vayam iti vyaktaṃ vaidhī bhaktir udīritā ।। yad-arīṇāṃ priyāṇāṃ ca prāpyam ekam ivoditam ।
tad brahma-kṛṣṇayor aikyāt kiraṇārkopamā-juṣoḥ ।। brahmaṇy eva layaṃ yānti prāyeṇa ripavo hareḥ । kecit prāpyāpi sārūpyābhāsaṃ majjanti tat-sukhe ।। siddha-lokas tu tamasaḥ pāre yatra vasanti hi ।
siddhā brahma-sukhe magnā daityāś ca hariṇa hatāḥ ।। rāga-bandhena kenāpi taṃ bhajanto vrajanty amī । aṅghri-padma-sudhāḥ prema-rūpās tasya priyā janāḥ ।। munaya upāsate tad-arayo api yayuḥ smaraṇāt ।
vayam api te samāḥ sama-dṛśo aṅghri-saroja-sudhāḥ ।। sā kāmarūpā sambhoga-tṛṣṇāṃ yā nayati svatām । yad asyāṃ kṛṣṇa-saukhyārtham eva kevalam udyamaḥ ।। iyaṃ tu vraja-devīṣu suprasiddhā virājate ।
āsāṃ prema-viśeṣo ayaṃ prāptaḥ kām api mādhurīṃ । tat-tat-krīḍā-nidānatvāt kāma ity ucyate budhaiḥ ।। tathā ca tantre premaiva gopa-rāmāṇāṃ kāma ity agamat prathām ।। ity uddhavādayo apy etaṃ vāñchati bhagavat-priyāḥ ।।kāma-prāyā ratiḥ kintu kubjāyām eva sammatā ।।
sambandha-rūpā govinde pitṛtvādy-ābhimānitā । atropalakṣaṇatayā vṛṣṇīnāṃ vallavā matāḥ । yadaiśya-jñāna-śūnyatvād eṣāṃ rāge pradhānatā ।। kāma-sambandha-rūpe te prema-mātra-svarūpake ।
nitya-siddhāśrayatayā nātra samyag vicārite ।। rāgātmikāyā dvaividhyād dvidhā rāgānugā ca sā । kāmānugā ca sambandhānugā ceti nigadyate ।। rāgātmikaika-niṣṭhā ye vraja-vāsi-janādayaḥ ।
teṣāṃ bhāvāptaye lubdho bhaved atrādhikāravān ।। tat-tad-bhāvādi-mādhurye śrute dhīr yad apekṣate । nātra śāstraṃ na yuktiṃ ca tal-lobhotpatti-lakṣaṇam ।। vaidha-bhakty-adhikārī tu bhāvāvirbhavanāvadhi ।
atra śāstraṃ tathā tarkam anukūlam apekṣate ।। kṛṣṇaṃ smaran janaṃ cāsya preṣṭhaṃ nija-samīhitam । tat-tat-kathā-rataś cāsau kuryād vāsaṃ vraje sadā ।। sevā sādhaka-rūpeṇa siddha-rūpeṇa cātra hi ।
tad-bhāva-lipsunā kāryā vraja-lokānusārataḥ ।। śravaṇotkīrtanādīni vaidha-bhakty-uditāni tu । yāny aṅgāni ca tāny atra vijñeyāni manīṣibhiḥ ।। tatra kāmānugā kāmānugā bhavet tṛṣṇā kāma-rūpānugāminī ।।
sambhogecchā-mayī tat-tad-bhāvecchātmeti sā dvidhā ।। keli-tātparyavaty eva sambhogecchā-mayī bhavet । tad-bhāvecchātmikā tāsām bhāva-mādhurya-kāmitā ।। śrī-mūrter mādhurīṃ prekṣya tat-tal-līlāṃ niśamya vā ।
tad-bhāvākāṇkṣiṇo ye syus teṣu sādhanatānayoḥ । purāṇe śruyate pādme puṃsam api bhaved iyam ।। purā maharṣayaḥ sarve daṇḍakāraṇya-vāsinaḥ । dṛṣṭvā rāmaṃ hariṃ tatra bhoktum aicchan suvigraham ।।
te sarve strītvam āpannāḥ samudbhūtāś ca gokule । hariṃ samprāpya kāmena tato muktā bhavārṇavāt ।। riraṃsāṃ suṣṭhu kurvan yo vidhi-mārgeṇa sevate । kevalenaiva sa tadā mahiṣītvam iyāt pure ।।
agni-putrā mahātmānas tapasā strītvam āpire । bhartāraṃ ca jagad-yoniṃ vāsudevam ajaṃ vibhum ।। sā sambandhānugā bhaktiḥ procyate sadbhir ātmani । yā pitṛtvādi-sambandha-mananāropanātmikā ।।
lubdhair vātsalya-sakhyādau bhaktiḥ kāryātra sādhakaiḥ । vrajendra-subalādīnāṃ bhāva-ceṣṭita-mudrayā ।। tathā hi śruyate śāstre kaścit kurupurī-sthitaḥ । nanda-sūnor adhiṣṭhānaṃ tatra putratayā bhajan ।
nāradasyopadeśena siddho abhūd vṛddha-vardhakiḥ ।। pati-putra-suhṛd-bhrātṛ-pitṛvan maitravad dharim । ye dhyāyanti sadodyuktās tebhyo apīha namo namaḥ ।। kṛṣṇa-tad-bhakta-kāruṇya-mātra-lābhaika-hetukā ।
puṣṭi-mārgatayā kaiścid iyaṃ rāgānugocyate ।। iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhau purva-vibhāge sādhana-bhakti-laharī-dvitiyā ।। śuddha-sattva-viśeṣātmā prema-sūryāṃśu-sāmya-bhāk । rucibhiś citta-māsṛṇya-kṛd asau bhāva ucyate ।।
premṇas tu prathamāvasthā bhāva ity abhidhīyate । sāttvikāḥ svalpa-mātrāḥ syur atrāśru-pulakādayaḥ ।। dhyāyaṃ dhyāyaṃ bhagavataḥ pādāmbuja-yugaṃ tadā । īṣad-vikriyamāṇātmā sārdra-dṛṣtir abhūd asau ।।
āvirbhūya mano-vṛttau vrajanti tat-svarūpatāṃ । svayaṃ-prakāśa-rūpāpi bhāsamānā prākāśyavat ।। vastutaḥ svayam āsvāda-svarūpaiva ratis tv asau । kṛṣṇādi-karmakāsvāda-hetutvaṃ pratipadyate ।।
sādhanābhiniveśena kṛṣṇa-tad-bhaktayos tathā । prasādenātidhanyānāṃ bhāvo dvedhābhijāyate । ādyas tu prāyikas tatra dvitīyo viralodayaḥ ।। vaidhī-rāgānugā-mārga-bhedena parikīrtitaḥ ।
dvividhaḥ khalu bhāvo atra sādhanābhiniveśajaḥ ।। sādhanābhiniveśas tu tatra niṣpādayan rucim । harāv āsaktim utpādya ratiṃ saṃjanayaty asau ।। tatra ādyo tatrānvahaṃ kṛṣṇa-kathāḥ pragāyatām anugraheṇāśṛṇavaṃ manoharāḥ । tāḥ śraddhayā me anupadaṃ viśṛṇvataḥ priya-śravasy aṅga mamābhavad ratiḥ ।। iti ।
ratyā tu bhāva evātra na tu premābhidhīyate । mama bhaktiḥ pravṛtteti vakṣyate sa yad agrataḥ ।। viśṛṇvato me anusavaṃ yaśo amalam । bhaktiḥ pravṛttātma rajas-tamopahā ।।
bhavanti hṛt-karṇa-rasāyanāḥ kathāḥ । śraddhā ratir bhaktir anukramiṣyati ।। purāṇe nātya-śāstre ca dvayos tu rati-bhāvayoḥ । samānārthatayā hy atra dvayam aikyena lakṣitam ।।
itthaṃ manorathaṃ bālā kurvatī nṛtya utsukā । hari-prītyā ca tāṃ sarvāṃ rātrim evātyavāhayat ।। sādhanena vinā yas tu sahasaivābhijāyate । sa bhāvaḥ kṛṣṇa-tad-bhakta-prasādaja itīyate ।।
atha śrī-kṛṣṇa-prasādajaḥ prasādā vācikāloka-dāna-hārdādayo hareḥ ।। sarva-maṇgala-mūrdhanyā pūrṇānanda-mayī sadā । dvijendra tava mayy astu bhaktir avyābhicāriṇī ।। adṛṣṭa-pūrvam ālokya kṛṣṇaṃ jāṅgala-vāsinaḥ ।
viklidyad-antarātmano dṛṣṭiṃ nākraṣṭum īśire ।। hārdaḥ prasāda āntaro yaḥ syāt sa hārda iti kathyate ।। mahābhāgavato jātaḥ putras te bādarāyaṇa । vinopāyair upeyābhūd viṣṇu-bhaktir ihoditā ।।
guṇair alam asaṅkhyeyair mahātmyaṃ tasya sūcyate । vāsudeve bhagavati yasya naisargikī ratiḥ ।। nāradasya prasādena prahlāde śudha-vāsanā । nisargaḥ saiva tenātra ratir naisargikī matā ।।
aho dhanyo asi devarṣe kṛpayā yasya tat-kṣaṇāt । nīco apy utpulako lebhe lubdhako ratim acyute ।। bhaktānāṃ bhedataḥ seyaṃ ratiḥ pañca-vidhā matā । agre vivicya vaktavyā tena nātra prapañcyate ।।
kṣāntir avyartha-kālatvaṃ viraktir māna-śunyatā । āśā-bandhaḥ samutkaṇṭhā nāma-gāne sadā ruciḥ ।। āsaktis tad-guṇākhyāne prītis tad-vasati-sthale । ity ādayo anubhāvāḥ syur jāta-bhāvāṅkure jane ।।
tatra kṣāntiḥ kṣobha-hetāv api prāpte kṣāntir akṣubhitātmatā ।। gaṅgā ca devī dhṛta-cittam īśe । daśatv alaṃ gāyata viṣṇu-gāthāḥ ।। tanvā namanto apy aniśaṃ na tṛptāḥ ।
āyur harer eva samarpayanti ।। atha viraktiḥ viraktir indriyārthānāṃ syād arocakatā svayaṃ ।। yo dustyajān dāra-sutān suhṛd rājyaṃ hṛdi-spṛśaḥ । jahau yuvaiva malavad uttamaḥśloka-lālasaḥ ।।
atha māna-śūnyatā utkṛṣṭatve apy amānitvaṃ kathitā māna-śūnyatā ।। harau ratiṃ vahann eṣa narendrāṇāṃ śikhā-maṇiḥ । bhikṣām aṭann ari-pure śvapākam api vandate ।। atha āśā-bandhaḥ āśā-bandho bhagavataḥ prāpti-sambhāvanā dṛḍhā ।।
jñānaṃ vā śubha-karma vā kiyad aho saj-jātir apy asti vā । he gopī-jana-vallabha vyathayate hā hā mad-āśaiva mām ।। atha samutkaṇṭhā samutkaṇṭhā nijābhīṣṭa-lābhāya guru-lubdhatā ।। ālolām anurāgiṇor nayanayor ārdrāṃ mṛdau jalpite ।
āśāste mama locanaṃ vraja-śiśor-mūrtiṃ jagan-mohinīm ।। rodana-bindu-maranda-syandi-dṛg-indīvarādya govinda । tava madhura-svara-kaṇṭhī gāyati nāmāvalīṃ bālā ।। manmathatā tasya kim api kaiśoram ।
ceto bata harati hanta kiṃ kurmaḥ ।। bandha-ccheda-karo api dāmabhir abhūd baddho atra dāmodaraḥ । ānandāśru-dharaḥ kadā madhu-purīṃ dhanyaś cariṣyāmy aham ।। vyaktaṃ masṛṇitevāntar lakṣyate rati-lakṣaṇam ।
mumukṣu-prabhṛtīnāṃ ced bhaved eṣā ratir na hi ।। vimuktākhila-tarṣair yā muktir api vimṛgyate । yā kṛṣṇenātigopyāśu bhajadbhyo api na dīyate ।। sā bhukti-mukti-kāmatvāc chuddhāṃ bhaktim akurvatām ।
hṛdaye sambhavaty eṣāṃ kathaṃ bhāgavatī ratiḥ ।। kintu bāla-camatkāra-karī tac-cihna-vīkṣayā । abhijñena subodho ayaṃ raty-ābhāsaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। pratibimbas tathā cchāyā raty-ābhāso dvidhā mataḥ ।।
aśramābhīṣṭa-nirvāhī rati-lakṣaṇa-lakṣitaḥ । bhogāpavarga-saukhyāṃśa-vyañjakaḥ pratibimbakaḥ ।। daivāt sad-bhakta-saṅgena kīrtanādy-anusāriṇām । prāyaḥ prasanna-manasāṃ bhoga-mokṣādi rāgiṇām ।।
keṣāṃcit hṛdi bhāvendoḥ pratibimba udañcati । tad-bhakta-hṛn-nabhaḥ-sthasya tat-saṃsarga-prabhāvataḥ ।। kṣudra-kautūhala-mayī cañcalā duḥkha-hāriṇī । rateś chāyā bhavet kiṃcit tat-sādṛśyāvalambinī ।।
hari-priya-kriyā-kāla-deśa-pātrādi-saṅgamāt । apy ānuṣaṅgikād eṣa kvacid ajñeṣv apīkṣyate ।। kintu bhāgyaṃ vinā nāsau bhāva-cchāyāpy udañcati । yad abhyudayataḥ kṣemaṃ tatra syād uttarottaram ।।
hari-priya-janasyaiva prasāda-bhara-lābhataḥ । bhāvābhāso api sahasā bhāvatvam upagacchati ।। tasminn evāparādhena bhāvābhāso apy anuttamaḥ । krameṇa kṣayam āpnoti kha-sthaḥ pūrṇa-śaśī yathā ।।
bhāvo apy abhāvam āyāti kṛṣṇa-preṣṭhāparādhataḥ । ābhāsatāṃ ca śanakair nyūna-jātīyatām api ।। gāḍhāsaṅgāt sadāyāti mumukṣau supratiṣṭhite । ābhāsatām asau kiṃ vā bhajanīyeśa-bhāvatām ।।
ata eva kvacit teṣu navya-bhakteṣu dṛśyate । kṣaṇam īśvara-bhāvo ayaṃ nṛtyādau mukti-pakṣagaḥ ।। sādhanekṣāṃ vinā yasminn akasmād bhāva īkṣyate । vighna-sthagitam atrohyaṃ prāg-bhavīyaṃ susādhanaṃ ।।
lokottara-camatkāra-kārakaḥ sarva-śaktidaḥ । yaḥ prathīyān bhaved bhāvaḥ sa tu kṛṣṇa-prasādajaḥ ।। jane cej jāta-bhāve api vaiguṇyam iva dṛśyate । kāryā tathāpi nāsūyā kṛtārthaḥ sarvathaiva saḥ ।।
bhṛśam alino api virājate manuṣyaḥ । timira-parābhavatām upaiti candraḥ ।। ratir aniśa-nisargoṣṇa-prabalatarānanda-pūra-rūpaiva । uṣmāṇam api vamantī sudhāṃśu-koṭer api svādvī ।।
iti śrī-śrī bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhau purva-vibhāge bhāva-bhakti-laharī tṛtīyā ।। samyaṅ-masṛṇita-svānto mamatvātiśayāṅkitaḥ । bhāvaḥ sa eva sāndrātmā budhaiḥ premā nigadyate ।। ananya-mamatā viṣṇau mamatā prema-saṅgatā ।
bhaktir ity ucyate bhīṣma-prahlādoddhava-nāradaiḥ ।। bhaktiḥ premocyate bhīṣma-mukhyair yatra tu saṅgatā । mamatānya-mamatvena varjitety atra yojanā ।। bhāvottho ati-prasādotthaḥ śrī-harer iti sa dvidhā ।।
bhāva evāntar-aṅgāṇam-aṅgānām-anusevayā । ārūḍhaḥ parama-utkarṣam bhāva-uttaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।। jātānurāgo druta-citta uccaiḥ । unmādavan nṛtyati loka-bāhyaḥ ।।
na patiṃ kāmayet kañcid brahmacarya-sthitā sadā । tam-eva mūrtiṃ dhyāyantī candrakantir-varānanā ।। śrī-kṛṣṇa-gāthāṃ gāyantī romāṇcodbheda-lakṣaṇā । asmin-manvantare snigdhā śrī-kṛṣṇa-priya-vartayā ।।
atha harer atiprasādotthaḥ harer atiprasādo ayaṃ saṅga-dānādir ātmanaḥ ।। te nādhīta-śruti-gaṇā nopāsita-mahattamāḥ । avratātapta-tapasaḥ mat-saṅgān mām upāgatāḥ ।। māhātmya-jñāna-yuktaś ca kevalaś ceti sa dvidhā ।।
māhātmya-jñāna-yuktas tu sudṛḍhaḥ sarvato adhikaḥ । sneho bhaktir iti proktas tayā sārṣṭyādinānyathā ।। kevalo, yathā tatraiva manogatir avicchinnā harau prema-pariplutā । abhisandhi-vinirmuktā bhaktir-viṣṇu-vaśaṅkarī ।। iti । mahima-jñāna-yuktaḥ syād vidhi-mārgānusāriṇām ।
rāgānugāśritānāṃ tu prāyaśaḥ kevalo bhavet ।। ādau śraddhā tataḥ sādhu-saṅgo atha bhajana-kriyā । tato anartha-nivṛttiḥ syāt tato niṣṭhā rucis tataḥ ।। athāsaktis tato bhāvas tataḥ premābhyudañcati ।
sādhakānām ayaṃ premnaḥ prādurbhāve bhavet kramaḥ ।। dhanyasyāyaṃ navaḥ premā yasyonmīlati cetasi । antarvāṇībhir apy asya mudrā suṣṭhu sudurgamā ।। bhāvonmatto hareḥ kiñcin na veda sukham ātmanaḥ ।
dukhaṃ ceti maheśāni paramānanda āplutaḥ ।। premṇa eva vilāsatvād vairalyāt sādhakeṣv api । atra snehādayo bhedā vivicya na hi śaṃsitāḥ ।। śrīmat-prabhupadāmbhojaiḥ sarvā bhāgavatāmṛte ।
vyaktīkṛtāsti gūḍhāpi bhakti-siddhānta-mādhurī ।। gopāla-rūpa-śobhāṃ dadhad api raghunātha-bhāva-vistārī । tuṣyatu sanātanātmā prathama-vibhāge sudhāmbu-nidheḥ ।। prabalam ananya-śrayiṇā niṣevitaḥ sahaja-rūpeṇa ।
agha-damano mathurāyāṃ sadā sanātana-tanur jayati ।। rasāmṛtābdher bhāge asmin dvitīye dakṣiṇābhidhe । sāmānya-bhagavad-bhakti-rasas tāvad udīryate ।। asya pañca laharyaḥ syur vibhāvākhyāgrimā matā ।
dvitīyā tv anubhāvākhyā tṛtīyā sāttvikābhidhā । vyabhicāry-abhidhā turyā sthāyi-saṃjñā ca pañcamī ।। athāsyāḥ keśava-rater lakṣitāyā nigadyate । sāmagrī-paripoṣena paramā rasa-rūpatā ।।
vibhāvair anubhāvaiś ca sāttvikair vyabhicāribhiḥ । svādyatvaṃ hṛdi bhaktānām ānītā śravaṇādibhiḥ । eṣā kṛṣṇa-ratiḥ sthāyī bhāvo bhakti-raso bhavet ।। prāktany ādhunikī cāsti yasya sad-bhakti-vāsanā ।
eṣa bhakti-rasāsvādas tasyaiva hṛdi jāyate ।। bhakti-nirdhūta-doṣāṇāṃ prasannojjvala-cetasām । śrī-bhāgavata-raktānāṃ rasikāsaṅga-raṅgiṇām ।। jīvanī-bhūta-govinda-pāda-bhakti-sukha-śriyām ।
premāntaraṅga-bhūtāni kṛtyāny evānutiṣṭhatām ।। bhaktānāṃ hṛdi rājantī saṃskāra-yugalojjvalā । ratir ānanda-rūpaiva nīyamānā tu rasyatām ।। kṛṣṇādibhir vibhāvādyair gatair anubhavādhvani ।
prauḍhānanda-camatkāra-kāṣṭhām āpadyate parām ।। kintu premā vibhāvādyaiḥ svalpair nīto apy aṇīyasīm । vibhāvanādy-avasthāṃ tu sadya āsvādyatāṃ vrajet ।। ye kṛṣṇa-bhakta-muralī-nādādyā hetavo rateḥ ।
kārya-bhūtāḥ smitādyāś ca tathāṣṭau stabdhatādayaḥ ।। nirvedādyāḥ sahāyāś ca te jñeyā rasa-bhāvane । vibhāvā anubhāvāś ca sāttvikā vyabhicāriṇaḥ ।। tatra jñeyā vibhāvās tu raty-āsvādana-hetavaḥ ।
te dvidhālambanā eke tathaivoddīpanāḥ pare ।। vibhāvyate hi raty-ādir yatra yena vibhāvyate । vibhāvo nāma sa dvedhālambanoddīpanātmakaḥ ।। kṛṣṇaś ca kṛṣṇa-bhaktāś ca budhair ālambanā matāḥ ।
raty-āder viṣayatvena tathādhāratayāpi ca ।। nāyakānāṃ śiro-ratnaṃ kṛṣṇas tu bhagavān svayam । yatra nityatayā sarve virājante mahā-guṇāḥ । so anyarūpa-svarūpābhyām asminn ālambano mataḥ ।।
hanta me katham udeti sa-vatse, vatsa-pāla-paṭale ratir atra । ity aniścita-matir baladevo, vismaya-stimita-mūrtir ivāsīt ।। atha svarūpam āvṛtaṃ prakaṭaṃ ceti svarūpaṃ kathitaṃ dvidhā ।। tatra āvṛtam anya-veśādinācchannaṃ svarūpaṃ proktam āvṛtam ।।
māṃ snehayati kim uccair, mahileyaṃ dvārakāvarodhe atra । āṃ viditaṃ kutukārthī, vanitā-veśo hariś carati ।। tamāla-śyāmāṅga-dyutir atitarāṃ chatrita-śirāḥ । karoty uccair modaṃ mama madhura-mūrtir madhuripuḥ ।।
ayaṃ netā suramyāṅgaḥ sarva-sal-lakṣaṇānvitaḥ । ruciras tejasā yukto balīyān vayasānvitaḥ ।। vividhādbhuta-bhāṣā-vit satya-vākyaḥ priyaṃ vadaḥ । vāvadūkaḥ supāṇḍityo buddhimān pratibhānvitaḥ ।।
vidagdhaś caturo dakṣaḥ kṛtajñaḥ sudṛḍha-vrataḥ । deśa-kāla-supātrajñaḥ śāstra-cakṣuḥ śucir vaśī ।। sthiro dāntaḥ kṣamā-śīlo gambhīro dhṛtimān samaḥ । vadānyo dhārmikaḥ śūraḥ karuṇo mānya-mānakṛt ।।
dakṣiṇo vinayī hrīmān śaraṇāgata-pālakaḥ । sukhī bhakta-suhṛt prema-vaśyaḥ sarva-śubhaṅkaraḥ ।। pratāpī kīrtimān rakta-lokaḥ sādhu-samāśrayaḥ । nārī-gaṇa-manohārī sarvārādhyaḥ samṛddhimān ।।
varīyān īśvaraś ceti guṇās tasyānukīrtitāḥ । samudrā iva pañcāśad durvigāhā harer amī ।। jīveṣu ete vasanto api bindu-bindutayā kvacit । paripūrṇatayā bhānti tatraiva puruṣottame ।।
tathā hi pādme pārvatyai śiti-kaṇṭhena tad-guṇāḥ । kandarpa-koṭi-lāvaṇya ity ādyāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।। eta eva guṇāḥ prāyo dharmāya vana-mālinaḥ । pṛthivyā prathama-skandhe prathayāñcakrire sphuṭam ।।
satyaṃ śaucaṃ dayā kṣāntis tyāgaḥ santoṣa ārjavam । śamo damas tapaḥ sāmyaṃ titikṣoparatiḥ śrutam ।। jñānaṃ viraktir aiśvaryaṃ śauryaṃ tejo balaṃ smṛtiḥ । svātantryaṃ kauśalaṃ kāntir dhairyaṃ mārdavam eva ca ।।
prāgalbhyaṃ praśrayaḥ śīlaṃ saha ojo balaṃ bhagaḥ । gāmbhīryaṃ sthairyam āstikyaṃ kīrtir māno anahaṅkṛtiḥ ।। ime cānye ca bhagavan nityā yatra mahā-guṇāḥ । prārthyā mahattvam icchadbhir na viyanti sma karhicit ।।
atha pañca-guṇā ye syur aṃśena giriśādiṣu ।। sadā svarūpa-samprāptaḥ sarva-jño nitya-nūtanaḥ । sac-cid-ānanda-sāndrāṅgaḥ sarva-siddhi-niṣevitaḥ ।। athocyante guṇāḥ pañca ye lakṣmīśādi-vartinaḥ ।
avicintya-mahā-śaktiḥ koṭi-brahmāṇḍa-vigrahaḥ ।। avatārāvalī-bījaṃ hatāri-gati-dāyakaḥ । ātmārāma-gaṇākarṣīty amī kṛṣṇe kilādbhutāḥ ।। sarvādbhuta-camatkāra- līlā-kallola-vāridhiḥ ।
atulya-madhura-prema-maṇḍita-priya-maṇḍalaḥ ।। trijagan-mānasākarṣi-muralī-kala-kūjitaḥ । asamānordhva-rūpa-śrī-vismāpita-carācaraḥ ।। līlā-premṇā priyādhikyaṃ mādhuryaṃ veṇu-rūpayoḥ ।
ity asādhāraṇaṃ proktaṃ govindasya catuṣṭayam ।। evaṃ guṇāś catur-bhedāś catuḥ-ṣaṣṭir udāhṛtāḥ । sodāharaṇam eteṣāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ kriyate kramāt ।। tatra suramyāṅgaḥ ślāghyāṅga-sanniveśo yaḥ suramyāṅgaḥ sa kathyate ।।
bhujau stambhārambhau sarasija-vareṇyaṃ kara-yugam । parikṣāmo madhyaḥ sphurati murahantur madhurimā ।। sarva-sal-lakṣaṇānvitaḥ tanau guṇottham aṅkottham iti sal-lakṣaṇaṃ dvidhā ।। tatra guṇottham guṇotthaṃ syād guṇair yogo raktatā-tuṅgatādibhiḥ ।।
visāras triṣu kharvatā triṣu tathā gambhīratā ca triṣu । dvātriṃśad-vara-lakṣaṇaḥ katham asau gopeṣu sambhāvyate ।। aṅkottham rekhāmayaṃ rathāṅgādi syād aṅkotthaṃ karādiṣu ।। sphuṭa-rekhāmayam ātmajasya paśya ।
dhvaja-vajrāṅkuśa-mīna-paṅkajāni ।। ruciraḥ saundaryeṇa dṛg-ānanda-kārī rucira ucyate ।। nirīkṣya dṛk-svastyayanaṃ tri-lokaḥ । arvāk-sṛtau kauśalam ity amanyata ।।
ekasmin katham api yatra ballavīnām । notthātuṃ dyuti-madhu-paṅkilāt kṣamāsīt ।। tejasā yuktaḥ tejo dhāma prabhāvaś cety ucyate dvividhaṃ budhaiḥ ।। tatra dhāma dīpti-rāśir bhaved dhāma ।।
ambara-maṇi-nikurambaṃ viḍambayann api marīci-kulaiḥ । hari-vakṣasi ruci-niviḍe maṇirāḍ ayam uḍur iva sphurati ।। prabhāvaḥ prabhāvaḥ sarvajit-sthitiḥ ।। komalāṅgam api raṅga-maṇḍale ।
kaṃsa-malla-nivahaḥ sa vivyathe ।। balīyān prāṇena mahatā pūrṇo balīyān iti kathyate ।। daitya-puṅgavam udagram ariṣṭam । puṇḍarīka-nayano vinunoda ।।
vāmas tāmarasākṣasya bhuja-daṇḍaḥ sa pātu vaḥ । krīḍā-kandukatāṃ yena nīto govardhano giriḥ ।। vayaso vividhatve api sarva-bhakti-rasāśrayaḥ । dharmī kiśora evātra nitya-nānā-vilāsavān ।।
smita-śrī-nirdhūta-sphurad-amala-rākā-pati-madam । murārer mādhuryaṃ manasi madirākṣīr madayati ।। vividhādbhuta-bhāṣāvit sa prokto yas tu kovidaḥ । nānā-deśyāsu bhāṣāsu saṃskṛte prākṛteṣu ca ।।
praṇata-śirasi saurīṃ bhāratīm ātanoti । katham ajani vidagdhaḥ sarva-bhāṣāvalīṣu ।। satya-vākyaḥ syān nānṛtaṃ vaco yasya satya-vākyaḥ sa kathyate ।। raṇorvaritam ity abhūt tava yathārtham evoditam ।
tathāpi na murāntaka vyabhicariṣṇur uktis tava ।। harir yathārthaṃ magadhendram ūce । māṃ viddhi kṛṣṇaṃ bhavataḥ sapatnam ।। priyaṃvadaḥ jane kṛtāparādhe api sāntva-vādī priyaṃvadaḥ ।।
tvayā vidheyā mayi doṣa-dṛṣṭiḥ । paraṃ hitāyādya gavāṃ kulasya ।। śruti-preṣṭhoktir akhila-vāg-guṇānvita-vāg api । iti dvidhā nigadito vāvadūko manīṣibhiḥ ।।
praty-akṣara-kṣarad-amanda-sudhā-rasena । nāhāri kasya hṛdayaṃ hari-bhāṣitena ।। jagad-eka-saṃśaya-vimarda-karī । hari-vāg iyaṃ mama dhinoti dhiyaḥ ।।
vidvān nītijña ity eṣa supaṇḍityo dvidhā mataḥ । vidvān akhila-vidyā-vin nītijñas tu yathārha-kṛt ।। pitāmahādy-ambudharaiḥ pravartitāḥ । tam eva vidyā-saritaḥ prapedire ।।
nyāyenānugatā purāṇa-suhṛdā mīmāṃsayā maṇḍitā । vidyā nāma vadhūś caturdaśa-guṇā govinda śuśrūyate ।। kandarpo ramaṇīṣu durgata-kule kalyāṇa-kalpa-drumaḥ । śāsti svasti-dhurandharo madhupurīṃ nītyā madhūnāṃ patiḥ ।।
buddhimān medhāvī sūkṣmadhīś ceti procyate buddhimān dvidhā ।। guror jagati darśayan samayam atra vidyārthinām । dadhau hṛdaya-mandire kim api citravan mādhavaḥ ।। tarala-tamasi tasmin vidravann eva neṣye ।
jhara-muci mucukundaḥ kandare yatra śete ।। pratibhānvitaḥ sadyo navanavollekhi-jñānaṃ syāt pratibhānvitaḥ ।। vāsaṃ brūhi śaṭha prakāma-subhage tvad-gātra-saṃsargataḥ । śaurir gopa-vadhūṃ chalaiḥ parihasann evaṃ-vidhaiḥ pātu vaḥ ।।
vidagdhaḥ kalā-vilāsa-digdhātmā vidagdha iti kīrtyate ।। veṇuṃ vādayate srajaṃ viracayaty ālekhyam abhyasyati । paśyoddāma-kalā-vilāsa-vasatiś citraṃ hariḥ krīḍati ।। caturaḥ caturo yugapad-bhūri-samādhāna-kṛd ucyate ।।
gopāṅganā-gaṇam apāṅga-taraṅgitena । dhinvann ariṣṭa-bhayadena harir vireje ।। dakṣaḥ duṣkare kṣipra-kārī yas taṃ dakṣaṃ paricakṣate ।। yāni yodhaiḥ prayuktāni śastrāstrāṇi kurūdvaha ।
haris tāny acchinat tīkṣṇaiḥ śarair ekaika-śastribhiḥ ।। tvam iti nikhila-gopī-prārthanā-pūrti-kāmaḥ । dadṛśur adhikam etās taṃ yathā sva-sva-pārśve ।। kṛtajñaḥ kṛtajñaḥ syād abhijño yaḥ kṛta-sevādi-karmaṇām ।।
ṛṇam etat pravṛddhaṃ me hṛdayān nāpasarpati । yad govindeti cukrośa kṛṣṇā māṃ dūra-vāsinam ।। akuruta bahumānaṃ śaurir ādāya kanyām । kim uta sa khalu sādhu-śreṇi-cūḍāgra-ratnam ।।
sudṛḍha-vrataḥ pratijñā-niyamau yasya satyau sa sudṛḍha-vrataḥ ।। na cāsurā naiva ca yakṣa-pannagāḥ । mune samarthāḥ khalu satyam astu te ।। vidhāya kaṃsārir apārijātau ।
satyāṃ ca kṛṣṇāṃ ca sukhām akārṣīt ।। girer uddharaṇaṃ kṛṣṇa duṣkaraṃ karma kurvatā । mad-bhaktaḥ syān na duḥkhīti sva-vrataṃ vivṛtaṃ tvayā ।। deśa-kāla-supātrajñaḥ deśa-kāla-supātrajñas tat-tad-yogya-kriyā-kṛtiḥ ।।
trilokyām ākṛīḍaḥ kvacid api na vṛndāvana-samaḥ । mano me sotkaṇṭhaṃ muhur ajani rāsotsava-rase ।। śāstra-cakṣuḥ śāstrānusāri-karmā yaḥ śāstra-cakṣuḥ sa kathyate ।। śāstram evārtha-dṛṣṭaye ।
vṛndān mādāya kevalam ।। pāvanaś ca viśuddheś cety ucyate dvividhaḥ śuciḥ । pāvanaḥ pāpa-nāśī syād viśuddhas tyakta-dūsaṇaḥ ।। śraddhā-rajyan-matir atitarām uttamaḥ-śloka-maulim ।
ābhāso api kṣapayati mahā-pātaka-dhvānta-rāśim ।। bata satrājiti nāpy adīnatā । prasabhaṃ kaustubha-sakhyam icchasi ।। vaśī vaśī jitendriyaḥ proktaḥ ।।
vrīḍāvaloka-nihato madano api yāsām । yasyendriyaṃ vimathituṃ kuhakair na śekuḥ ।। sthiraḥ āphalodayakṛt sthiraḥ ।। nācintayad vyasanam ṛkṣa-vilapraveśe ।
syād udyamaḥ kṛta-dhiyāṃ hi phalodayāntaḥ ।। dāntaḥ sa dānto duḥsaham api yogyaṃ kleśaṃ saheta yaḥ ।। harir aja-gaṇa-dantaḥ komalāṅgo api nāyam । kim api manasi citraṃ cintyamānā tanoti ।।
kṣamāśīlaḥ kṣamāśīlo aparādhānāṃ sahanaḥ parikīrtyate ।। śapamānāya na cedi-bhūbhṛte । na hi gomāyu-rutāni keśarī ।। praṇata iti dayālur yac ca caidyasya kṛṣṇa ।
vada kim apadam āgas tasya te asti kṣamāyāḥ ।। gambhīraḥ durvibodhāśayo yas tu sa gambhīraḥ itīryate ।। vṛndāvane varātiḥ stutibhir nitarām upāsyamāno api । śakto na harir vidhinā ruṣṭas tuṣṭo athavā jñātum ।।
unmado api harir navya-rādhā-praṇaya-sīdhunā । abhijñenāpi rāmeṇa lakṣito ayam avikriyaḥ ।। dhṛtimān pūrṇa-spṛhaś ca dhṛtimān śāntaś ca kṣobha-kāraṇe ।। kaṃsārir magadha-pater vadha-prasiddhām ।
kiṃ lokottara-guṇa-śālinām apekṣyam ।। sambhrameṇa munibhiḥ stutasya ca । kāpi nāsya vikṛtir vitarkitā ।। samaḥ rāga-dveṣa-vimukto yaḥ samaḥ sa kathito budhaiḥ ।।
tavāvatāraḥ khala-nigrahāya । dhatse damaṃ phalam evānuśaṃsan ।। yaduvara yadi duṣṭo daṇḍanīyaḥ suto api । kvacid api viṣamaṃ te ceṣṭitaṃ jāghaṭīti ।।
vadānyaḥ dāna-vīro bhaved yas tu sa vadānyo nigadyate ।। vyarthīkṛtāḥ kaṃsa-nisūdanena । kalpa-drumā dvāravatīṃ bhajanti ।। cāṣṭāśliṣṭa-śataṃ vibhāti paritas tat-saṅkhya-patnī-yujām ।
gṛṣṭīnāṃ yugapac ca baddham adadād yas tasya vā kaḥ samaḥ ।। dhārmikaḥ kurvan kārayate dharmaṃ yaḥ sa dhārmika ucyate ।। guptasya gopendra tathābhyavardhi । adharma-sparśāṇi haṭhāj jaghāsa ।।
ākṛṣyamāṇeṣu patiṣv anāratam । tavāvatāraṃ navamaṃ namasyati ।। śūraḥ utsāhī yudhi śūro astra-prayoge ca vicakṣaṇaḥ ।। dviṣad-aravinda-vane vihāra-caryām ।
tvam agha-vidāraṇa vāraṇendra-līlaḥ ।। kṣaṇād akṣauhiṇī-vṛnde jarāsandhasya dāruṇe । dṛṣṭaḥ ko apy atra nādaṣṭo hareḥ praharaṇāhibhiḥ ।। karuṇaḥ para-duḥkhāsaho yas tu karuṇaḥ sa nigadyate ।।
duḥkhāndhakāra-paṭalaiḥ svayam andhitānām । vṛnde tam adya yadunandana-padma-bandhum ।। tvarā-bhara-taraṅgataḥ kavalitātma-visphūrtaye । sapadya-vaśa-vartmaṇo bhagavataḥ kṛpāyai namaḥ ।।
mānyamānakṛt guru-brāhmaṇa-vṛddhādi-pūjako mānyamāna-kṛt ।। pitaraṃ pūrvajam apy athānataḥ । yadu-vṛddhānana-mat-kramādayam ।। dakṣiṇaḥ sauśīlya-saumya-carito dakṣiṇaḥ kīrtyate budhaiḥ ।।
sevāṃ manāg api kṛtāṃ bahudhābhyupaiti । śīlena nirmala-matiḥ puruṣottamo ayam ।। vinayī auddhatya-parihārī yaḥ kathyate vinayīty asau ।। rabhasād rathād avatarītum icchataḥ ।
vinayaṃ viśeṣayati sambhrameṇa saḥ ।। jñāte asmara-rahasye anyaiḥ kriyamāṇe stave athavā । śālīnatvena saṅkocaṃ bhajan hrīmān udīryate ।। karotkampād īṣac calati kila govardhana-girau ।
puro dṛṣṭvā rāmaṃ jayati namitāsyo madhuripuḥ ।। śaraṇāgata-pālakaḥ pālayan śaraṇāpannān śaraṇāgata-pālakaḥ ।। jvara parihara vitrāsaṃ tvam atra samare kṛtāparādhe api । sadyaḥ prapadyamāne yad indavati yādavendro ayam ।।
sukhī bhoktā ca duḥkha-gandhair apy aspṛṣṭaś ca sukhī bhavet ।। svapne dambholi-pāṇer api duradhigamaṃ dvāri tauryatrikaṃ ca । sīmantinyaś ca nityaṃ yaduvara bhuvane kas tvad-anyo asti bhogī ।। na ghoraṃ nodghūrṇāṃ na kila kadanaṃ vetti kim api ।
harir vṛndāraṇye param aniśam uccair viharati ।। bhakta-suhṛt susevyo dāsa-bandhuś ca dvidhā bhakta-suhṛn mataḥ ।। tulasī-dala-mātreṇa jalasya culukena ca । vikrīṇīte svam ātmānaṃ bhaktebhyo bhakta-vatsalaḥ ।।
ṛtam adhikartum avapluto rathasthaḥ । harir iva hantum ibhaṃ gatottarīyaḥ ।। prema-vaśyaḥ priyatva-mātra-vaśyo yaḥ prema-vaśyo bhaved asau ।। sakhyuḥ priyasya viprarṣer aṅga-saṅgāti-nirvṛtaḥ ।
prīto vyamuñcad adhvindūn netrābhyāṃ puṣkarekṣaṇaḥ ।। sva-mātuḥ svinna-gātrāyā visrasta-kavara-srajaḥ । dṛṣṭvā pariśramaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ kṛpayāsīt sva-bandhane ।। sarva-śubhaṅkaraḥ sarveṣāṃ hita-kārī yaḥ sa syāt sarva-śubhaṅkaraḥ ।।
khala-kṣayeṇākhila-dhārmikāś ca । na kasya pathyaṃ hariṇā vyadhāyi ।। pratāpī pratāpī pauruṣodbhūta-śatru-tāpi prasiddhi-bhāk ।। bhuvanaṃ kṛṣṇa pratāpayati ।
śaraṇam abhūt kandarā-timiram ।। kīrtimān sādguṇyair nirmalaiḥ khyātaḥ kīrtimān iti kīrtyate ।। śubhra-bhāvam abhito nayanty api । kṛṣṇa-bhāva-kalilaṃ jagat-trayam ।।
śubhraṃ dṛṣṭvā kṣipati vasanaṃ vismito nīla-vāsāḥ । gīte dāmodara-yaśasi te vīṇayā nāradena ।। rakta-lokaḥ pātraṃ lokānurāgāṇāṃ rakta-lokaṃ vidur budhāḥ ।। raviṃ vinākṣṇor iva nas tavācyuta ।।
deva-śreṇī-stuti-kala-kalo meduraḥ prādurasti । ke vā raṅga-sthala-bhuvi harau bhejire nānurāgam ।। sādhu-samāśrayaḥ sad-eka-pakṣapātī yaḥ sa syāt sādhu-samāśrayaḥ ।। bhuvane asmin na bhavān bhuvaḥ śivāya ।
sujanānāṃ bata kā daśābhaviṣyat ।। nārī-gaṇa-mano-hārī nārī-gaṇa-mano-hārī sundarī-vṛnda-mohanaḥ ।। śruta-mātro api yaḥ strīṇāṃ prasahyākarṣate manaḥ । urugāyorugīto vā paśyantīnāṃ ca kiṃ punaḥ ।।
tvaṃ cumbako asi mādhava loha-mayī nūnam aṅganā-jātiḥ । dhāvati tatas tato asau yato yataḥ krīḍayā bhramasi ।। sarvārādhyaḥ sarveṣām agra-pūjyo yaḥ sa sarvārādhya ucyate ।। sadasi yudhiṣṭhira-rājasūya eṣām ।
mama dṛśi-gocara eṣa āvir ātmā ।। samṛddhimān mahā-sampatti-yukto yo bhaved eṣa samṛddhimān ।। varṣanty aṣṭau kim api nidhayaś cārtha-jātaṃ tavāmī । lakṣmīṃ paśyan mura-damana te nātra citrāyate kaḥ ।।
śṛṅgāra-puṣpa-taravas taravaḥ surāṇām । vṛndāni ceti sukha-sindhur aho vibhūtiḥ ।। varīyān sarveṣām ati-mukhyo yaḥ sa varīyān itīryate ।। tuṣṇīṃ tiṣṭha surendra cāṭubhir alaṃ vārīśa dūrībhava ।
hanta dvāravatī-pater avasaro nādyāpi niṣpadyate ।। īśvaraḥ dvidheśvaraḥ svatantraś ca durlaṅghyājñaś ca kīrtyate ।। pādāṅkam eva kila kāliya-pannagāya । sthāne svatantra-carito nigamair nuto ayam ।।
svārājya-lakṣmy-āpta-samasta-kāmaḥ । kirīṭa-koṭy-eḍita-pāda-pīṭhaḥ ।। rudraughaḥ kāla-jīrṇe kṣayam avatanute yaḥ kṣayāyānuśiṣṭaḥ । kaṃsāre santi sarve diśi diśi bhavataḥ śāsane ajāṇḍanāthāḥ ।।
atha sadā-svarūpa-samprāptaḥ sadā-svarūpa-samprāpto māyā-kārya-vaśīkṛtaḥ ।। etad īśanam īśasya prakṛti-stho api tad-guṇaiḥ । na yujyate sadātma-sthair yathā buddhis tad-āśrayā ।। para-citta-sthitaṃ deśa-kālādy-antaritaṃ tathā ।
yo jānāti samastārthaḥ sa sarvajño nigadyate ।। durvāsaso ari-racitād ayutāgra-bhug yaḥ । tṛptām amaṃsta salile vinimagna-saṅghaḥ ।। sadānubhūyamāno api karoty ananubhūtavat ।
vismayaṃ mādhurībhir yaḥ sa prokto nitya-nūtanaḥ ।। tathāpi tasyāṅghri-yugaṃ navaṃ navam । calāpi yac chrīr na jahāti karhicit ।। sumukhi niśita-dīrghāpāṅga-ṭaṅka-cchaṭābhiḥ ।
marakata-maṇi-lakṣair goṣṭha-kakṣāṃ cinoti ।। sac-cid-ānanda-sāndrāṅgaḥ sac-cid-ānanda-sāndrāṅgaś cidānanda-ghanākṛtiḥ ।। yad-brahma-saukhyaṃ svayam asphurat param । śyāmo ayam āmoda-bharaḥ prakāśate ।।
koṭiṣv aśeṣa-vasudhādi vibhūti-bhinnam । govindam ādi-puruṣaṃ tam ahaṃ bhajāmi ।। ataḥ śrī-vaiṣṇavaiḥ sarva-śruti-smṛti-nidarśanaiḥ । tad brahma śrī-bhagavato vibhūtir iti kīrtyate ।।
daśottarāṇy āvaraṇāni yāni ca । parātparaṃ brahma ca te vibhūtayaḥ ।। sarva-siddhi-niṣevitaḥ sva-vaśākhila-siddhiḥ syāt sarva-siddhi-niṣevitaḥ ।। daśabhiḥ siddha-sakhībhir vṛtā mahā-siddhayaḥ kramād aṣṭau ।
aṇimādayo labhante nāvasaraṃ dvāri kṛṣṇasya ।। divya-sargādi-kartṛtvaṃ brahma-rudrādi-mohanam । bhakta-prārabdha-vidhvaṃsa ity ādy acintya-śaktitā ।। aṃśenāṃśena cakre tad anu bahu-catur-bāhutāṃ teṣu tene ।
tāvad brahmāṇḍa-sevyaḥ sphuṭam ajani tato yaḥ prapadye tam īśam ।। hanta śambhur api jṛmbhito raṇe । ke mahendra vibudhā bhavad-vidhāḥ ।। guru-putram ihānītaṃ nija-karma-nibandhanam ।
ānayasva mahārāja mac-chāsana-puraskṛtaḥ ।। vibhur api bhuja-yugmotsaṅga-paryāpta-mūrtiḥ । dhiyam ayam avicintyānanta-śaktir dhinoti ।। agaṇya-jagad-aṇḍāḍhyaḥ koṭi-brahmāṇḍa-vigrahaḥ ।
iti śrī-vigrahasyāsya vibhutvam anukīrtitam ।। saṃveṣṭitāṇḍa-ghaṭa-sapta-vitasti-kāyaḥ । vātādhva-roma-vivarasya ca te mahitvam ।। pañcāśat-koṭy-akharva-kṣiti-khacitam idaṃ yac ca pātāla-pūrṇam ।
dṛṣṭaṃ yasyātra vṛndāvanam api bhavataḥ kaḥ stutau tasya śaktaḥ ।। avatārāvalī-bījam avatārāvalī-bījam avatārī nigadyate ।। daityaṃ dārayate baliṃ chalayate kṣatra-kṣayaṃ kurvate । mlecchān mūrcchayate daśākṛti-kṛte kṛṣṇāya tubhyaṃ namaḥ ।।
hatāri-gati-dāyakaḥ mukti-dātā hatārīṇāṃ hatāri-gati-dāyakaḥ ।। bandhaṃ ca bhītiṃ ca mṛtiṃ ca kṛtvā । tvaṃ śātravāṇām apavargado asi ।। tvayā samantād anubaddha-yuddhaḥ ।
mitrasya kurvann amṛtaṃ prayāti ।। ātmārāma-gaṇākarṣī ātmārāma-gaṇākarṣīty etad vyaktārtham eva hi ।। pūrṇa-paramahaṃsaṃ māṃ mādhava līlā-mahauṣadhir ghrātā । kṛtvā bata sāraṅgaṃ vyadhita kathaṃ sārase tṛṣitam ।।
santi yadyapi me prājyā līlās tās tā manoharāḥ । na hi jāne smṛte rāse mano me kīdṛśaṃ bhavet ।। tathā bhuvana-nandinas tad-avatāra-vṛndasya ca । bibharti hṛdi vismayaṃ kam api rāsa-līlā-rasaḥ ।।
truṭir yugāyate tvām apaśyatām । jaḍa udīkṣitāṃ pakṣma-kṛt dṛśām ।। sā kṣaṇārdhavad agāt tava saṅge । brahma-rātri-tativad virahe abhūt ।।
śakra-śarva-parameṣṭhi-purogāḥ । kaśmalaṃ yayur aniścita-tattvāḥ ।। dhyānād antarayan sanandana-mukhān vismerayan vedhasam । bhindann aṇḍa-kaṭāha-bhittim abhito babhrāma vaṃśī-dhvaniḥ ।।
māyā-balaṃ darśayatā gṛhītam । paraṃ padaṃ bhūṣaṇa-bhūṣaṇāṅgam ।। saṃmohitā'ryapadavīṃ na calet trilokyām । yad go-dvija-druma-mṛgān pulakāny abibhrat ।।
sphurati mama garīyān eṣa mādhurya-pūraḥ । sarabhasam upabhoktuṃ kāmaye rādhikeva ।। samasta-vividhāścarya-kalyāṇa-guṇa-vāridheḥ । guṇānām iha kṛṣṇasya diṅ-mātram upadarśitam ।।
hitāvatīrṇasya ka īśire asya । bhū-pāṃśavaḥ khe mihikā dyubhāsaḥ ।। nitya-guṇo vanamālī, yad api śikhāmaṇir aśeṣa-netṝṇām । bhaktāpekṣikam asya, trividhatvaṃ likhyate tad api ।।
hariḥ pūrṇatamaḥ pūrṇataraḥ pūrṇa iti tridhā । śreṣṭha-madhyādibhiḥ śabdair nāṭye yaḥ paripaṭhyate ।। prakāśitākhila-guṇaḥ smṛtaḥ pūrṇatamo budhaiḥ । asarva-vyañjakaḥ pūrṇataraḥ pūrṇo alpa-darśakaḥ ।।
kṛṣṇasya pūrṇatamatā vyaktābhūd gokulāntare । pūrṇatā pūrṇataratā dvārakā-mathurādiṣu ।। sa punaś caturvidhaḥ syād dhīrodāttaś ca dhīra-lalitaś ca । dhīra-praśānta-nāmā tathaiva dhīroddhataḥ kathitaḥ ।।
bahuvidha-guṇa-kriyāṇām āspada-bhūtasya padmanābhasya । tat-tal-līlā-bhedād virudhyate na hi catur-vidhāḥ ।। gambhīro vinayī kṣantā karuṇaḥ sudṛḍha-vrataḥ । akatthano gūḍha-garvo dhīrodāttaḥ su-sattva-bhṛt ।।
nirvyūḍha-vratam unnata-kṣiti-dharoddhāreṇa dhīrākṛtim । prekṣya tvāṃ mama durvitarkya-hṛdayaṃ dhīr gīś ca na spandate ।। gambhīratvādi-sāmānya-guṇā yad iha kīrtitāḥ । tad eteṣu tad-ādhikya-pratipādana-hetave ।।
idaṃ hi dhīrodāttatvaṃ pūrvaiḥ proktaṃ raghūdvahe । tat-tad-bhaktānusāreṇa tathā kṛṣṇe vilokyate ।। vidagdho nava-tāruṇyaḥ parihāsa-viśāradaḥ । niścinto dhīra-lalitaḥ syāt prāyaḥ preyasī-vaśaḥ ।।
vrīḍā-kuñcita-locanāṃ viracayann agre sakhīnām asau । kaiśoraṃ saphalī-karoti kalayan kuñje vihāraṃ hariḥ ।। govinde prakaṭaṃ dhīra-lalitatvaṃ pradarśyate । udāharanti nāṭya-jñāḥ prāyo atra makara-dhvajam ।।
śama-prakṛtikaḥ kleśa-sahanaś ca vivecakaḥ । vinayādi-guṇopeto dhīra-śānta udīryate ।। vacana-paṭima-bhaṅgī-sūcitāśeṣa-nītiḥ । dvija-patir iva sākṣāt prekṣyate kaṃsa-vairī ।।
yudhiṣṭhirādiko dhīrair dhīra-śāntaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। mātsaryavān ahaṅkārī māyāvī roṣaṇaś calaḥ । vikatthanaś ca vidvadbhir dhīroddhata udāhṛtaḥ ।। vāsaḥ kutracid andha-kūpa-kuhara-kroḍe adya nirmīyatām ।
jāgarmi tvad-upagrahāya bhujagaḥ kṛṣṇo atra kṛṣṇābhidhaḥ ।। dhīroddhatas tu vidvadbhir bhīmasenādir ucyate ।। mātsaryādyāḥ pratīyante doṣatvena yad apy amī । līlā-viśeṣa-śālitvān nirdoṣe atre guṇāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
ghorāḍambara-ḍambaraḥ suvikuṭām utkṣipya hastārgalām । re śrīdāma-kuraṅgasaṅgara-bhuvo bhaṅgaṃ tvam aṅgīkuru ।। mitho virodhino apy atra kecin nigaditā guṇāḥ । harau niraṅkuśaiśvaryāt ko api na syād asambhavaḥ ।।
asthūlaś cāṇuś caiva sthūlo aṇuś caiva sarvataḥ । avarṇaḥ sarvataḥ proktaḥ śyāmo raktānta-locanaḥ । aiśvarya-yogād bhagavān viruddhārtho abhidhīyate ।। tathāpi doṣāḥ parame naivāhāryāḥ kathañcana ।
guṇā viruddhā apy ete samāhāryāḥ samantataḥ ।। sarve nityāḥ śāśvatāś ca dehās tasya parātmanaḥ । hānopādāna-rahitā naiva prakṛtijāḥ kvacit ।। paramānanda-sandohā jñāna-mātrāś ca sarvataḥ ।
sarve sarva-guṇaiḥ pūrṇāḥ sarva-doṣa-vivarjitāḥ ।। aṣṭādaśa-mahā-doṣai rahitā bhagavat-tanuḥ । sarvaiśvaryamayī satya-vijñānānanda-rūpiṇī ।। mohas tandrā bhramo rukṣa-rasatā kāma ulbaṇaḥ ।
lolatā mada-mātsarye hiṃsā kheda-pariśramau ।। asatyaṃ krodha ākāṅkṣā āśaṅkā viśva-vibhramaḥ । viṣamatvaṃ parāpekṣā doṣā aṣṭādaśoditāḥ ।। itthaṃ sarvāvatārebhyas tato apy atrāvatāriṇaḥ ।
vrajendra-nandane suṣṭhu mādhurya-bhara īritaḥ ।। jīvanti loma-bilajā jagad-aṇḍa-nāthāḥ । govindam ādi-puruṣaṃ tam ahaṃ bhajāmi ।। athāṣṭāv anukīrtyante sad-guṇatvena viśrutāḥ ।
maṅgalālaṅkriyā-rūpāḥ sattva-bhedās tu pauruṣāḥ ।। śobhā vilāso mādhuryaṃ māṅgalyaṃ sthairya-tejasī । lalitaudāryam ity ete sattva-bhedās tu pauruṣāḥ ।। nīce dayādhike spardhā śauryotsāhau ca dakṣatā ।
satyaṃ ca vyaktim āyāti yatra śobheti tāṃ viduḥ ।। nīcān ālocya paścān namuci-ripu-mukhānūḍha-kāruṇya-vīciḥ । bandhūn ānandayiṣyann udaharatu hariḥ satya-sandho mahādrim ।। vṛṣabhasyeva gambhīrā gatir dhīraṃ ca vīkṣaṇam ।
sa-smitaṃ ca vaco yatra sa vilāsa itīryate ।। vyādhunvāno dvipa iva bhuvaṃ vikramāḍambareṇa । tuṅge raṅga-sthala-parisare sārasākṣaḥ sasāra ।। mādhuryam tan mādhuryaṃ bhaved yatra ceṣṭādeḥ spṛhaṇīyatā ।।
kadambaiḥ prālambaṃ pravalita-vilambaṃ viracayan । kuraṅgī-netrāyāṃ madhu-ripur apāṅgaṃ vikirati ।। māṅgalyam māṅgalyaṃ jagatām eva viśvāsāspadatā matā ।। rakṣī kṛṣṇa iti pramattam abhitaḥ krīḍāsu raktāḥ surāḥ ।
ke viśvambhara na tvad-aṅghri-yugale viśrambhitāṃ bhejire ।। sthairyam vyavasāyād acalanaṃ sthairyaṃ vighnākulād api ।। pratikule api sa-śūle, śive śivāyāṃ niraṃśukāyāṃ ca । vyalunād eva mukundo vindhyāvali-nandanasya bhujān ।।
tejaḥ sarva-cittāvagāhitvaṃ tejaḥ sadbhir udīryate ।। gopānāṃ svajano asatāṃ kṣitirbhujāṃ śāstā sva-pitroḥ śiśuḥ । vṛṣṇīnāṃ paradevateti vidito raṅgaḥ gataḥ sāgrajaḥ ।। yathā tejo budhair avajñāder asahiṣṇutvam ucyate ।।
nande cānakadundubhau ca purataḥ kaṃsena viśva-druhā । mañcasyopari sañcukurdiṣur asau paśyācyutaḥ prāñcati ।। lalitam śṛṅgāra-pracurā ceṣṭā yatra taṃ lalitaṃ viduḥ ।। kareṇa vyagrātmā sarabhasam asavyena rasikaḥ ।
udañcad-romāñcaṃ racayati ca kṛṣṇaḥ parikaram ।। audāryam ātmādy-arpaṇa-kāritvam audāryam iti kīrtyate ।। vadānyaḥ ko bhaved atra vadānyaḥ puruṣottamāt । akiñcanāya yenātmā nirguṇāyāpi dīyate ।।
sāmānyā nāyaka-guṇāḥ sthiratādyā yad apy amī । tathāpi pūrvataḥ kiñcid viśeṣāt punar īritāḥ ।। asya gargādayo dharme yuyudhānādayo yudhi । uddhavādyās tathā mantre sahāyāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।।
atha kṛṣṇa-bhaktāḥ tad-bhāva-bhāvita-svāntāḥ kṛṣṇa-bhaktā itīritāḥ ।। yo satya-vākya ity ādyā hrīmān ity antimā guṇāḥ । proktāḥ kṛṣṇe asya bhakteṣu te vijñeyā manīṣibhiḥ ।। te sādhakāś ca siddhāś ca dvi-vidhāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।।
utpanna-ratayaḥ samyaṅ nairvighnyam anupāgatāḥ । kṛṣṇa-sākṣāt-kṛtau yogyāḥ sādhakāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।। īśvare tad-adhīneṣu bāliśeṣu dviṣatsu ca । prema-maitrī-kṛpopekṣā yaḥ karoti sa madhyamaḥ ।।
tiṣṭhaty eva bhavāgni-hetir iti te dhīmann alaṃ cintayā । nediṣṭaḥ pṛthu-roma-tāṇḍava-bharāt kṛṣṇāmbudhasyodgamaḥ ।। bilvamaṅgala-tulyā ye sādhakās te prakīrtitāḥ ।। avijñātākhila-kleśāḥ sadā kṛṣṇāśrita-kriyāḥ ।
siddhāḥ syuḥ santata-prema-saukhyāsvāda-parāyaṇāḥ ।। samprāpta-siddhayaḥ siddhā nitya-siddhāś ca te tridhā ।। tatra samprāpta-siddhayaḥ sādhanaiḥ kṛpayā cāsya dvidhā samprāpta-siddhayaḥ ।। dūre yamā hy upari naḥ spṛhaṇīya-śīlāḥ ।
vaiklavya-bāṣpa-kalayā pulakī-kṛtāṅgāḥ ।। dṛk-pāte api ghṛṇāṃ kṛta-praṇatiṣu prāyeṇa mokṣādiṣu । nirdhautāsya-taṭān muhuḥ pulakino dhanyān namaskurmahe ।। mārkaṇḍeyādayaḥ proktāḥ sādhanaiḥ prāpta-siddhayaḥ ।।
nāsāṃ dvijāti-saṃskāro na nivāso gurāv api । na tapo nātma-mīmāṃsā na śaucaṃ na kriyāḥ śubhāḥ ।। athāpi hy uttamaḥśloke kṛṣṇe yogeśvareśvare । bhaktir dṛḍhā na cāsmākaṃ saṃskārādimatām api ।।
na sādhana-vidhau ca te śrama-lavasya gandho apy abhūt । mukunda-pada-padmayoḥ praṇaya-sīdhuno dhārayā ।। kṛpā-siddhā yajña-patnī-vairocani-śukādayaḥ ।। ātma-koṭi-guṇaṃ kṛṣṇe premāṇaṃ paramaṃ gatāḥ ।
nityānanda-guṇāḥ sarve nitya-siddhā mukundavat ।। atha brahmādi-devānāṃ tathā prārthanayā bhuvaḥ । āgato ahaṃ gaṇāḥ sarve jātās te api mayā saha ।। ete hi yādavāḥ sarve mad-gaṇā eva bhāmini ।
sarvadā mat-priyā devi mat-tulya-guṇa-śālinaḥ ।। aho bhāgyam aho bhāgyaṃ nanda-gopa-vrajaukasām । yan-mitraṃ paramānandaṃ pūrṇaṃ brahma sanātanam ।। dustyajaś cānurāgo asmin sarveṣāṃ no vrajaukasām ।
nanda te tanaye asmāsu tasyāpy autpattikaḥ katham ।। sanātanaṃ mitram iti tasyāpy autpattikaḥ katham । sneho asmāsv iti caiteṣāṃ nitya-preṣṭhatvam āgatam ।। ity ataḥ kathitā nitya-priyā yādava-vallavāḥ ।
eṣāṃ laukikavac-ceṣṭā līlā mura-ripor iva ।। yathā saumitri-bharatau yathā saṅkarṣaṇādayaḥ । tathā tenaiva jāyante nija-lokād yadṛcchayā ।। punas tenaiva gacchanti tat-padaṃ śāśvataṃ param ।
na karma-bandhanaṃ janma vaiṣṇavānāṃ ca vidyate ।। ye proktāḥ pañca-pañcāśat kramāt kaṃsaripor guṇāḥ । te cānye cāpi siddheṣu siddhidatvādayo matāḥ ।। bhaktās tu kīrtitāḥ śāntās tathā dāsa-sutādayaḥ ।
sakhāyo guru-vargāś ca preyasyaś ceti pañcadhā ।। uddīpanās tu te proktā bhāvam uddīpayanti ye । te tu śrī-kṛṣṇa-candrasya guṇāś ceṣṭāḥ prasādhanam ।। smitāṅga-saurabhe vaṃśa-śṛṅga-nūpura-kambavaḥ ।
padāṅka-kṣetra-tulasī-bhakta-tad-vāsarādayaḥ ।। tatra guṇāḥ guṇās tu trividhāḥ proktāḥ kāya-vāṅ-mānasāśrayāḥ ।। tatra kāyikāḥ vayaḥ-saundarya-rūpāṇi kāyikāmṛdutādayaḥ ।। guṇāḥ svarūpam evāsya kāyikādyā yadapy amī ।
bhedaṃ svīkṛtya varṇyante tathāpy uddīpanā iti ।। atas tasya svarūpasya syād ālambanataiva hi । uddīpanatvam eva syād bhūṣaṇādes tu kevalam ।। eṣām ālambanatvaṃ ca tathoddīpanatāpi ca ।।
tatra vayaḥ vayaḥ kaumāra-paugaṇḍa-kaiśoram iti tat tridhā ।। kaumāraṃ pañcamābdāntaṃ paugaṇḍaṃ daśamāvadhi । ā-ṣoḍaśāc ca kaiśoraṃ yauvanaṃ syāt tataḥ param ।। aucityāt tatra kaumāraṃ vaktavyaṃ vatsale rase ।
paugaṇḍaṃ preyasi tat-tat-khelādi-yogataḥ ।। śraiṣṭhyam ujjvala evāsya kaiśorasya tathāpy adaḥ । prāyaḥ sarva-rasaucityād atrodāhriyate kramāt ।। ādyaṃ madhyaṃ tathā śeṣaṃ kaiśoraṃ trividhaṃ bhavet ।।
varṇasyojjvalatā kāpi netrānte cāruṇa-cchaviḥ । romāvali-prakaṭatā kaiśore prathame sati ।। praviśati dṛśor ante kāntir manāg iva lohinī । sphurati suṣamā navyedānīṃ tanau vana-mālinaḥ ।।
vaijayantī-śikhaṇḍādi-naṭa-pravara-veśatā । vaṃśī-madhurimā vastra-śobhā cātra paricchadaḥ ।। bibhrad-vāsaḥ kanaka-kapiśaṃ vaijayantīṃ ca mālām । vṛndāraṇyaṃ sva-pada-ramaṇaṃ prāviśad gīta-kīrtiḥ ।।
kharatātra nakhāgrāṇāṃ dhanur āndolitā bhruvoḥ । radānāṃ rañjanaṃ rāga-cūrṇair ity ādi ceṣṭitam ।। śarālir iva śāṇitā nakhara-rājir agre kharā । na kā sakhi samīkṣaṇād yuvatir asya vitrasyati ।।
na vyādātuṃ kvacid api jane vaktram apy utsahante । sva-prāṇebhyas trayam udasṛjann adya toyāñjalīnām ।। ūru-dvayasya bāhvoś ca kāpi śrīr urasas tathā । mūrter mādhurimādyaṃ ca kaiśore sati madhyame ।।
garuḍa-maṇi-kavāṭī-sakhyam icchaty uraś ca । abhinava-taruṇimnaḥ prakrame keśavasya ।। mukhaṃ smita-vilāsāḍhyaṃ vibhramottarale dṛśau । tri-jagan-mohanaṃ gītam ity ādir iha mādhurī ।।
mukhāmbujam udañcita-smita-vilāsa-ramyādharam । hares taruṇimāṅkure sphurati mādhurī kāpy abhūt ।। vaidagdhī-sāra-vistāraḥ kuñja-keli-mahotsavaḥ । ārambho rāsa-līlāder iha ceṣṭādi-sauṣṭhavam ।।
talpair vicyuta-kāñcibhiḥ kvacid asau vyākīrṇa-kuñjotkarā । govindasya vilāsa-vṛndam adhikaṃ vṛndāṭavī śaṃsati ।। udasyan dharmenduṃ vidadhad abhito rāga-paṭalam । tarasvī kṛṣṇābbhre madhurima-bharārko abhyudayate ।।
pūrvato apy adhikotkarṣaṃ bāḍham aṅgāni bibhrati । tri-vali-vyaktir ity ādyaṃ kaiśore carame sati ।। śata-makha-maṇi-stambhārambha-pramāthi-bhuja-dvayam । madana-kadalī-sādhiṣṭhoruṃ smarāmy asurāntakam ।।
vidhūnita-vadhū-dhṛtiṃ varakalā-vilāsāspadam । sphurat-taruṇimodgamaṃ taruṇi paśya pītāmbaram ।। idam eva hareḥ prājñair nava-yauvanam ucyate ।। atra gokula-devīnāṃ bhāva-sarvasva-śālitā ।
abhūta-pūrva-kandarpa-tantra-līlotsavādayaḥ ।। kīrair arpayati kvacid vitanute krīḍābhisārodyamam । sandhiṃ kvāpy anuśāsti kuñja-nṛpatiḥ śṛṅgāra-rājyottamam ।। patyur vañcana-cāturī guṇanikā kuñja-prayāṇe niśi ।
kaiśoreṇa tavādya kṛṣṇa guruṇā gaurī-gaṇaḥ paṭhyate ।। netuḥ svarūpam evoktaṃ kaiśoram iha yadyapi । nānākṛti-prakaṭanāt tathāpy uddīpanaṃ matam ।। bālye api nava-tāruṇya-prākaṭyaṃ kvacit ।
tan nātirasa-vāhitvān na rasajñair udāhṛtam ।। atha saundaryam bhavet saundaryam aṅgānāṃ sanniveśo yathocitam ।। bhuja-dvandvaṃ stambha-dyuti-suvalitaṃ pārśva-yugalam । na kasyāḥ kaṃsāre harati hṛdayaṃ paṅkaja-dṛśaḥ ।।
atha rūpam vibhūṣaṇaṃ vibhūṣyaṃ syād yena tad rūpam ucyate ।। nītāṅga-saṅgatim alaṅkṛtaye varāṅgi । sā pratyuta svayam analpam alaṅkṛtāsīt ।। atha mṛdutā mṛdutā komalasyāpi saṃsparśāsahatocyate ।।
ahaha navāmbuda-kānter amuṣya sukumāratā kumārasya । api nava-pallava-saṅgād aṅgāny aparajya śīryanti ।। ye nāyaka-prakaraṇe vācikā mānasās tathā । guṇāḥ proktānta evātra jñeyā uddīpanā budhaḥ ।।
ceṣṭā ceṣṭā rāsādi-līlāḥ syus tathā duṣṭa-vadhādayaḥ ।। gīrvāṇībhir anaṅga-raṅga-vivaśaṃ sandṛśyamāna-śriyaḥ । rāsārambha-rasārthino madhurimā cetāṃsi naḥ karṣati ।। mlānaḥ salīlam api yatra śiro dhunāne ।
taṃ duṣṭa-puṅgavam asau harir unmamātha ।। atha prasādhanam kathitaṃ vasanākalpa-maṇḍanādyaṃ prasādhanam ।। navārka-raśmi-kāśmīra-haritālādi-sannibham । yugaṃ catuṣkaṃ bhūyiṣṭhaṃ vasanaṃ tri-vidhaṃ hareḥ ।।
tatra yugam paridhānaṃ sa-saṃvyānaṃ yuga-rūpam udīritam ।। tad-upari navaraktaṃ vastram itthaṃ dadhānaḥ । praṇayatu mama netrābhīṣṭa-pūrtiṃ mukundaḥ ।। catuṣkam catuṣkaṃ kañcukoṣṇīṣa-tunda-bandhāntarīyakam ।।
channāṅgaḥ puraṭa-rucoru-kañcakena । kaṃsārir vahati mahotsave mudaṃ naḥ ।। khaṇḍitākhaṇḍitaṃ bhūri naṭa-veśa-kriyocitam । aneka-varṇaṃ vasanaṃ bhūyiṣṭhaṃ kathitaṃ budhaiḥ ।।
paṭaiḥ kṛta-yathocita-prakaṭa-sanniveśojjvalaḥ । karoti karabhoru me ghana-rucir mudaṃ mādhavaḥ ।। keśa-bandhanam ālepo mālā-citra-viśeṣakaḥ । tāmbūla-keli-padmādir ākalpaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।।
syāj jūṭaḥ kavarī cūḍā veṇī ca kaca-bandhanam । pāṇḍuraḥ karburaḥ pīta ity ālepas tridhā mataḥ ।। mālā tridhā vaijayantī ratna-mālā vana-srajaḥ । asyā vaikakṣakāpīḍa-prālambādyā bhidā matāḥ ।।
makarī-patra-bhaṅgāḍhyaṃ citraṃ pīta-sitāruṇam । tathā viśeṣako api syād anyad ūhyaṃ svayaṃ budhaiḥ ।। bhakti-ccheda-lasat-sughṛṣṭa-ghusṛṇālepa-śriyā peśalaḥ । śyāmāṅga-dyutir adya me sakhi dṛśor dugdhe mudaṃ mādhavaḥ ।।
kirīṭaṃ kuṇḍale hāraś catuṣkī valayormayaḥ । keyūra-nūpurādyaṃ ca ratna-maṇḍanam ucyate ।। hāras tāro valayam amalaṃ candrā-cāruś catuṣkī । aṅgair evābharaṇa-paṭalī bhūṣitā dogdhi bhūṣām ।।
kusumādi-kṛtaṃ cedaṃ vanya-maṇḍanam īritam । dhātu-k ptaṃ tilakaṃ patra-bhaṅga-latādikam ।। vikhaṇḍitāśeṣa-rasāntarāṇi । jayanti śītāni tava smitāni ।।
pulakayati vapur naḥ kāpy apūrvā munīnām । kuru-bhuvam anavadyāmoda-sindhur viveśa ।। nindan sudhā-madhurimāṇam adhīra-dharmā । vaṃśī-dhvanir jayati kaṃsa-nisūdanasya ।।
eṣa tridhā bhaved veṇu-muralī-vaṃśikety api ।। pāvikākhyo bhaved veṇur dvādaśāṅguler dairghya-bhāk । sthaulye aṅguṣṭha-mitaḥ ṣaḍbhir eṣa randhraiḥ samanvitaḥ ।। hasta-dvaya-mitāyāmā mukha-randhra-samanvitā ।
catuḥ-svara-cchidra-yuktā muralī cāru-nādinī ।। ardhāṅgulāntaronmānaṃ tārādi-vivarāṣṭakam । tataḥ sārdhāṅgulād yatra mukha-randhraṃ tathāṅgulam ।। śiro vedāṅgulaṃ pucchaṃ try-aṅgulaṃ sā tu vaṃśikā ।
nava-randhrā smṛtā sapta-daśāṅgula-mitā budhaiḥ ।। daśāṅgulāntarā syāc cet sā tāra-mukha-randhrayoḥ । mahānandeti vyākhyātā tathā saṃmohinīti ca ।। bhavet sūryāntarā sā cet tata ākarṣiṇī matā ।
ānandinī tadā vaṃśī bhaved indrāntarā yadi ।। gopānāṃ vallabhā seyaṃ vaṃśulīti ca viśrutā । kramān maṇimayī haimī vaiṇavīti tridhā ca sā ।। śṛṅgaṃ tu gavalaṃ hema-nibaddhāgrima-paścimam ।
ratna-jāla-sphuran-madhyaṃ mandra-ghoṣābhidhaṃ smṛtam ।। tārāvalīlā-garalena daṣṭā । viṣāṇi kāmaṃ dvi-guṇī-cakāra ।। niśamayya sambhṛta-gabhīra-sambhramā ।
bahir adya hanta guravaḥ puraḥ sthitāḥ ।। atha kambuḥ kambus tu dakṣiṇāvartaḥ pāñcajanyatayocyate ।। tridiva-pura-purandhrī-vṛnda-nāndīkaro ayam । kṛta-pulaka-kadambaḥ kambu-rājasya nādaḥ ।।
premṇordhva-romāśru-kalākulekṣaṇaḥ । prabhor amūny aṅghri-rajāṃsy aho iti ।। sphuṭam amunā yamunā-taṭīm ayāsīt । dhvaja-kuliśākuśa-paṅkajāṅkiteyam ।।
bata dūre astu sudurlabha-śriyām । praviśan nāma mano dhinoti naḥ ।। tulasī-mañjari kiñcid arthayāmi । caraṇābja-śaraṇābhilāṣiṇaṃ mām ।।
abhyutthitaḥ sādhvasa-vismṛta-kramaḥ । pārṣat-pradhānāv iti saṃhatāñjaliḥ ।। smita-vilasad-apāṅgaḥ prāṅgaṇe bhrājamānaḥ । kathaya sa dayitas te kvāyam āste vayasyaḥ ।।
adbhutā bahavaḥ santu bhagavat-parva-vāsarāḥ । āmodayati māṃ dhanyā kṛṣṇa-bhādrapadāṣṭamī ।। iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhau dakṣiṇa-vibhāge bhakti-rasa-sāmānya-nirūpaṇe vibhāva-laharī prathamā । anubhāvās tu citta-stha-bhāvānām avabodhakāḥ ।
te bahir vikriyā prāyāḥ proktā udbhāsvarākhyayā ।। nṛtyaṃ viluṭhitaṃ gītaṃ krośanaṃ tanu-moṭanam । huṅkāro jṛmbhaṇaṃ śvāsa-bhūmā lokānapekṣitā । lālā-sravo aṭṭahāsaś ca ghūrṇā-hikkādayo api ca ।।
te śītāḥ kṣepaṇāś ceti yathārthākhyā dvidhoditāḥ । śītāḥ syur gīta-jṛmbhādyā nṛtyādyāḥ kṣepaṇābhidhāḥ ।। hari-vaktrendum avekṣya kampitaḥ । dhvanibhis tāṇḍavam āśrito haraḥ ।।
śvaphalka-putro bhagavat-prapannaḥ । aceṣṭata prema-vibhinna-dhairyaḥ ।। vana-srag-āmodam avāpya mattā । gātraṃ sugātrī vraṇayāñcakāra ।।
kurvatī tava navaṃ guṇa-gānam । rādhikādya-dṛṣadāṃ suhṛdāṃ ca ।। sa vicukrośa tathādya nāradaḥ । danujā yena dhṛtā vililyire ।।
kararīva vraja-rāja-nanda । muhur ākrośad ihādya sundarī ।। prīṇite manasi vaiṇiko muniḥ । vapus troṭayaty akhila-yajña-sūtrakam ।।
śaṅkarasya divi huṅkṛti-svanaḥ । sādhu-vṛndam akarot sadā navam ।। udayati pūrṇe kalānidhau purataḥ । bhajate jṛmbhām aho citram ।।
vivṛddha-tṛṣṇā lalitākhya-cātakī । kṛṣṇāmbudākāram avekṣya cukṣubhe ।। aho paśyata nārīṇām api kṛṣṇe jagad-gurau । duranta-bhāvaṃ yo avidhyan mṛtyupāśān gṛhābhidhān ।।
bhuvi viluṭhāma naṭāma nirviśāma ।। śaṅke prema-bhujaṅgena daṣṭaḥ kaṣṭaṃ gato muniḥ । niścalasya yad etasya lālā sravati vaktrataḥ ।। aṭṭahāsaḥ hāsād bhinno aṭṭahāso ayaṃ citta-vikṣepa-sambhavaḥ ।।
cetas taṭe bhakti-latā praphullā । prasūna-puñjāś caṭulaṃ skhalanti ।। nanu murali tvayi phutkṛti-cchalena । sakhi tava ghūrṇayati vrajāmbujākṣīḥ ।।
mudhā priya-sakhīṃ prati tvam aśivaṃ kim āśaṅkase । varākṣi harir ity asau vitanute adya hikkā-bharam ।। vapur-utphullatā-raktodgamādyāḥ syuḥ pare api ye । atīva-viralatvāt te naivātra parikīrtitāḥ ।।
iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhau dakṣiṇa-vibhāge bhakti-rasa-sāmānya-nirūpaṇe anubhāva-laharī dvitīyā । kṛṣna-sambandhibhiḥ sākṭāt kiñcid vā vyavadhānataḥ । bhāvaiś cittam ihākrāntaṃ sattvam ity ucyate budhaiḥ ।। sattvād asmāt samutpannā ye ye bhāvās te tu sāttvikāḥ ।
snigdhā digdhās tathā rukṣā ity amī trividhā matāḥ ।। tatra snigdhāḥ snigdhās tu sāttvikā mukhyā gauṇāś ceti dvidhā matāḥ ।। ākramān mukhyayā ratyā mukhyāḥ syuḥ sāttvikā amī । vijñeyaḥ kṛṣṇa-sambandhaḥ sākṣād evātra sūribhiḥ ।।
srajāṃ varāṃ kunda-viḍambi-dantī । gāndharvikā spandana-śūnya-gātrī ।। mukhyaḥ stambho ayam itthaṃ te jñeyāḥ svedādayo api ca ।। ratyākramaṇataḥ proktā gauṇās te gauṇa-bhūtayā ।
atra kṛṣṇasya sambandhaḥ syāt kiñcid vyavadhānataḥ ।। puri nīte puruṣottame purā । nṛpam ākrośati gokuleśvarī ।। imau gauṇau vaivarṇya-svara-bhedau ।
rati-dvaya-vinābhūtair bhāvair manasa ākramāt । jane jāta-ratau digdhās te ced raty-anugāminaḥ ।। sā niśānta-luṭhad-udbhaṭa-gātrīm । putram ākula-matir vicinoti ।।
kampo raty-anugāmitvād asau digdha itīryate ।। madhurāścarya-tad-vārtotpannair mud-vismayādibhiḥ । jātā bhaktopame rukṣā rati-śūnye jane kvacit ।। svaṃ ceṣṭayā hṛdayam atra vivṛṇvato api ।
tasyāṅgam utpulakitaṃ madhurais tadāsīt ।। rukṣo ayaṃ rati-śūnyatvād romāñcaṃ kathito budhaiḥ । mumukṣu-prabhṛtau pūrvaṃ yo ratābhyāsa īritaḥ ।। cittaṃ sattvībhavat prāṇe nyasyaty ātmānam udbhaṭam ।
prāṇas tu vikriyāṃ gacchan dehaṃ vikṣobhayaty alam । tadā stambhādayo bhāvā bhakta-dehe bhavanty amī ।। te stambha-sveda-romāñcāḥ svara-bhedo atha vepathuḥ । vaivarṇyam aśru pralaya ity aṣṭau sāttvikāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
catvāri kṣmādi-bhūtāni prāṇo jātv avalambate । kadācit sva-pradhānaḥ san dehe carati sarvataḥ ।। stambhaṃ bhūmi-sthitaḥ prāṇas tanoty aśru-jalāśrayaḥ । tejasthaḥ sveda-vaivarṇye pralayaṃ viyad-āśrayaḥ ।।
svastha eva kramān manda-madhya-tīvratva-bheda-bhāk । romāñca-kampa-vaivarṇyāṇy atra trīṇi tanoty asau ।। bahir antaś ca vikṣobha-vidhāyitvād ataḥ sphuṭam । proktānubhāvatāmīṣāṃ bhāvatā ca manīṣibhiḥ ।।
stambho harṣa-bhayāścarya-viṣādāmarṣa-sambhavaḥ । tatra vāg-ādi-rāhityaṃ naiścalyaṃ śūnyatādayaḥ ।। līlāvaloka-pratilabdha-mānāḥ । dhiyo avatasthuḥ kila kṛtya-śeṣāḥ ।।
purataḥ prāṇa-parārdhataḥ parārdhyam । nayanā hanta babhūva niścalāṅgī ।। tato atikutukodvṛtya- stimitaikādaśendriyaḥ । tad-dhāmnābhūd ajas tūṣṇīṃ pūr-devy-antīva putrikā ।।
śiśoḥ śyāmasya paśyantī śailam abhraṃlihaṃ kare । tatra citrārpitevāsīd goṣṭhī goṣṭha-nivāsinām ।। pūrataḥ prekṣya viśantam acyutam । prakaṭaṃ citrapaṭāyate divi ।।
patri-mokṣam akṛpe kṛpī-sute । niṣkriyaḥ kṣaṇam abhūt kapi-dhvajaḥ ।। atha svedaḥ svedo harṣa-bhaya-krodhādi-jaḥ kleda-karas tanoḥ ।। mugdhākṣi cāturyam urīkaroṣi ।
svinnāsi bhinnā kusumāyudhena ।। harim ākruśya girā pragalbhayā । ajani svinna-tanuḥ sa raktakaḥ ।। samīkṣya śakraṃ saruṣo garutmataḥ ।
nipetur aṅgād ghana-nīra-bindavaḥ ।। romāñco ayaṃ kilāścarya-harṣotsāha-bhayādijaḥ । romṇām abhyudgamas tatra gātra-saṃsparśanādayaḥ ।। vilokya vailakṣyavatī mukhāntaḥ ।
tanu-ruhaiḥ kuḍmalitāṅga-yaṣṭiḥ ।। sparśotsavotpulakitāṅga-ruhair vibhāsi । āho varāha-vapuṣaḥ parirambhaṇena ।। śṛṅgaṃ kelir aṇārambhe raṇayaty agha-mardane ।
śrīdāmno yoddhu-kāmasya reme romāñcitaṃ vapuḥ ।। prekṣya tatra puruṣottamaṃ puraḥ । śiśriye vikaṭa-kaṇṭakāṃ tanum ।। visāda-vismayāmarṣa-harṣa-bhīty-ādi-sambhavam ।
vaisvaryaṃ svara-bhedaḥ syād eṣa gadgadikādikṛt ।। svayam ity ardha-viśīrṇa-jalpayā । ślathayantyā kila roditā sakhī ।। mukundam udvīkṣya vinamra-kandharaḥ ।
sa-vepathur gadgadayailatelayā ।। kṛṣṇaṃ tad-artha-vinivartita-sarva-kāmāḥ । saṃrambha-gadgada-giro abruvatānuraktāḥ ।। harṣād, yathā tatraiva hṛṣyat-tanūruho bhāva-pariklinnātma-locanaḥ ।।
girā gadgadayāstauṣīt sattvam ālambya sātvataḥ । praṇamya mūrdhnāvahitaḥ kṛtāñjali-puṭaḥ śanaiḥ ।। śrutvā mad-īritam udīrṇa-vivarṇa-bhāvaḥ । patrī mukunda tad anena sa hārito asti ।।
atha vepathuḥ vitrāsāmarṣa-harṣādyair vepathur gātra-laulya-kṛt ।। prekṣya vistṛta-bhujaṃ jighṛkṣayā । kampa-sampadam adhatta rādhikā ।। kṛṣṇādhikṣepa-jātena vyākulo nakulāmbujaḥ ।
cakampe drāg amarṣeṇa bhū-kampe girirāḍ iva ।। vihasasi kathaṃ hatāśe paśya bhayenādya kampamānāsmi । cañcalam upasīdantaṃ nivāraya vraja-pates tanayam ।। viṣāda-roṣa-bhīty-āder vaivarṇyaṃ varṇa-vikriyā ।
