bhāva-jñair atra mālinya-kārśyādyāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।। śvetīkṛtākhila-janaṃ viraheṇa tavādhunā । gokulaṃ kṛṣṇa devarṣeḥ śvetadvīpa-bhramaṃ dadhe ।। vīkṣya kaṃsa-sahajān udāyudhān ।
prodyad-indu-nibham ānanaṃ babhau ।। parvataṃ vara-mudasya līlayā । ūcivān manasi bhītim utthitām ।। viṣāde śvetimā proktā dhausaryaṃ kālimā kvacit ।
roṣe tu raktimā bhītyāṃ kālimā kvāpi śuklimā ।। raktimā lakṣyate vyakto harṣodreke api kutracit । atrāsārvatrikatvena naivāsyodāhṛtiḥ kṛtā ।। harṣa-roṣa-viṣādādyair aśru netre jalodgamaḥ ।
harṣaje aśruṇi śītatvam auṣṇyaṃ roṣādi-sambhave । sarvatra nayana-kṣobha-rāga-saṃmārjanādayaḥ ।। govinda-prekṣaṇākṣepi-bāṣpa-pūrābhivarṣiṇam । uccair anindad ānandam aravinda-vilocanā ।।
tasyāḥ susrāva netrābhyāṃ vāri praṇaya-kopajam । kuśeśaya-palāśābhyām avaśyāya-jalaṃ yathā ।। reje aśru-visrāvi ruṣoparaktam । sāndhya-tviṣā grastam ivendu-bimbam ।।
bhuvaṃ likhanty aśrubhir añjanāsitaiḥ । tasthāv adho-mukhy atiduḥkha-ruddha-vāk ।। pralayaḥ sukha-duḥkhābhyāṃ ceṣṭā-jñāna-nirākṛtiḥ । atrānubhāvāḥ kathitā mahī-nipatanādayaḥ ।।
milantaṃ harim ālokya latā-puñjād atarkitam । jñapti-śūnya-manā reje niścalāṅgī vrajāṅganā ।। anyāś ca tad-anudhyāna-nivṛttāśeṣa-vṛttayaḥ । nābhyajānan imaṃ lokam ātma-lokaṃ gatā iva ।।
sarve hi sattva-mūlatvād bhāvā yadyapi sāttvikāḥ । tathāpy amīṣāṃ sattvaika-mūlatvāt sāttvika-prathā ।। sattvasya tāratamyāt prāṇa-tanu-kṣobha-tāratamyaṃ syāt । tata eva tāratamyaṃ sarveṣāṃ sāttvikānāṃ syāt ।।
dhūmāyitās te jvalitā dīptā uddīpta-saṃjñitāḥ । vṛddhiṃ yathottaraṃ yāntaḥ sāttvikāḥ syuś catur-vidhāḥ ।। sā bhūri-kāla-vyāpitvaṃ bahv-aṅga-vyāpitā'pi ca । svarūpeṇa tathotkarṣa iti vṛddhis tridhā bhavet ।।
tatra netrāmbu-vaisvarya-varjānām eva yujyate । bahv-aṅga-vyāpitāmīṣāṃ tayoḥ kāpi viśiṣṭatā ।। tatrāśrūṇāṃ dṛg-aucchūnya-kāritvam avadātatā । tathā tārātivaicitrī-vailakṣaṇya-vidhāyitā ।
vaisvarṇyasya tu bhinnatve kauṇṭhya-vyākulatādayaḥ ।। bhinnatvaṃ sthāna-vibhraṃśaḥ kauṇṭhyaṃ syāt sanna-kaṇṭhatā । vyākulatvaṃ tu nānocca-nīca-gupta-viluptatā ।। prāyo dhūmāyitā eva rukṣās tiṣṭhanti sāttvikāḥ ।
snigdhās tu prāyaśaḥ sarve caturdhaiva bhavanty amī ।। mahotsavādi-vṛtteṣu sad-goṣṭhī-tāṇḍavādiṣu । jvalanty ullāsinaḥ kvāpi te rukṣā api kasyacit ।। sarvānanda-camatkāra-hetur bhāvo varo ratiḥ ।
ete hi tad-vinābhāvān na camatkāritāśrayāḥ ।। advitīyā amī bhāvā athavā sa-dvitīyakāḥ । īṣad-vyaktā apahnotuṃ śakyā dhūmāyitā matāḥ ।। pakṣmāgra-miśra-viralāśrur abhūt purodhāḥ ।
prasvinna-nāsikam uvāha mukhāravindam ।। te dvau trayo vā yugapad yāntaḥ suprakaṭāṃ daśām । śakyāḥ kṛcchreṇa nihnotuṃ jvalitā iti kīrtitāḥ ।। dṛśau sāsre piñchaṃ na paricinutaṃ satvara-kṛti ।
vanād vaṃśī-dhvāne parisaram avāpte śravaṇayoḥ ।। hriyā sadyo gūḍhāḥ sakhi vighaṭito vepathur api । tathāpy ūhāñcakre mama manasi rāgaḥ parijanaiḥ ।। prauḍhāṃ tri-caturā vyaktiṃ pañca vā yugapad-gatāḥ ।
saṃvarītum aśakyās te dīptā dhīrair udāhṛtāḥ ।। na gadgada-niruddha-vāk prabhur abhūd upaślokane । madhu-dviṣi parisphuraty avaśam-mūrtir āsīn muniḥ ।। sa-romāñce kampe himam anilam ākrośasi kutaḥ ।
nirābādhā rādhe vadati madanādhiṃ svara-bhidā ।। ekadā vyaktim āpannāḥ pañca-ṣāḥ sarva eva vā । ārūḍhā paramotkarṣam uddīptā iti kīrtitāḥ ।। dhatte kākubhir ākulaṃ vilapati mlāyaty analpoṣmabhiḥ ।
sadyas tad-viraheṇa muhyati muhur goṣṭhādhivāsī janaḥ ।। uddīptā eva sūddiptā mahā-bhāve bhavanty amī । sarva eva parāṃ koṭiṃ sāttvikā yatra bibhrati ।। kiṃ ca athātra sāttvikābhāsā vilikhyante catur-vidhāḥ ।।
raty-ābhāsa-bhavās te tu sattvābhāsa-bhavās tathā । niḥsattvāś ca pratīpāś ca yathā-pūrvam amī varāḥ ।। tatra ādyāḥ mumukṣu-pramukheṣv ādyā raty-ābhāsāt puroditāt ।। vārāṇasī-nivāsī kaścid ayaṃ vyāharan hareś caritam ।
yati-goṣṭhyām utpulakaḥ siñcati gaṇḍa-dvayīm asraiḥ ।। mud-vismayāder ābhāsaḥ prodyan jātyā ślathe hṛdi । sattvābhāsa iti proktaḥ sattvābhāsa-bhavās tataḥ ।। jaran-mīmāṃsakasyāpi śṛṇvataḥ kṛṣṇa-vibhramam ।
hṛṣṭāyamāna-manaso babhūvotpulakaṃ vapuḥ ।। kathaṃ kathana-cāturī-madhurimā gurur varṇyatām । niśamya vijayaṃ prabhor dadhati bāṣpa-dhārām amī ।। nisarga-picchila-svānte tad-abhyāsa-pare api ca ।
sattvābhāsaṃ vināpi syuḥ kvāpy aśru-pulakādayaḥ ।। niśamayato hari-caritaṃ na hi sukha-duḥkhādayo asya hṛdi bhāvāḥ । anabhiniveśāj jātā katham asravad asram aśrāntam ।। prakṛtyā śithilaṃ yeṣāṃ manaḥ picchilam eva vā ।
teṣv eva sāttvikābhāsaḥ prāyaḥ saṃsadi jāyate ।। atha pratīpāḥ hitād anyasya kṛṣṇasya pratīpāḥ krud-bhayādibhiḥ ।। tasya prasphuritauṣṭhasya raktādhara-taṭasya ca । vaktraṃ kaṃsasya roṣeṇa rakta-sūryāyate tadā ।।
siṣveda mallas tv adhi-bhāla-śukti । atyādarāt pādyam ivājahāra ।। niśamya kaṃsasya bhayātirekam । parimlāna-mukhas tadāsīt ।।
nāsty arthaḥ sāttvikābhāsa-kathane ko api yadyapi । sāttvikānāṃ vivekāya dik tathāpi pradarśitā ।। iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhau dakṣiṇa-vibhāge bhakti-rasa-sāmānya-nirūpaṇe sāttvika-laharī tṛtīyā । athocyante trayas-triṃśad-bhāvā ye vyabhicāriṇaḥ ।
viśeṣeṇābhimukhyena caranti sthāyinaṃ prati ।। vāg-aṅga-sattva-sūcyā jñeyās te vyabhicāriṇaḥ । sañcārayanti bhāvasya gatiṃ sañcāriṇo api ।। unmajjanti nimajjanti sthāyiny amṛta-vāridhau ।
ūrmivad vardhayanty enaṃ yānti tad-rūpatāṃ ca te ।। nirvedo atha viṣādo dainyaṃ glāni-śramau ca mada-garvau । śaṅkā-trāsāvegā unmādāpasmṛtī tathā vyādhiḥ ।। moho mṛtir ālasyaṃ jāḍyaṃ vrīḍāvahitthā ca ।
smṛtir atha vitarka-cintā-mati-dhṛtayo harṣa utsukatvaṃ ca ।। augryam arṣāsūyāś cāpalyaṃ caiva nidrā ca । suptir bodha itīme bhāvā vyabhicāriṇaḥ samākhyātāḥ ।। mahārti-viprayogerṣyā-sad-vivekādi-kalpitam ।
svāvamānanam evātra nirveda iti kathyate । atra cintāśru-vaivarṇya-dainya-niḥśvasitādayaḥ ।। pālitair viphala-puṇya-phalair naḥ । svaṃ kuṭumbini haṭhāj juhavāma ।।
apuṣpite nīrasatāṃ prayāte । prāṇity apuṇyaḥ subalo dvirephaḥ ।। śravaṇayor alam aśravaṇir mama । sakhi vilocanayoś ca kilānayoḥ ।।
stotavyā yadi tāvat sā nāradena tavāgrataḥ । durbhago ayaṃ janas tatra kim artham anuśabditaḥ ।। rājya-śriyonnaddha-madasya bhūpateḥ । āsajjamānasya duranta-cintayā ।।
amaṅgalam api procya nirvedaṃ prathamaṃ muniḥ । mene amuṃ sthāyinaṃ śānta iti jalpanti kecana ।। iṣṭānavāpti-prārabdha-kāryāsiddhi-vipattitaḥ । aparādhādito api syād anutāpo viṣaṇṇatā ।।
atropāya-sahāyānusandhiś cintā ca rodanam । vilāpa-śvāsa-vaivarṇya-mukha-śoṣādayo api ca ।। mano-vṛttiś ceyaṃ smṛti-vidhuratā-paddhatim agāt । mayā hanta prāpto na bhajana-rucer apy avasaraḥ ।।
yatnena tair viracitā vana-mālikā ca । hā tāvad eva tarasā virarāma nidrā ।। katham asau na nigṛhya gṛhe dhṛtaḥ । vidhuritaṃ vidhum atra vidhitsati ।।
hy ahaṃ kiyān aiccham ivārcir agnau ।। syamantakam ahaṃ hṛtvā gato ghorāsyam antakam । karavai taraṇīṃ kāṃ vā kṣipto vaitaraṇīyam anu ।। duḥkha-trāsāparādhādyair anaurjityaṃ tu dīnatā ।
cāṭu-kṛn-māndya-mālinya-cintāṅga-jaḍimādi-kṛt ।। avitṛṣa-ṣaḍa-mitro labdha-śāntiḥ kathaṅcit । abhayam ṛtam aśokaṃ pāhi māpannam īśa ।। abhidravati mām īśa śaras taptāyaso vibho ।
kāmaṃ dahatu māṃ nātha mā me garbho nipātyatām ।। eṣo anukampyo mayi nāthavān iti ।। mā'nayaṃ bhoḥ kṛthās tvāṃ tu nanda-gopa-sutaṃ priyam । jānīmo aṅga vraja-ślāghyaṃ dehi vāsāṃsi vepitāḥ ।।
ojaḥ somātmakaṃ dehe bala-puṣṭi-kṛd asya tu । kṣayāccham ādhi-raty-ādyair glānir niṣprāṇatā matā । kampāṅga-jāḍya-vaivarṇya-kārśya-dṛg-bhramaṇādi-kṛt ।। goṣṭhāntar-madhuripu-kīrti-nartitauṣṭhī ।
kṛṣṇāya klama-bhara-niḥspṛhā babhūva ।। cāru puṣpa-paṭalaṃ vicinvatī । kānane kṣaṇam abhūn mṛgekṣaṇā ।। kṣīṇa-jīvanatayoccala-haṃsā ।
śuṣyati sma sarasī śucineva ।। kṛṣṇena talpāvaropitā sā । jyotsnā-kṛtānandam alindam āpa ।। adhva-nṛtya-ratādy-utthaḥ khedaḥ śrama itīryate ।
nidrā-svedāṅga-saṃmarda-jṛmbhāśvāsādi-bhāg asau ।। vrajājirāntar vraja-rāja-rājñī । babhūva gharmāmbu-karambitāṅgī ।। saṅgītonmukha-mukharair vṛtaḥ suhṛdbhiḥ ।
kurvāṇas taṭa-bhuvi tāṇḍavāni rāmaḥ ।। tāsām ativihāreṇa śrāntānāṃ vadanāni saḥ । prāmṛjat karuṇaḥ premṇā śantamenāṅga pāṇinā ।। viveka-hara ullāso madaḥ sa dvi-vidho mataḥ ।
madhu-pāna-bhavo anaṅga-vikriyā-bhara-jo api ca । gaty-aṅga-vāṇī-skhalana-dṛg-ghūrṇā-raktimādi-kṛt ।। pinasmi jagad-aṇḍakaṃ nanu hariḥ krudhaṃ dhāsyati । udeti mada-ḍambara-skhalita-cūḍam agre halī ।।
kṛ-kṛṣṇa vavada drutaṃ ha-ha-hasanti kiṃ vṛṣṇayaḥ । mada-skhalitam ālapan hala-dharaḥ śriyaḥ vaḥ kriyāt ।। uttamas tu madāc chete madhyo hasati pāyati । kaniṣṭhaḥ krośati svairaṃ puruṣaṃ vakti roditi ।।
mado api tri-vidhaḥ proktas taruṇādi-prabhedataḥ । atra nātyupayogitvād vistārya na hi varṇitaḥ ।। bhramati hasati rodity āsyam antardadhāti । nava-madana-madāndhā hanta gāndharvikeyam ।।
saubhāgya-rūpa-tāruṇya-guṇa-sarvottamāśrayaiḥ । iṣṭa-lābhādinā cānya-helanaṃ garva īryate ।। atra solluṇṭha-vacanaṃ līlānuttara-dāyitā । svāṅgekṣā nihnavo anyasya vacanāśravaṇādayaḥ ।।
hastam utkṣipya yāto asi balāt kṛṣṇa kim adbhutam । hṛdayād yadi niryāsi pauruṣaṃ gaṇayāmi te ।। dhanyā babhūva nitarām api yauvana-śrīḥ । dṛk-pātam ācaratu kṛṣṇa kathaṃ sakhī me ।।
dāmāni kāmaṃ dhṛta-rāmaṇīyakaiḥ । kṛṣṇo madīyāṃ hṛdi vismitaḥ srajam ।। vināyakānīkapa-mūrdhasu prabho ।। āsādya nandita-matir muhur uddhato asmi ।
vaikuṇṭha-nātha-karuṇām api nādya cetaḥ ।। svīya-cauryāparādhādeḥ para-krauryāditas tathā । svāniṣṭotprekṣaṇaṃ yat tu sā śaṅkety abhidhīyate । atrāsya-śoṣa-vaivarṇya-dik-prekṣā-līnatādayaḥ ।।
sa-dambham ambhoruha-sambhavas tadā । aṣṭābhir aṣṭau haritaḥ samīkṣate ।। nihnutya dūre yad ahaṃ prayātaḥ । śarmāṇi citte mama nirbhinatti ।।
yad-avadhi vṛṣṭim acīkaraḥ śacīśa । śriyam aviśaṅkam alaṅkuru tvam aindrīm ।। sahacari vallava-candra-viprayogaḥ । danujapater nagare yathāsya vāsaḥ ।।
śaṅkā tu pravara-strīṇāṃ bhīrutvād bhaya-kṛd bhavet ।। trāsaḥ kṣobho hṛdi taḍid-ghora-sattvogra-nisvanaiḥ । pārśvasthālamba-romāñca-kampa-stambha-bhramādi-kṛt ।। bāḍhaṃ niviḍayā sadyas taḍitā tāḍitekṣaṇaḥ ।
rakṣa kṛṣṇeti cukrośa ko api gopī-stanandhayaḥ ।। svaṃ puṅgavīkṛtya surāri-puṅgave । tamālam āliṅgya babhūva niścalā ।। visphūrjitaṃ diśi diśi prakaṭaṃ vṛkāṇām ।
sā netra-catvara-caraṃ ciram ācacāra ।। gātrotkampī manaḥ-kampaḥ sahasā trāsa ucyate । pūrvāpara-vicārotthaṃ bhayaṃ trāsāt pṛthag bhavet ।। cittasya sambhramo yaḥ syād āvego ayaṃ sa cāṣṭadhā ।
priyāpriyānala-marud-varṣotpāta-gajāritaḥ ।। priyotthe pulakaḥ sāntvaṃ cāpalyābhyudgamādayaḥ । apriyotthe tu bhū-pāta-vikrośa-bhramaṇādayaḥ ।। vyatyasta-gati-kampākṣi-mīlanāsrādayo agnije ।
vātaje ajāvṛti-kṣipra-gati-dṛṅ-mārjanādayaḥ ।। vṛṣṭijo dhāvana-cchatra-gātra-saṅkocanādi-kṛt । autpāte mukha-vaivarṇya-vismayo akaṇṭhitādayaḥ ।। gāje palāyanotkampa-trāsa-pṛṣṭhekṣaṇādayaḥ ।
arijo varma-śastrādi-grahāpasaraṇādikṛt ।। prekṣya vṛndāvanāt putram āyāntaṃ prasnuta-stanī । saṅkulā pulakair āsīd ākulā gokuleśvarī ।। śrutvācyutam upāyātaṃ nityaṃ tad-darśanotsukāḥ ।
tat-kathākṣipta-manaso babhūvur jāta-sambhramāḥ ।। iti ghora-dhvani-ghūrṇitā lapantī । tanayaṃ bhrāmyati sambhramād yaśodā ।। mahījayor madhyagam ūrdhva-netrā ।
biddhā vidheyaṃ na vidāñcakāra ।। gavyā gauravataḥ samīkṣya niviḍe tiṣṭhantam antar-vane । dīrghābhiḥ sura-dīrghikāmbu-laharīm arcibhir ācāmati ।। bhāṇḍīroddaṇḍa-śākhā-bhuja-tatiṣu gate tāṇḍavācārya-caryām ।
kṣauṇyām aprekṣya putraṃ vrajapati-gṛhiṇī paśya sambambhramīti ।। atyāsārātivātena paśavo jāta-vepanāḥ । gopā gopyaś ca śītārtā govindaṃ śaraṇaṃ yayuḥ ।। pratidiśam iha goṣṭhe vṛṣṭi-dhārāḥ patanti ।
sphuṭam asi tad-agārān mā sma bhūr niryiyāsuḥ ।। upari ghuranti ca hanta ghoram ulkāḥ । taṭam aṭatīty adhunā kim atra kuryām ।। mudira-sundara he purataḥ karī ।
hṛdayam āvijate pura-yoṣitām ।। gajena duṣṭa-sattvo anyaḥ paśv-ādir upalakṣyate ।। drāg andhaṅkaraṇaḥ surendra-sudṛśāṃ goṣṭhoddhūtaiḥ pāṃśubhiḥ । dragiṣṭhe muhur atra jāgrati bhuje vyagrāsi mātaḥ katham ।।
kvāyaṃ bāla-tamāla-kandala-mṛduḥ kandarpa-kāntaḥ śiśuḥ । hā goṣṭheśvari kīdṛg adya tapasāṃ pākas tavonmīlati ।। tūṇas tūṇo dhanur uta dhanur bhoḥ kṛpāṇī kṛpāṇī । rājñaḥ putrī bata hṛta-hṛtā kāminā vallavena ।।
āvegābhāsa evāyaṃ parāśrayatāpi cet । nāyakotkarṣa-bodhāya tathāpy atra nidarśitaḥ ।। atha unmādaḥ unmādo hṛd-bhramaḥ prauḍhānandāpad-virahādijaḥ ।। atrāṭṭa-hāso naṭanaṃ saṅgītaṃ vyartha-ceṣṭitam ।
pralāpa-dhāvana-krośa-viparīta-kriyādayaḥ ।। manthānakaṃ vidadhatī dadhi-rikta-pātre । devo api ruddha-hṛdayo dhavalaṃ dudoha ।। tarūn api cikitsakā iti viṣauṣadhaṃ pṛcchati ।
vrajendra-gṛhiṇī muhur bhrama-mayīm avasthāṃ gatā ।। vicikyur unmattakavad vanād vanam । bhūteṣu santaṃ puruṣaṃ vanaspatīn ।। unmādaḥ pṛthag ukto ayaṃ vyādhiṣv antarbhavann api ।
yat tatra vipralambhādau vaicitrīṃ kurute parām ।। adhirūḍhe mahā-bhāve mohanatvam upāgate । avasthāntaram āpto asau divyonmāda itīryate ।। duḥkhottha-dhātu-vaiṣamyādy-udbhūtaś citta-viplavaḥ ।
apasmāro atra patanaṃ dhāvanāsphoṭana-bhramāḥ । kampaḥ phena-srutir bāhu-kṣepaṇa-vikrośanādayaḥ ।। āghūrṇate luṭhati kujati līyate ca । beleva vṛṣṇi-tilaka vraja-rāja-rājñī ।।
daityas tasya suhṛttamaḥ pariṇatiṃ ghorāṃ gataḥ kām api । ghūrṇann arṇava-sīmni maṇḍalatayā bhrāmyan na viśrāmyati ।। unmādavad iha vyādhi-viśeṣo apy eṣa varṇitaḥ । parāṃ bhayānakābhāse yat karoti camatkṛtim ।।
doṣodreka-viyogādyair vyādhayo ye jvarādayaḥ । iha tat-prabhavo bhāvo vyādhir ity abhidhīyate । atra stambhaḥ ślathāṅgatva-śvāsottāpa-klamādayaḥ ।। dadhad-uru-jaḍimāni dhmāpitāny aṅgakāni ।
luṭhati dharaṇi-pṛṣṭhe goṣṭha-vāṭī-kuṭumbam ।। moho hṛn-mūḍhatā harṣād viśleṣād bhayatas tathā । viṣādādeś ca tatra syād dehasya patanaṃ bhuvi । śūnyendriyatvaṃ bhramaṇaṃ tathā niśceṣṭatā-mayaḥ ।।
tat-smāritānanta-hṛtākhilendriyaḥ । pratyāha taṃ bhāgavatottamottamam ।। nirīha-nikhilendriyāḥ pratinivṛtta-cid-vṛttayaḥ । vrajāmbuja-dṛśo abhajan kanaka-śālabhañjī-śriyam ।।
sahālībhir lebhe taralita-manā yāmuna-taṭīm । avasthā tastāra sphuṭam atha suṣupteḥ priya-sakhī ।। nirūpayan vānara-varya-ketuḥ । na gāṇḍīvaṃ khaṇḍita-dhīr viveda ।।
kṛṣṇaṃ mahā-baka-grastaṃ dṛṣṭvā rāmādayo arbhakāḥ । babhūvur indriyāṇīva vinā prāṇaṃ vicetasaḥ ।। asyānyatrātma-paryante syāt sarvatraiva mūḍhatā । kṛṣṇa-sphūrti-viśeṣas tu na kadāpy atra līyate ।।
viṣāda-vyādhi-santrāsa-samprahāra-klamādibhiḥ । prāṇa-tyāgo mṛtis tasyām avyaktākṣara-bhāṣaṇam । vivarṇa-gātratā-śvāsa-māndya-hikkādayaḥ kriyāḥ ।। vivṛṇvantaḥ kāye kim api nava-vaivarṇyam abhitaḥ ।
prajalpantaḥ prāṇān jahati mathurāyāṃ sukṛtinaḥ ।। kṣaṇa-vighaṭita-tāmyad-dṛṣṭi-khadyota-dīptiḥ । kṣayam agamad akasmāt pūtanā kāla-rātriḥ ।। prāyo atra maraṇāt pūrvā citta-vṛttir mṛtir matā ।
mṛtir atrānubhāvaḥ syād iti kenacid ucyate । kintu nāyaka-vīryārthaṃ śatrau maraṇam ucyate ।। sāmarthyasyāpi sad-bhāve kriyānunmukhatā hi yā । tṛpti-śramādi-sambhūtā tad-ālasyam udīryate ।।
atrāṅga-bhajo jṛmbhā ca kriyā dveṣo akṣi-mardanam । śayyāsanaika-priyatā tandrā-nidrādayo api ca ।। viprāṇāṃ nas tathā tṛptir āsīd govardhanotsave । nāśīrvāde api gopendra yathā syāt prabhaviṣṇutā ।।
prītaye mama vidhāya niyuddham । nāhavāya sahasāhvayatām amum ।। jāḍyam apratipattiḥ syād iṣṭāniṣṭha-śrutīkṣaṇaiḥ । virahādyaiś ca tan-mohāt pūrvāvasthāparāpi ca ।
atrānimiṣatā tūṣṇīm-bhāva-vismaraṇādayaḥ ।। pīyūṣam uttabhita-karṇa-puṭaiḥ pibantyaḥ । govindam ātmani dṛśāśru-kulāḥ spṛśantyaḥ ।। keśavasya giram arpita-śalyām ।
lakṣmaṇā kṣaṇam avartata tūṣṇīm ।। govindaṃ gṛham ānīya deva-deveśam ādṛtaḥ । pūjāyāṃ nāvidat kṛtyaṃ pramādopahato nṛpaḥ ।। yāvad ālakṣyate ketur yāvad reṇū rathasya ca ।
anuprasthāpitātmāno lekhyānīvopalakṣitāḥ ।। alaṅkṛtibhir ujjhitā bhuvi niviśya tatra sthitāḥ । sphuranti khala-devala-dvija-gṛhe surārcā iva ।। navīna-saṅgamākārya-stavāvajñādinā kṛtā ।
adhṛṣṭatā bhaved vrīḍā tatra maunaṃ vicintanam । avaguṇṭhana-bhū-lekhau tathādhomukhatādayaḥ ।। premāndhā vara-vapur arpaṇaṃ sakhi । vikrīte kariṇi kim aṅkuśe vivādaḥ ।।
vadanaṃ ca trapayā śacī-pate । katham agre mukham īkṣayiṣyasi ।। bhūri-sādguṇya-bhāreṇa stūyamānasya śauriṇā । uddhavasya vyarociṣṭa namrī-bhūtaṃ tadā śiraḥ ।।
vasanta-kusumaiś citraṃ sadā raivatakaṃ girim । priyā bhūtvā'priyā bhūtā kathaṃ drakṣyāmi taṃ punaḥ ।। atha avahitthā avahitthākāra-guptir bhaved bhāvena kenacit ।। atrāṅgādeḥ parābhyūha-sthānasya parigūhanam ।
anyatrekṣā vṛthā-ceṣṭā vāg-bhaṅgīty-ādayaḥ kriyāḥ ।। tathā coktam anubhāva-pidhānārtho avahitthaṃ bhāva ucyate ।। sahāsa-līlekṣaṇa-vibhrama-bhruvā । saṃstutya īṣat kupitā babhāṣire ।।
nīte praṇīta-mahasā madhusūdanena । sauśīlyataḥ kila na ko api vidāmbabhūva ।। duranta-bhāvāḥ parirebhire patim । vilajjatīnāṃ bhṛgu-varya vaiklavāt ।।
kā vṛṣasyati taṃ goṣṭha-bhujaṅgaṃ kula-pālikā । dūti yatra smṛte mūrtir bhītyā romāñcitā mama ।। gūḍhā gābhīrya-sampadbhir mano-gahvara-garbhagā । prauḍhāpy asyā ratiḥ kṛṣṇe durvitarkā parair abhūt ।।
smerāsyaiḥ sphuṭam iha narma nirmimāṇe । yatnena smitam atha saṃvavāra patrī ।। hetuḥ kaścid bhavet kaścid gopyaḥ kaścana gopanaḥ । iti bhāva-trayasyātra viniyogaḥ samīkṣyate ।।
hetutvaṃ gopanatvaṃ ca gopyatvaṃ cātra sambhavet । prāyeṇa sarva-bhāvānām ekaśo anekaśo api ca ।। yā syāt pūrvānubhūtārtha-pratītiḥ sadṛśekṣayā । dṛḍhābhyāsādinā vāpi sā smṛtiḥ parikīrtitā ।
bhaved atra śiraḥ-kampo bhrū-vikṣepādayo api ca ।। vilokya śyāmam ambhodam ambhoruha-vilocanā । smāraṃ smāraṃ mukunda tvāṃ smāraṃ vikramam anvabhūt ।। praṇidhāna-vidhim idānīm akurvato api pramādato hṛdi me ।
hari-pada-paṅkaja-yugalaṃ kvacit kadācit parisphurati ।। vimarṣāt saṃśayādeś ca vitarkas tūha ucyate । eṣa bhrū-ksepaṇa-śiro aṅguli-sañcālanādi-kṛt ।। na kaṇṭhe yan mālyaṃ kalayasi purastāt kṛtam api ।
sphuṭaṃ rādhā-netra-bhramara-vara vīryonnatir iyam ।। payodaḥ kiṃ vāmaṃ na yad iha niraṅko himakaraḥ । dhruvaṃ mūrdhany adrer vidhu-mukhi mukundo viharati ।। vinirṇayānta evāyaṃ tarka ity ūcire pare ।।
dhyānaṃ cintā bhaved iṣṭānāpty-aniṣṭāpti-nirmitam । śvāsādhomukha-bhūlekha-vaivarṇyān nidratā iha । vilāpottāpa-kṛśatā-bāṣpa-dainyādayo api ca ।। bimbādharāṇi caraṇena likhantyaḥ ।
tasthur mṛjantya uru-duḥkha-bharāḥ sma tūṣṇīm ।। katham api cirād adhyāsīnā praghāṇam aghāntaka । kim ahaha gṛhaṃ krīḍā-lubdha tvayādya visasmare ।। glapaya na mukha-padmaṃ tapta-bāṣpa-plavena ।
tava sutam aham eva drāk parāvartayāmi ।। atha matiḥ śāstrādīnāṃ vicārottham artha-nirdhāraṇaṃ matiḥ ।। atra kartavya-karaṇaṃ saṃśaya-bhramayoś chidā । upadeśaś ca śiṣyāṇām ūhāpohādayo api ca ।।
tāṃ tām eva hi devatāṃ paramikāṃ jalpantu kalpāvadhi । vyāpāreṣu vivecana-vyatikaraṃ nīteṣu niścīyate ।। ātmātmadaś ca jagatām iti me vṛto asi । dhvastāśiṣo abja-bhavanākapatīn kuto anye ।।
dhṛtiḥ syāt pūrṇatā jñāna-duḥkhābhāvottamāptibhiḥ । aprāptātīta-naṣṭārthān abhisaṃśocanādi-kṛt ।। aśnīmahi vayaṃ bhikṣām āśāvāso vasīmahi । śayīmahi mahī-pṛṣṭhe kurvīmahi kim īśvaraiḥ ।।
gāvaś ca dhāvanti paraḥ-parārdhāḥ । tṛptir mamābhūd gṛhamedhi-saukhye ।। hari-līlā-sudhā-sindhos taṭam apy adhitiṣṭhataḥ । mano mama catur-vargaṃ tṛṇāyāpi na manyate ।।
abhīṣṭekṣaṇa-lābhādi-jātā cetaḥ-prasannatā । harṣaḥ syād iha romāñcaḥ svedo aśru mukha-phullatā । āvegonmāda-jaḍatās tathā mohādayo api ca ।। tau dṛṣṭvā vikasad-vaktra-sarojaḥ sa mahāmatiḥ ।
pulakāñcita-sarvāṅgas tadākrūro abhavan mune ।। tatraikāṃsagataṃ bāhuṃ kṛṣṇasyotpalasaurabham । candanāliptam āghrāya hṛṣṭaromā cucumba ha ।। kālākṣamatvam autsukyam iṣṭekṣāpti-spṛhādibhiḥ ।
mukha-śoṣa-tvarā-cintā-niḥśvāsa-sthiratādikṛt ।। autsukya-viślathita-keśa-dukūla-baddhāḥ । draṣṭuṃ yayur yuvatayaḥ sma narendra-mārge ।। druta-gati harim ārāt prāpya kuñje smitākṣī ।
snapayati nija-dāsye rādhikā māṃ kadā nu ।। drāghayaty aghaharāgrataḥ kathām । gahvaraṃ druta-pada-kramaṃ yayau ।। aparādha-durukty-ādi- jātaṃ caṇḍatvam ugratā ।
vadha-bandha-śiraḥ-kampa-bhartsanottāḍanādi-kṛt ।। viracayati mad-īśe kilbiṣaṃ kāliyo api । sapadi danuja-hantuḥ kintu roṣād bibhemi ।। na hi danuja-ripor yaḥ prauṅdha-kīrter visoḍhum ।
śirasi pṛthuni tasya nyasyate savya-pādaḥ ।। khalāḥ kuru-kulādhamāḥ prabhum ajāṇḍa-koṭiṣv amī । haṭhād iha kaṭākṣayanty akhila-vandyam apy acyutam ।। atha amarṣaḥ adhikṣepāpamānādeḥ syād amarṣo asahiṣṇutā ।।
tatra svedaḥ śiraḥkampo vivarṇatvaṃ vicintanam । upāyānveṣaṇākrośa-vaimukhyottāḍanādayaḥ ।। kalyāṇī me nivasati vadhūḥ paśya pārśve navoḍhā । niḥśaṅkas tvaṃ bhramasi bhavitā nākulatvaṃ kuto me ।।
jane bhavati mad-vidhe paribhavo hi nātaḥ paraḥ । varāpi yad ayogyayā sphuṭam adūṣi tārākhyayā ।। ativilaṅghya te anty acyutāgatāḥ । kitava yoṣitaḥ kas tyajen niśi ।।
dveṣaḥ parodaye asūyānya-saubhāgya-guṇādibhiḥ । tatrerṣyānādarākṣepā doṣāropo guṇeṣv api । apavṛttis tiro-vīkṣā bhruvor bhaṅguratādayaḥ ।। kṛṣṇa-svahasta-likhitā nava-mañjarīti ।
vairī na ced bhavati vepathur antarāyaḥ ।। tasyā amūni naḥ kṣobhaṃ kurvanty uccaiḥ padāni yat । yaikāpahṛtya gopīnāṃ raho bhuṅkte acyutādharam ।। svayaṃ parājayaṃ prāptān kṛṣṇa-pakṣān vijitya naḥ ।
baliṣṭhā bala-pakṣāś ced durbalāḥ ke tataḥ kṣitau ।। rāga-dveṣādibhiś citta-lāghavaṃ cāpalaṃ bhavet । tatrāvicāra-pāruṣya-svacchandācaraṇādayaḥ ।। guptaḥ sametya pṛtanā-patibhiḥ parītaḥ ।
māṃ rākṣasena vidhinodvaha vīrya-śulkām ।। vaṃśī-pūreṇa kālindyāḥ sindhuṃ vindatu vāhitā । guror api puro nīvīṃ yā bhraṃśayati subhruvām ।। cintālasya-nisarga-klamādibhiś citta-mīlanaṃ nidrā ।
tatrāṅga-bhaṅga-jṛmbhā-jāḍya-śvāsākṣi-mīlanāni syuḥ ।। lohitāyati mārtaṇḍe veṇu-dhvanim aśṛṇvatī । cintayākrānta-hṛdayā nidadrau nanda-gehinī ।। dāmodarasya bandhana-karmabhir atiniḥsahāṅga-latikeyam ।
dara-vighūrṇitottamāṅgā kṛtāṅga-bhaṅgā vrajeśvarī sphurati ।। parihṛta-gṛha-vāstu-dvāra-bandhānubaddhāḥ । sukham avicalad-aṅgāḥ śerate paśya gopāḥ ।। saṅkrānta-dhātu-citrā suratānte sā nitānta-tāntā'dya ।
vakṣasi nikṣiptāṅgī harer viśākhā yayau nidrām ।। yuktāsya sphūrti-mātreṇa nirviśeṣeṇa kenacit । hṛn-mīlanāt puro avasthā nidrā bhakteṣu kathyate ।। suptir nidrā-vibhāvā syān nānārthānubhavātmikā ।
indriyoparati-śvāsa-netra-saṃmīlanādi-kṛt ।। darpaḥ sarpa-pates tad asya tarasā nirdhūyatām uddhūraḥ । niḥśvāsena darottaraṅgad-udaraṃ nidrāṃ gato lāṅgalī ।। atha bodhaḥ avidyā-moha-nidrāder dhvaṃsodbodhaḥ prabuddhatā ।।
avidyā-dhvaṃsato bodho vidyodaya-puraḥsaraḥ । aśeṣa-kleśa-viśrānti-svarūpāvagamādi-kṛt ।। buddhvā sadyaḥ satya-vijñāna-rūpam । sāndrānandākāram anveṣayāmi ।।
bodho moha-kṣayāc chabda-gandha-sparśa-rasair hareḥ । dṛg-unmīlana-romāñca-dharotthānādi-kṛd bhavet ।। kavalitendriya-vṛttir abhūd iyam । lalitayodamimīlad ihākṣiṇī ।।
vana-bhuvi śavalāṅgī śānta-niḥśvāsa-vṛttiḥ । pulakita-tanur eṣā pāṃśu-puñjād udasthāt ।। viśīryantyāḥ saura-pulina-vanam ālokya mama yaḥ । drutaṃ mūrcchām antaḥ sakhi sukha-mayīṃ pallavayati ।।
srastāṅga-yaṣṭir ajaniṣṭa sakhī visaṃjñā । nyastaṃ mayā mukha-puṭe pulakojjvalāsīt ।। bodho nidrākṣayāt svapna-nidrā-pūrti-svanādibhiḥ । tatrākṣi-mardanaṃ śayyā-mokṣo aṅga-valanādayaḥ ।।
na yāvad-vṛddhāyai sphuṭam abhidadhe tvac-caṭulatām । puro dṛṣṭvā gaurī namita-mukha-bimbā muhur abhūt ।। dūtī cāgāt tad-āgāraṃ jajāgāra ca rādhikā । tūrṇaṃ puṇyavatīnāṃ hi tanoti phalam udyamaḥ ।।
dūrād vidrāvayan nidrā-marālīr gopa-subhruvām । sāraṅga-raṅgadaṃ reje veṇu-vārida-garjitam ।। iti bhāvās trayas-triṃśat kathitā vyabhicāriṇaḥ । śreṣṭha-madhya-kaniṣṭheṣu varṇanīyā yathocitam ।।
mātsaryodvega-dambherṣyā viveko nirṇayas tathā । klaibyaṃ kṣamā ca kutukam utkaṇṭhā vinayo api ca ।। saṃśayo dhārṣṭyam ity ādyā bhāvā ye syuḥ pare api ca । ukteṣv antarbhavantīti na pṛthaktvena darśitāḥ ।।
asūyāyāṃ tu mātsaryaṃ trāse apy udvega eva tu । dambhas tathāvahitthāyām īrṣyāmarṣe matāv ubhau । viveko nirṇayaś cemau dainye klaibyaṃ kṣamā dhṛtau ।। autsukye kutukotkaṇṭhe lajjāyāṃ vinayas tathā ।
saṃśayo antarbhavet tarke tathā dhārṣṭyaṃ ca cāpale ।। eṣāṃ sañcāri-bhāvānāṃ madhye kaścana kasyacit । vibhāvaś cānubhāvaś ca bhaved eva parasparam ।। nirvede tu yatherṣyāyā bhaved atra vibhāvatā ।
asūyāyāṃ punas tasyā vyaktam uktānubhāvatā ।। autsukyaṃ prati cintāyāḥ kathitātrānubhāvatā । nidrāṃ prati vibhāvatvam evaṃ jñeyaḥ pare apy amī ।। eṣāṃ ca sāttvikānāṃ ca tathā nānā-kriyā-tateḥ ।
kārya-kāraṇa-bhāvas tu jñeyaḥ prāyeṇa lokataḥ ।। nindāyās tu vibhāvatvaṃ vaivarṇyāmarṣayor matam । asūyāyāṃ punas tasyāḥ kathitaivānubhāvatā ।। prahārasya vibhāvatvaṃ saṃmoha-pralayau prati ।
augryaṃ pratyanubhāvatvam evaṃ jñeyāḥ pare api ca ।। trāsa-nidrā-śramālasya-mada-bhid-bodha-varjinām । sañcāriṇām iha kvāpi bhaved raty-anubhāvatā ।। sākṣād-rater na sambandhaḥ ṣaḍbhis trāsādibhiḥ saha ।
syāt parasparayā kintu līlānuguṇatākṛte ।। vitarka-mati-nirveda-dhṛtīnāṃ smṛti-harṣayoḥ । bodha-bhid-dainya-suptīnāṃ kvacid rati-vibhāvatā ।। paratantrāḥ svatantrāś cety uktāḥ sañcāriṇo dvidhā ।।
tatra paratantrāḥ varāvaratayā proktāḥ paratantrā api dvidhā ।। tatra varaḥ sākṣād vyavahitaś ceti varo apy eṣa dvidhoditaḥ ।। tatra sākṣāt mukhyām eva ratiṃ puṣṇan sākṣād ity abhidhīyate ।। tanoti me nāma niśamya yasya ।
vyarthena kiṃ hanta dṛśor dvayena ।। atha vyavahitaḥ puṣṇāti yo ratiṃ gauṇīṃ sa vyavahito mataḥ ।। dhig astu me bhuja-dvandvaṃ bhīmasya parighopamam । mādhavākṣepiṇaṃ duṣṭaṃ yat pinaṣṭi na cedipam ।।
nirvedaḥ krodha-vaśyatvād ayaṃ vyavahito rateḥ ।। atha avaraḥ rasa-dvayasyāpy aṅgatvam agacchann avaro mataḥ ।। jaganti daṃṣṭrāsphuṭad-uttamāṅgaiḥ । na svaṃ viśuṣyan smarati sma jiṣṇuḥ ।।
ghora-kriyādy-anubhāvād ācchādya sahajāṃ ratim । durvarāvirabhūd bhītir moho ayaṃ bhī-vaśas tataḥ ।। sadaiva pāratantrye api kvacid eṣāṃ svatantratā । bhūpāla-sevakasyeva pravṛttasya kara-grahe ।।
bhāvajñai rati-śūnyaś ca raty-anusparśanas tathā । rati-gandhiś ca te tredhā svatantrāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।। tatra rati-śūnyaḥ janeṣu rati-śūnyeṣu rati-śūnyo bhaved asau ।। dhig janma nas trivṛd-vidyāṃ dhig vrataṃ dhig bahujñatām ।
dhik kulaṃ dhik kriyā-dīkṣāṃ vimukhā ye tv adhokṣaje ।। atra svatantro nirvedaḥ । yaḥ svato rati-gandhena vihīno api prasaṅgataḥ । paścād ratiṃ spṛśed eṣa raty-anusparśano mataḥ ।।
gariṣṭhāriṣṭa-ṭaṅkārair vidhurā vadhirāyitā । hā kṛṣṇa pāhi pāhīti cukrośābhīra-bālikā ।। atra trāsaḥ । atha rati-gandhiḥ yaḥ svātantrye api tad-gandhaṃ rati-gandhir vyanakti saḥ ।।
saṅgopanāya na hi naptri vidhehi yatnam । rādhāvaguṇṭhita-mukhī tarasā tadāsīt ।। atra lajjā । ābhāsaḥ punar eteṣām asthāne vṛttito bhavet ।
prātikūlyam anaucityam asthānatvaṃ dvidhoditam ।। tatra prātikūlyam vipakṣe vṛttir eteṣāṃ prātikūlyam itīryate ।। hanti me hanta mama jīvita-nirviśeṣam । durjīvitena hata-kaṃsa-narādhipasya ।।
atra nirvedasyābhāsaḥ । goṣṭha-bhūbhṛd api loṣṭra-sodaraḥ । yena mūrkha jagadīśateryate ।। atrāsūyāyāḥ ।
asatyatvam ayogyatvam anaucityaṃ dvidhā bhavet । aprāṇini bhaved ādyaḥ tiryag-ādiṣu cāntimam ।। kṛṣṇena hanta mama tasya dhig astu janma । mṛdnan kariṣyati hariś caritārthatāṃ te ।।
atra nirvedasya । adhirohatu kaḥ pakṣī kakṣām aparo mamādya medhyasya । hitvāpi tārkṣya-paksaṃ bhajate pakṣaṃ harir yasya ।। atra garvasya ।
vahamāneṣv api sadā jñāna-vijñāna-mādhurīm । kadambādiṣu sāmānya-dṛṣṭy-ābhāsatvam ucyate ।। bhāvānāṃ kvacid utpatti-sandhi-śāvalya-śāntayaḥ । daśāś catasra etāsām utpattis tv iha sambhavaḥ ।।
lohitāyati niśamya yaśodā । prasrava-stimita-kañculikāsīt ।। atra harṣotpattiḥ । uṣasi sakhi tavālī mekhalā paśya bhāti ।
dṛśam anṛju kirantī rādhikā vaḥ punātu ।। atrāsūyotpattiḥ । atha sandhiḥ sarūpayor bhinnayor vā sandhiḥ syād bhāvayor yutiḥ ।। tatra sarūpayoḥ sandhiḥ sandhiḥ sarūpayos tatra bhinna-hetūtthayor mataḥ ।।
gokuleśa-gṛhiṇī patitāṅgīm । hanta niścala-tanuḥ kṣaṇam āsīt ।। atrāniṣṭeṣṭa-saṃvīkṣākṛtayor jāḍyayor yutiḥ । atha bhinnayoḥ bhinnayor hetunaikena bhinnenāpy upajātayoḥ ।।
durvāracāpalo ayaṃ dhāvann antar bahiś ca goṣṭhasya । śiśur akutaścid bhītir dhinoti hṛdayaṃ dunoti ca me ।। tatra harṣa-śaṅkayoḥ । sutam utphulla-vilocanaṃ puraḥ ।
himam uṣṇaṃ ca jalaṃ dṛśor dadhe ।। atra harṣa-viṣādayoḥ sandhiḥ । ekena jāyamānānām anekena ca hetunā । bahūnām api bhāvānāṃ sandhiḥ sphuṭam avekṣyate ।।
haṭhād antaḥ-smerāṃ taralatara-tārojjvala-kalām । dṛśaṃ nyasyanty asmin jayati vṛṣabhānoḥ kula-maṇiḥ ।। atra harṣautsukya-garvāmarṣāsūyānāṃ sandhiḥ । nikaṭa-bhuvi tathāgre tarka-bhāk smera-padmām ।
mahasi vinata-vakra-prasphura-mlāna-vaktrā ।। atra lajjāmarṣa-harṣa-viṣādānāṃ sandhiḥ । atha śāvalyam śavalatvaṃ tu bhāvānāṃ saṃmardaḥ syāt parasparam ।। ātiṣṭheyaṃ tam eva drutam atha śaraṇaṃ kuryur etan na vīrāḥ ।
kuryām adyaiva gatvā vraja-bhuvi kadanaṃ hā tataḥ kampate dhīḥ ।। atra garva-viṣāda-dainya-mati-smṛti-śaṅkāmarṣa-trāsānāṃ śāvalyam । vidyeyaṃ mama kiṅkarī-kṛta-nṛpā kālas tu sarvaṅkaraḥ । sadmany eva hariṃ bhajeya hṛdayaṃ vṛndāṭavī karṣati ।।
atra nirveda-garva-śaṅkā-dhṛti-viṣāda-maty-autsukyānāṃ śāvalyam । atha śāntiḥ atyārūḍhasya bhāvasya vilayaḥ śāntir ucyate ।। tam aghaharaṃ gahane gaveṣayantaḥ । vraja-śiśavaḥ pulakojjvalā babhūvuḥ ।।
atra viṣāda-śāntiḥ । śabdārtha-rasa-vaicitrī vāci kācana nāsti me । yathā-kathañcid evoktaṃ bhāvodāharaṇaṃ param ।। trayastriṃśad ime aṣṭau ca vakṣyante sthāyinaś ca ye ।
mukhya-bhāvābhidhās tv eka-catvāriṃśad amī smṛtāḥ ।। śarīrendriya-vargasya vikāraṇāṃ vidhāyakāḥ । bhāvāvirbhāva-janitāś citta-vṛttaya īritāḥ ।। kvacit svābhāviko bhāvaḥ kaścid āgantukaḥ kvacit ।
yas tu svābhāviko bhāvaḥ sa vyāpyāntar-bahiḥ-sthitaḥ ।। mañjiṣṭhādye yathā dravye rāgas tan-maya īkṣyate । atra syān nāma-mātreṇa vibhāvasya vibhāvatā ।। etena sahajenaiva bhāvenānugatā ratiḥ ।
eka-rūpāpi yā bhakter vividhā pratibhāty asau ।। āgantukas tu yo bhāvaḥ paṭādau raktimeva saḥ । tais tair vibhāvair evāyaṃ dhīyate dīpyate api ca ।। vibhāvanādi-vaiśiṣṭyād bhaktānāṃ bhedatas tathā ।
prāyeṇa sarva-bhāvānāṃ vaiśiṣṭyam upajāyate ।। vividhānāṃ tu bhaktānāṃ vaiśiṣṭyād vividhaṃ manaḥ । mano anusārād bhāvānāṃ tāratamyaṃ kilodaye ।। citte gariṣṭhe gambhīre mahiṣṭhe karkaśādike ।
samyag-unmīlitāś cāmī na lakṣyante sphuṭaṃ janaiḥ ।। citte laghiṣṭhe cottāne kṣodiṣṭhe komalādike । manāg-unmīlitāś cāmī lakṣyante bahir ulbaṇāḥ ।। gariṣṭhaṃ svarṇa-piṇḍābhaṃ laghiṣṭhaṃ tula-piṇḍavat ।
citta-yugme atra vijñayā bhāvasya pavanopamā ।। gambhīraṃ sindhuvac cittam uttānaṃ palvalādivat । citta-dvaye atra bhāvasya mahādri-śikharopamā ।। pattanābhaṃ mahiṣṭhaṃ syāt kṣodiṣṭhaṃ tu kuṭiravat ।
citta-yugme atra bhāvasya dīpenebhena vopamā ।। karkaśaṃ trividhaṃ proktaṃ vajraṃ svarṇaṃ tathā jatu । citta-traye atra bhāvasya jñeyā vaiśvānaropamā ।। atyanta-kaṭhinaṃ vajram akutaścana mārdavam ।
īdṛśaṃ tāpasādīnāṃ cittaṃ tāvad avekṣyate ।। svarṇaṃ dravati bhāvāgnes tāpenātigarīyasā । jatu dravatvam āyāti tāpa-leśena sarvataḥ ।। komalaṃ ca tridhaivoktaṃ madanaṃ navanītakam ।
amṛtaṃ ceti bhāvo atra prāyaḥ sūryātapāyate ।। draved atrādya-yugalam ātapena yathāyatham । dravībhūtaṃ svabhāvena sarvadaivāmṛtaṃ bhavet । govinda-preṣṭha-varyāṇāṃ cittaṃ syād amṛtaṃ kila ।।
kṛṣṇa-bhakti-viśeṣasya gariṣṭhatvādibhir guṇaiḥ । samavetaṃ sadāmībhir dvitrair api mano bhavet ।। kintu suṣṭhu mahiṣṭhatvaṃ bhāvo bāḍham upāgataḥ । sarva-prakāram evedaṃ cittaṃ vikṣobhayaty alam ।।
ahāryāṃ maryādāṃ dadhad api harer āspadam api । vikāraṃ na sphāraṃ jala-nidhir ivendau prabhavati ।। iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhau dakṣiṇa-vibhāge bhakti-rasa-sāmānya-nirūpaṇe vyabhicāri-laharī caturthī ।। aviruddhān viruddhāṃś ca bhāvān yo vaśatāṃ nayan ।
su-rājeva virājeta sa sthāyī bhāva ucyate ।। sthāyī bhāvo atra sa proktaḥ śrī-kṛṣṇa-viṣayā ratiḥ । mukhyā gauṇī ca sā dvedhā rasa-jñaiḥ parikīrtitā ।। śuddha-sattva-viśeṣātmā ratir mukhyeti kīrtitā ।
mukhyāpi dvi-vidhā svārthā parārthā ceti kīrtyate ।। aviruddhaiḥ sphuṭaṃ bhāvaiḥ puṣṇāty ātmānam eva yā । viruddhair duḥkha-glāniḥ sā svārthā kathitā ratiḥ ।। aviruddhaṃ viruddhaṃ ca saṅkucantī svayaṃ ratiḥ ।
yā bhāvam anugṛhṇāti sā parārthā nigadyate ।। śuddhā prītis tathā sakhyaṃ vātsalyaṃ priyatety asau । svaparārthyaiva sā mukhyā punaḥ pañca-vidhā bhavet ।। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ pātra-vaiśiṣṭyād ratir eṣopagacchati ।
yathārkaḥ pratibimbātmā sphaṭikādiṣu vastuṣu ।। sāmānyāsau tathā svacchā śāntiś cety ādimā tridhā । eṣāṅga-kampatā-netrāmīlanonmīlanādi-kṛt ।। kañcid viśeṣam aprāptā sādhāraṇa-janasya yā ।
bālikadaiś ca kṛṣṇe syāt sāmānyā sā ratir matā ।। asmin mathurā-vīthyām udayati madhure virocane purataḥ । kathasva sakhe mradimānaṃ mānasa-madanaṃ kim eti mama ।। tri-varṣā bālikā seyaṃ varṣīyasi samīkṣyatām ।
yā puraḥ kṛṣṇam ālokya huṅkurvaty abhidhāvati ।। tat-tat-sādhanato nānā-vidha-bhakti-prasaṅgataḥ । sādhākānāṃ tu vaividhyaṃ yāntī svacchā ratir matā ।। yadā yādṛśī bhakte syād āsaktis tādṛśaṃ tadā ।
rūpaṃ sphaṭikavad dhatte svacchāsau tena kīrtitā ।। kvacit tanaya ity avan kvacana kānta ity ullasan । abhūd vividha-sevayā vividha-vṛttir āryo dvijaḥ ।। anācānta-dhiyāṃ tat-tad-bhāva-niṣṭhā sukhārṇave ।
āryāṇām atiśuddhānāṃ prāyaḥ svacchā ratir bhavet ।। atha śāntiḥ mānase nirvikalpatvaṃ śama ity abhidhīyate ।। vihāya viṣayonmukhyaṃ nijānanda-sthitir yataḥ । ātmanaḥ kathyate so atra svabhāvaḥ śama ity asau ।।
prāyaḥ śama-pradhānānāṃ mamatā-gandha-varjitā । paramātmatayā kṛṣṇe jātā śānta-ratir matā ।। devarṣi-vīṇayā pīte hari-līlā-mahotsave । sanakasya tanau kampo brahmānubhavino apy abhūt ।।
apara-vargānubhavaṃ kilāvadhīrya । paramaṃ brahma didṛkṣate mano me ।। agrato vakṣyamāṇais tu svādaiḥ prīty-ādi-saṃśrayaiḥ । rater asyā asamparkād iyaṃ śuddheti bhaṇyate ।।
atha bheda-trayī hṛdyā rateḥ prīty-ādir īryate । gāḍhānukūlatotpannā mamatvena sadāśritā ।। kṛṣṇa-bhakteṣv anugrāhya-sakhi-pūjyeṣv anukramāt । tri-vidheṣu trayī prītiḥ sakhyaṃ vatsalatety asau ।।
atra netrādi-phullatva-jṛmbhaṇodghūrṇanādayaḥ । kevalā saṅkulā ceti dvi-vidheyaṃ rati-trayī ।। raty-antarasya gandhena varjitā kevalā bhavet । vrajānuge rasālādau śrīdāmādau vayasyake ।
gurau ca vrajanāthādau krameṇaiva sphuraty asau ।। eṣāṃ dvayos trayāṇāṃ vā sannipātas tu saṅkulā । udbhavādau ca bhīmādau mathurādau krameṇa sā । yasyādhikyaṃ bhaved yatra sa tena vyapadiśyate ।।
svasmād bhavanti ye nyūnās te anugrāhyā harer matāḥ । ārādhyatvātmikā teṣāṃ ratiḥ prītir itīritā ।। tatrāsakti-kṛd anyatra prīti-saṃhāriṇī hy asau ।। narake vā narakāntaka prakāmam ।
caraṇau te maraṇe api cintayāmi ।। ye syus tulyā mukundasya te sakhāyaḥ satāṃ matāḥ । sāmyād viśrambha-rūpaiṣāṃ ratiḥ sakhyam ihocyate । parihāsa-prahāsādi-kāriṇīyam ayantraṇā ।।
nimeṣa-viśleṣa-vidīrṇa-mānasāḥ । dūrād ahaṃpūrvikayādya remire ।। dāmodara tvam iha darpa-dhurā daridraḥ । devyai hriye trayam adāyi jvalāñjalīnām ।।
guravo ye harer asya te pūjyā iti viśrutāḥ । anugraha-mayī teṣāṃ ratir vātsalyam ucyate । idaṃ lālana-bhavyāśīś cibuka-sparśanādi-kṛt ।। kaṃsasya kiṅkara-gaṇair girito apy udagraiḥ ।
bālaḥ prayāty avirataṃ bata kiṃ karomi ।। cibukāgre dadhatī dayārdra-dhīḥ । sthiti-bhājaṃ vraja-rāja-gehinī ।। mitho harer mṛgākṣyāś ca sambhogasyādi-kāraṇam ।
madhurāpara-paryāyā priyatākhyoditā ratiḥ । asyāṃ kaṭākṣa-bhrū-kṣepa-priya-vāṇī-smitādayaḥ ।। ciram utkuṇṭhita-manaso rādhā-mura-vairiṇoḥ ko api । nibhṛta-nirīkṣaṇa-janmā pratyāśā-pallavo jayati ।।
yathottaram asau svāda-viśeṣollāsa-mayy api । ratir vāsanayā svādvī bhāsate kāpi kasyacit ।। vibhāvotkarṣajo bhāva-viśeṣo yo anugṛhyate । saṅkucantyā svayaṃ ratyā sa gauṇī ratir ucyate ।।
hāso vismaya utsāhaḥ śokaḥ krodho bhayaṃ tathā । jugupsā cety asau bhāva-viśeṣaḥ saptadhoditaḥ ।। api kṛṣṇa-vibhāvatvam ādya-ṣaṭkasya sambhavet । syād dehādi-vibhāvatvaṃ saptamyās tu rater vaśāt ।।
hāsādāv atra bhinne api śuddha-sattva-viśeṣataḥ । parārthāyā rater yogād rati-śabdaḥ prayujyate ।। hāsottarā ratir yā syāt sā hāsa-ratir ucyate । evaṃ vismaya-raty-ādyā vijñeyā ratayaś ca ṣaṭ ।।
kañcit kālaṃ kvacid bhakte hāsādyāḥ sthāyitām amī । ratyā cāru-kṛtā yānti tal-līlādy-anusārataḥ ।। tasmād aniyatādhārāḥ sapta sāmayikā ime । sahajā api līyante baliṣṭhena tiraskṛtāḥ ।।
kāpy avyabhicarantī sā svādhārān sva-svarūpataḥ । ratir ātyantika-sthāyī bhāvo bhakta-jane a khile । syur etasyā vinā-bhāvād bhāvāḥ sarve nirarthakāḥ ।। vipakṣādiṣu yānto api krodhādyāḥ sthāyitāṃ sadā ।
labhante rati-śūnyatvān na bhakti-rasa-yogyatām ।। aviruddhair api spṛṣṭā bhāvaiḥ sañcāriṇo akhilāḥ । nirvedādyā vilīyante nārhanti sthāyitāṃ tataḥ ।। ity ato mati-garvādi-bhāvānāṃ ghaṭate na hi ।
sthāyitā kaiścid iṣṭāpi pramāṇaṃ tatra tad-vidaḥ ।। sapta hāsādayas tv ete tais tair nītāḥ supuṣṭatām । bhakteṣu sthāyitāṃ yānto rucir ebhyo vitanvate ।। aṣṭānām eva bhāvānāṃ saṃskārādhāyitā matā ।
tat-tiraskṛta-saṃskārāḥ pare na sthāyitocitāḥ ।। ceto-vikāso hāsaḥ syād vāg-veṣehādi-vaikṛtāt । sa dṛg-vikāsana-sauṣṭha-kapola-spandanādikṛt ।। kṛṣṇa-sambandhi-ceṣṭotthaḥ svayaṃ saṅkucad-ātmanā ।
pratyānugṛhyamāṇo ayaṃ hāso hāsa-ratir bhavet ।। sakhī tava nirargalā tad api me mukhaṃ jighrati । vadaty ajani dūtikā hasita-rodhane na kṣamā ।। lokottarārtha-vīkṣāder vismayaś citta-vistṛtiḥ ।
atra syur netra-vistāra-sādhūkti-pulakādayaḥ । pūrvokta-rītyā niṣpannaḥ sa vismaya-ratir bhavet ।। lasac-chrīvatsāṅkaḥ pṛthu-bhuja-catuṣkair dhṛta-ruciḥ । para-brahmollāsān vahati kim idaṃ hanta kim idam ।।
stheyasī sādhubhiḥ ślāghya-phale yuddhādi-karmaṇi । satvarā mānasāsaktir utsāha iti kīrtyate ।। kālānavekṣaṇaṃ tatra dhairya-tyāgodyamādayaḥ । siddhaḥ pūrvokta-vidhinā sa utsāha ratir bhavet ।।
nikvāṇair iha mukharī-kṛtāmbarāyām । śrīdāmā parikaram udbhaṭaṃ babandha ।। śokas tv iṣṭa-viyogādyaiś citta-kleśa-bharaḥ smṛtaḥ । vilāpa-pāta-niḥśvāsa-mukha-śoṣa-bhramādi-kṛt ।
pūrvokta-vidhinaivāyaṃ siddhaḥ śoka-ratir bhavet ।। bhṛśam anutapta-dhiyo aśru-pūrṇa-mukhyaḥ । pavana upārata-pāṃśu-varṣa-vege ।। tanayaṃ prāṇa-sahasra-vallabham ।
dhig imāṃ martya-tanoḥ kaṭhoratām ।। prātikūlyādibhiś citta-jvalanaṃ krodha īryate । pāruṣya-bhrū-kuṭī-netra-lauhityādi-vikāra-kṛt ।। evaṃ pūrvoktavat-siddhaṃ viduḥ krodha-ratiṃ budhāḥ ।
dvidhāsau kṛṣṇa-tad-vairi-bhāvatvena kīrtitā ।। rādhikā-maṇi-saraṃ paricitya । bhaṅga-bhīmatara-dṛṣṭir dadarśa ।। harim abhyudyati tīvra-heti-bhāji ।
dviṣato abhūd bhrū-kuṭī-payoda-rekhā ।। bhayaṃ cittāticāñcalyaṃ mantu-ghorekṣaṇādibhiḥ । ātma-gopana-hṛcchoṣa-vidrava-bhramaṇādikṛt ।। niṣpannaṃ pūrvavad idaṃ budhā bhaya-ratiṃ viduḥ ।
eṣāpi krodha-rativad dvi-vidhā kathitā budhaiḥ ।। śauriṇā sadasi gāndinī-sutaḥ । tatra śuṣyad-adharaḥ klamaṃ yayau ।। dvāri vārida-nibhe vṛṣāsure ।
kampra-mūrtir abhavad vrajeśvarī ।। jugupsā syād ahṛdyānubhavāc citta-nimīlanam । tatra niṣṭhīvanaṃ vaktra-kūṇanaṃ kutsanādayaḥ । rater anugrahāj jātā sā jugupsā-ratir matā ।।
nava-nava-rasa-dhāmany udyataṃ rantum āsīt । bhavati mukha-vikāraḥ suṣṭhu-niṣṭhīvanaṃ ca ।। ratitvāt prathamaikaiva sapta hāsādayas tathā । ity aṣṭau sthāyino yāvad rasāvasthāṃ na saṃśritāḥ ।।
cet svatantrās trayas-triṃśad bhaveyur vyabhicāriṇaḥ । ihāṣṭau sāttvikāś caite bhāvākhyās tān asaṅkhyakāḥ ।। kṛṣṇānvayād guṇātīta-prauḍhānanda-mayā api । bhānty amī triguṇotpanna-sukha-duḥkha-mayā iva ।।
tatra sphuranti hrī-bodhotsāhādyāḥ sāttvikā iva । tathā rājasavad-garva-harṣa-supti-hasādayaḥ । viṣāda-dīnatā-moha-śokādyās tāmasā iva ।। prāyaḥ sukha-mayāḥ śītā uṣṇā duḥkha-mayā iha ।
citreyaṃ paramānanda-sāndrāpy uṣṇā ratir matā ।। śītair bhāvair baliṣṭhais tu puṣṭā śītāyate hy asau । uṣṇais tu ratir atyuṣṇā tāpayantīva bhāsate ।। ratir dvidhāpi kṛṣṇādyaiḥ śrutair avagataiḥ smṛtaiḥ ।
tair vibhāvāditāṃ yadbhis tad-bhakteṣu raso bhavet ।। yathā dadhy-ādikaṃ dravyaṃ śarkarā-maricādibhiḥ । saṃyojana-viśeṣeṇa rasālākhyo raso bhavet ।। tad atra sarvathā sākṣāt kṛṣṇādy-anubhavādbhutaḥ ।
prauḍhānanda-camatkāro bhaktaiḥ ko apy anurasyate ।। sa raty-ādi-vibhāvādyair ekībhāva-mayo api san । jñapta-tat-tad-viśeṣaś ca tat-tad-udbhedato bhavet ।। pratīyamānāḥ prathamaṃ vibhāvādyās tu bhāgaśaḥ ।
gacchanto rasa-rūpatvaṃ militā yānty akhaṇḍatām ।। yathā marica-khaṇḍāder ekībhāve prapānake । udbhāsaḥ kasyacit kvāpi vibhāvādes tathā rase ।। rate kāraṇa-bhūtā ye kṛṣṇa-kṛṣṇa-priyādayaḥ ।
stambhādyāḥ kāra-bhūtāś ca nirvedādyāḥ sahāyakāḥ ।। hitvā kāraṇa-kāryādi-śabda-vācyatvam atra te । rasodbodhe vibhāvādi-vyapadeśatvam āpnuyuḥ ।। rates tu tat-tad-āsvāda-viśeṣāyātiyogyatām ।
vibhāvayanti kurvantīty uktā dhīrair vibhāvakāḥ ।। tāṃ cānubhāvayanty antas tadvanty āsvāda-nirbharām । ity uktā anubhāvās te kaṭākṣādyāḥ sa-sāttvikāḥ ।। sañcārayanti vaicitrīṃ nayante tāṃ tathā-vidhām ।
ye nirvedādayo bhāvās te tu sañcāriṇo matāḥ ।। eteṣāṃ tu tathā-bhāve bhagavat-kāvya-nāṭyayoḥ । sevām āhuḥ paraṃ hetuṃ kecit tat-pakṣa-rāgiṇaḥ ।। kintu tatra sudustarka-mādhuryādbhuta-sampadaḥ ।
rater asyāḥ prabhāvo ayaṃ bhavet kāraṇam uttamam ।। mahā-śakti-vilāsātmā bhāvo acintya-svarūpa-bhāk । raty-ākhyā ity ayaṃ yukto na hi tarkeṇa bādhitum । bhāratādy-uktir eṣā hi prāktanair apy udāhṛtā ।।
prakṛtibhyaḥ paraṃ yac ca tad acintyasya lakṣaṇam ।। vibhāvatādīn ānīya kṛṣṇādīn mañjulā ratiḥ । etair eva tathābhūtaiḥ svaṃ saṃvardhayati sphuṭam ।। yathā svair eva salilaiḥ paripūrya balāhakān ।
ratnālayo bhavaty ebhir vṛṣṭais tair eva vāridhiḥ ।। nave raty-aṅkure jāte hari-bhaktasya kasyacit । vibhāvatvādi-hetutvaṃ kiñcit tat kāvya-nāṭyayoḥ ।। harer īṣac-chruti-vidhau rasāsvādaḥ satāṃ bhavet ।
rater eva prabhāvo ayaṃ hetus teṣāṃ tathākṛtau ।। mādhuryādy-āśrayatvena kṛṣṇādīṃs tanute ratiḥ । tathānubhūyamānās te vistīrṇāṃ kurvate ratim ।। atas tasya vibhāvādi-catuṣkasya rater api ।
atra sāhāyikaṃ vyaktaṃ mitho ajasram avekṣyate ।। kintv etasyāḥ prabhāvo api vairūpye sati kuñcati । vairūpyas tu vibhāvāder anaucityam udīryate ।। alaukikyā prakṛtyeyaṃ sudurūhā rasa-sthitiḥ ।
yatra sādhāraṇatayā bhāvāḥ sādhu sphuranty amī ।। eṣāṃ sva-para-sambandha-niyamānirṇayo hi yaḥ । sādhāraṇyaṃ tad evoktaṃ bhāvānāṃ pūrva-sūribhiḥ ।। tad uktaṃ śrī-bharatena śaktir asti vibhāvādeḥ kāpi sādhāraṇī-kṛtau । pramātā tad-abhedena svaṃ yayā pratipadyate ।। iti ।
duḥkhādayaḥ sphuranto api jātu bhāntaḥ svīyatayā hṛdi । prauḍhānanda-camatkāra-carvaṇām eva tanvate ।। parāśrayatayāpy ete jātu bhāntaḥ sukhādayaḥ । hṛdaye paramānanda-sandoham upacinvate ।।
sad-bhāvaś ced vibhāvādeḥ kiñcin-mātrasya jāyate । sadyaś catuṣṭayākṣepāt pūrṇataivopapadyate ।। ratiḥ sthitānukāryeṣu laukikatvādi-hetubhiḥ । rasaḥ syān neti nāṭya-jñā yad āhur yuktam eva tat ।।
alaukikī tv iyaṃ kṛṣṇa-ratiḥ sarvādbhutādbhutā । yoge rasa-viśeṣatvaṃ gacchanty eva hari-priye ।। viyoge tv adbhutānanda-vivartatvaṃ dadhaty api । tanoty eṣā pragāḍhārti-bharābhāsatvam ūrjitā ।।
tatrāpi vallavādhīśa-nandanālambanā ratiḥ । sāndrānanda-camatkāra-paramāvadhir iṣyate ।। yat-sukhaugha-lavāgastyaḥ pibaty eva sva-tejasā । remaśa-mādhurī-sākṣātkārānandābdhim apy alam ।।
paramānanda-tādātmyād ratyāder asya vastutaḥ । rasasya sva-prakāśatvam akhaṇḍatvaṃ ca sidhyati ।। pūrvam uktād dvidhā bhdedān mukhya-gauṇatayā rateḥ । bhaved bhakti-raso apy eṣa mukhya-gauṇatayā dvidhā ।।
pañcadhāpi rater aikyān mukhyas tv eka ihoditaḥ । saptadhātra tathā gauṇa iti bhakti-raso aṣṭadhā ।। mukhyas tu pañcadhā śāntaḥ prītaḥ preyāṃś ca vatsalaḥ । madhuraś cety amī jñeyā yathā-pūrvam anuttamāḥ ।।
hāsyo adbhutas tathā vīraḥ karuṇo raudra ity api । bhayānakaḥ sa bībhatsa iti gauṇaś ca saptadhā ।। evaṃ bhakti-raso bhedād dvayor dvādaśadhocyate । vastutas tu purāṇādau pañcadhaiva vilokyate ।।
śvetaś citro aruṇaḥ śoṇaḥ śyāmaḥ pāṇḍura-piṅgalau । gauro dhūmras tathā raktaḥ kālo nītaḥ kramād amī ।। kapilo mādhavopendrau nṛsiṃho nanda-nandanaḥ । balaḥ kūrmas tathā kalkī rāghavo bhārgavaḥ kiriḥ ।
mīna ity eṣu kathitāḥ kramād dvādaśa devatāḥ ।। pūrter vikāra-vistāra-vikṣepa-kṣobhatas tathā । sarva-bhakti-rasāsvādaḥ pañcadhā parikīrtitaḥ ।। pūrtiḥ śānte vikāśas tu prītādiṣv api pañcasu ।
vīre adbhute ca vistāro vikṣepaḥ karuṇograyoḥ । bhayānake atha bībhatse kṣobho dhīrair udāhṛtaḥ ।। akhaṇḍa-sukha-rūpatve apy eṣām asti kvacit kvacit । raseṣu gahanāsvāda-viśeṣaḥ ko apy anuttamaḥ ।।
pratīyamānā apy ajñair grāmyaiḥ sapadi duḥkhavat । karuṇādyā rasāḥ prājñaiḥ prauḍhānanda-mayā matāḥ ।। alaukika-vibhāvatvaṃ nītebhyo rati-līlayā । sad-uktyā ca sukhaṃ tebhyaḥ syāt suvyaktam iti sthitiḥ ।।
karuṇādāv api rase jāyate yat paraṃ sukham । sucetasām anubhavaḥ pramāṇaṃ tatra kevalam ।। sarvatra karuṇākhyasya rasasyaivopapādanāt । bhaved rāmāyaṇādīnām anyathā duḥkha-hetutā ।।
tathātve rāma-pādābja-prema-kallola-vāridhiḥ । prītyā rāmāyaṇaṃ nityaṃ hanumān śṛṇuyāt katham ।। sañcārī syāt samāno vā kṛṣṇa-ratyāḥ suhṛd-ratiḥ । adhikā puṣyamāṇā ced bhāvollāsā ratiḥ ।।
phalgu-vairāgya-nirdagdhāḥ śuṣka-jñānāś ca haitukāḥ । mīmāṃsakā viśeṣeṇa bhaktyāsvāda-bahirmukhāḥ ।। ity eṣa bhakti-rasikaś caurād iva mahā-nidhiḥ । jaran-mīmāṃsakād rakṣyaḥ kṛṣṇa-bhakti-rasaḥ sadā ।।
sarvathaiva durūho ayam abhaktair bhagavad-rasaḥ । tat-pādāmbuja-sarvasvair bhaktair evānurasyate ।। vyatītya bhāvanā-vartma yaś camatkāra-kāra-bhūḥ । hṛdi sattvojjvale bāḍhaṃ svadate sa raso mataḥ ।।
bhāvanāyāḥ pade yas tu budhenānanya-buddhinā । bhāvyate gāḍha-saṃskāraiś citte bhāvaḥ sa kathyate ।। gopāla-rūpa-śobhāṃ dadhad api raghunātha-bhāva-vistārī । tuṣyatu sanātanātmā daikṣiṇa-vibhāge sudhāmbunidheḥ ।।
iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhau dakṣiṇa-vibhāge bhakti-rasa-sāmānya-nirūpaṇe sthāyi-bhāva-laharī pañcamī । dakṣiṇa-vibhāgaḥ samāptaḥ ।। dhṛta-mugdha-rūpa-bhāro bhāgavatārpita-pṛthu-premā । sa mayi sanātana-mūrtis tanotu puruṣottamas tuṣṭim ।।
rasāmṛtābdher bhāge atra tṛtīye paścimābhidhe । mukhyo bhakti-rasaḥ pañcavidhaḥ śāntādīr īryate ।। ato atra pāñcavidhyena laharyaḥ pañca kīrtitāḥ । athāmī pañca lakṣyante rasāḥ śāntādayaḥ kramāt ।।
sthāyī śānti-ratir dhīraiḥ śānta-bhakti-rasaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। prāyaḥ sva-sukha-jātīyaṃ sukhaṃ syād atra yoginām । kintv ātma-saukhyam aghanaṃ ghanaṃ tv īśam ayaṃ sukham ।। tatrāpīśa-svarūpānubhavasyaivoru-hetutā ।
dāsādi-van-mano-jñatva-līlāder na tathā matā ।। tatra ālambanāḥ caturbhujaś ca śāntāś ca asminn ālambanā matāḥ ।। ānanda-rāśir akhilātma-sindhu-taraṅgaḥ । pratyak-padāt paramahaṃsa-muner mano api ।।
saccidānanda-sāndrāṅga ātmārāma-śiromaṇiḥ । paramātmā paraṃ brahma śamo dāntaḥ śucir vaśī ।। sadā svarūpa-samprāpto hatāri-gati-dāyakaḥ । vibhur ity ādi guṇavān asminn ālambano hariḥ ।।
śāntāḥ syuḥ kṛṣṇa-tat-preṣṇha-kāruṇyena ratiṃ gatāḥ । ātmārāmās tadīyādhva-baddha-śraddhāś ca tāpasāḥ ।। ātmārāmās tu sanaka-sananda-mukhā matāḥ । prādhānyāt sanakādīnāṃ rūpaṃ bhaktiś ca kathyate ।।
te pañcaṣābda-bālābhāś catvāras tejasojjvalāḥ । gaurāṅgā vāta-vasanāḥ prāyeṇa sahacāriṇaḥ ।। gate kim api vastuni svayam adīpi tāvat sukham । mukunda sukha-cid-ghanā tava babhūva sākṣāt-kṛtiḥ ।।
bhaktir muktyaiva nirvighnety ātta-yukta-viraktatāḥ । anujjhita-mumukṣā ye bhajante te tu tāpasāḥ ।। vasānaḥ kaupīnaṃ racita-phala-kandāśana-ruciḥ । cidānandaṃ jyotiḥ kṣaṇam iva vineṣyāmi rajanīḥ ।।
bhaktātmārāma-karuṇā prapañcenaiva tāpasāḥ । śāntākhya-bhāva-candrasya hṛd-ākāśe kalāṃ śritāḥ ।। śrutir mahopaniṣadāṃ vivikta-sthāna-sevanam । antar-vṛtti-viśeṣo asya sphūrtis tattva-vivecanam ।।
vidyāśakti-pradhānatvaṃ viśva-rūpa-pradarśanam । jñāni-bhaktena saṃsargo brahma-satrādayas tathā । eṣv asādhāraṇāḥ proktā budhair uddīpanā amī ।। kurvantaḥ śruti-śirasāṃ śrutiṃ śruta-jñāḥ ।
yogīndrāḥ pulaka-bhṛto navāpy avāpuḥ ।। pādābja-tulasī-gandhaḥ śaṅkha-nādo mura-dviṣaḥ । puṇya-śailaḥ śubhāraṇyaṃ siddha-kṣetraṃ svarāpagā ।। viṣayādi-kṣayiṣṇutvaṃ kālasyākhila-hāritā ।
ityādy uddīpanā sādhāraṇās teṣāṃ kilāśritaiḥ ।। kiñjalka-miśra-tulasī-makaranda-vāyuḥ । saṅkṣobham akṣara-juṣām api citta-tanvoḥ ।। nāsāgra-nyasta-netratvam avadhūta-viceṣṭitam ।
yuga-mātrekṣita-gatir jñāna-mudrā-pradarśanam ।। harer dviṣy api na dveṣo nātibhaktiḥ priyeṣv api । siddhatāyās tathā jīvan-mukteś ca bahu-mānitā ।। nairapekṣyaṃ nirmamatā nirahaṅkāritā kathā ।
maunam ity ādayaḥ śītāḥ syur asādhāraṇāḥ kriyāḥ ।। spanda-bandhura-śirā virājate । asya nūnam avagāhate hariḥ ।। jṛmbhāṅga-moṭanaṃ bhakter upadeśo harer natiḥ ।
stavādayaś ca dāsādyaiḥ śītāḥ sādhāraṇāḥ kriyāḥ ।। bhāvāmbara-maṇir udeti yogīndra । jṛmbhām avalambate bhavataḥ ।। atha sāttvikāḥ romāñca-sveda-kampādyāḥ sāttvikāḥ pralayaṃ vinā ।।
kṣobhayan sapadi biddha-samādhiḥ । pudgale pulaka-pālim anaiṣīt ।। eṣāṃ nirabhimānānāṃ śarīrādiṣu yoginām । sāttvikās tu jvalanty eva na tu dīptā bhavanty amī ।।
sañcārino atra nirvedo dhṛtir harṣo matiḥ smṛtiḥ । viṣādotsukatāvega-vitarkādyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।। vṛthā gato bata ciraṃ kālaḥ ।। atha sthāyī atra śānti-ratiḥ sthāyī samā sāndrā ca sā dvidhā ।।
samādhau yoginas tasminn asamprajñāta-nāmani । līlayā mayi labdhe asya babhūvotkampinī tanuḥ ।। āvirbhūto nirvikalpe samādhau । mayy ānandaḥ sāndratāṃ koṭidhāsīt ।।
śānto dvidhaiṣa pārokṣya-sākṣātkāra-vibhedataḥ ।। munīśvara purātanī parama-yogacaryāpy asau । vilocana-camatkṛtiṃ kathaya kiṃ nu nirmāsyati ।। sāndraṃ mahaḥ pathi vilocanayor yadāsīt ।
na pratyag-ātmani mano ramate pureva ।। bata sākṣāt-karaṇa-pramodataḥ । katarad brahma-vido api vidyate ।। mūrdhnā ruddha-dṛg-aśrubhiḥ pulakito drāg eṣa līna-vrataḥ ।
mudrābhiḥ prakaṭīkaroty avamatiṃ yogī svarūpa-sthitau ।। bhavet kadācit kutrāpi nanda-sūnoḥ kṛpā-bharaḥ । prathamaṃ jñāna-niṣṭho api so atraiva ratim udvahet ।। svānanda-siṃhāsana-labdha-dīkṣāḥ ।
dāsī-kṛtā gopa-vadhū-viṭena ।। tat-kāruṇya-ślathībhūta-jñāna-saṃskāra-santatiḥ । eṣa bhakti-rasānanda-nipuṇaḥ syād yathā śukaḥ ।। śamasya nirvikāratvān nāṭyajñair naiṣa manyate ।
śānty-ākhyāyā rater atra svīkārān na virudhyate ।। śamo man-niṣṭhatā buddher iti śrī-bhagavad-vacaḥ । tan-niṣṭhā durghaṭā buddher etāṃ śānta-ratiṃ vinā ।। nāsti yatra sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ na dveṣo na ca matsaraḥ ।
samaḥ sarveṣu bhūteṣu sa śāntaḥ prathito rasaḥ ।। sarvathaivam ahaṅkāra-rahitatvaṃ vrajanti cet । atrāntarbhāvam arhanti dharma-vīrādayas tadā ।। sthāyinam eke tu nirveda-sthāyinaṃ pare ।
śāntam eva rasaṃ pūrve prāhur ekam anekadhā ।। nirvedo viṣaye sthāyi tattva-jñānodbhavaḥ sa cet । iṣṭāniṣṭa-viyogāpti-kṛtas tu vyabhicāry asau ।। iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhau paścima-vibhāge mukhya-bhakti-rasa-pañcaka-nirūpaṇe śānta-bhakti-rasa-laharī prathamā ।
śrīdhara-svāmibhiḥ spaṣṭam ayam eva rasottamaḥ । raṅga-prasaṅge sa-premakākhyaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। rati-sthāyitayā nāma-kaumudī-kṛdbhir apy asau । śāntatvenāyam evāddhā sudevādyaiś ca varṇitaḥ ।।
ātmocitair vibhāvādyaiḥ prītir āsvādanīyatām । nītā cetasi bhaktānāṃ prīti-bhakti-raso mataḥ ।। anugrāhyasya dāsatvāl lālyatvād apy ayaṃ dvidhā । bhidyate sambhrama-prīto gaurava-prīta ity api ।।
dāsābhimānināṃ kṛṣṇe syāt prītiḥ sambhramottarā । pūrvavat puṣyamāṇo ayaṃ sambhrama-prīta ucyate ।। tatra ālambanāḥ hariś ca tasya dāsāś ca jñeyā ālambanā iha ।। ālambano asmin dvibhujaḥ kṛṣṇo gokula-vāsiṣu ।
anyatra dvi-bhujaḥ kvāpi kutrāpy eṣu catur-bhujaḥ ।। nidhāya muralīṃ sphurat-puraṭa-nindi paṭṭāmbaraḥ । prabhur divi divaukaso bhuvi dhinoti naḥ kiṅkarān ।। kara-yuga-bhāg arikambur ambudābhaḥ ।
ravi-śaśi-maṇḍala-maṇḍitaś cakāsti ।। sakhyenojjvalitais tathā jalajayor āḍhyaś caturbhir bhujaiḥ । māṃ vyasmārayad eṣa kaṃsa-vijayī vaikuṇṭha-goṣṭhī-śriyam ।। brahmāṇḍa-koṭi-dhāmaika-roma-kūpaḥ kṛpāmbudhiḥ ।
avicintya-mahā-śaktiḥ sarva-siddhi-niṣevitaḥ ।। avatārāvalī-bījaṃ sadātmārāma-hṛd-guṇaḥ । īśvaraḥ paramārādhyaḥ sarvajñaḥ sudṛḍha-vrataḥ ।। samṛddhimān kṣamā-śīlaḥ śaraṇāgata-pālakaḥ ।
dakṣiṇaḥ satya-vacano dakṣaḥ sarva-śubhaṅkaraḥ ।। pratāpī dhārmikaḥ śāstra-cakṣur bhakta-suhṛttamaḥ । vadānyas tejasā yuktaḥ kṛtajñaḥ kīrti-saṃśrayaḥ ।। varīyān balavān prema-vaśya ity ādibhir guṇaiḥ ।
yutaś catur-vidheṣv eṣa dāseṣv ālambano hariḥ ।। dāsās tu praśritās tasya nideśa-vaśa-vartiṇaḥ । viśvastāḥ prabhutā-jñāna-vinamrita-dhiyaś ca te ।। iha tulanām aparaḥ prayāti nāsya ।
hita-caritān hari-sevakān bhajadhvam ।। caturdhāmī adhikṛtāśrita-pāriṣadānurāgāḥ ।। brahma-śaṅkara-śakrādyāḥ proktā adhikṛtā budhaiḥ । rūpaṃ prasiddham evaiṣāṃ tena bhaktir udīryate ।।
taṃ kaḥ stauty eṣa dhātā praṇamati viluṭhan kaḥ kṣitau vāsavo ayam । kālindī jāmbavatyāṃ tridaśa-paricayaṃ jāla-randhrād vyatānīt ।। atha āśritāḥ te śaraṇyā jñāni-carāḥ sevā-niṣṭhās tridhāśritāḥ ।। vijñātārthās tvad-anubhavataḥ prāsya kecin mumukṣām ।
vṛndāraṇyotsava kila vayaṃ deva sevemahi tvām ।। tatra śaraṇyāḥ śaraṇyāḥ kāliya-jarāsandha-baddha-nṛpādayaḥ ।। prabhu-vara mayy adbhutādya te karuṇā । yad ahaṃ pada-mudrayojjvalitaḥ ।।
teṣāṃ jātā mayi na karuṇā na trapā nopaśāntiḥ । tvām āyātaḥ śaraṇam abhayaṃ māṃ niyuṅkṣvātma-dāsye ।। ye mumukṣāṃ parityajya harim eva samāśritāḥ । śaunaka-pramukhās te tu proktā jñāni-carāḥ budhaiḥ ।।
ekena bhāty eṣa bhavo guṇena । kṛtādya no yena kṛśā mumukṣā ।। teṣām āstāṃ hṛdaya-kuhare śuddha-cinmātra ātmā । megha-śyāmaḥ kanaka-paridhiḥ paṅkajākṣo ayam ātmā ।।
mūlato bhajanāsaktāḥ sevā-niṣṭhā itīritāḥ । candradhvajo harihayo bahulāśvas tathā nṛpāḥ । ikṣvākuḥ śrutadevāś ca puṇḍarīkādayaś ca te ।। śūnyodyāne nayati vihagān apy alaṃ bhikṣu-caryām ।
sevāyāṃ te sphuṭam aghahara śraddhayā gardhito asmi ।। uddhavo dāruko jaitraḥ śrutadevaś ca śatrujit । nandopananda-bhadrādyāḥ pārṣadā yadu-pattane ।। niyuktāḥ santy amī mantra-sārathyādiṣu karmasu ।
tathāpi kvāpy avasare paricaryāṃ ca kurvate । kauraveṣu tathā bhīṣma-parīkṣid-vidurādayaḥ ।। tridiveśāvali-jaitra-kānti-leśāḥ । pracurālaṅkaraṇojjvalā jayanti ।।
śaṅkā-pañca-lavaṃ madād agaṇayan kālāgni-rudrād api । dvāri dvāravatī-purasya purataḥ sevotsukas tiṣṭhati ।। eteṣāṃ pravaraḥ śrīmān uddhavaḥ prema-viklavaḥ ।। labdhenāñcitam ambareṇa ca lasad-gorocanā-rociṣā ।
mukhyaṃ pāriṣadeṣu bhakti-laharī-ruddhaṃ bhajāmy uddhavam ।। sindhuṃ prārthayate bhuvaṃ tanutarāṃ brahmāṇḍa-koṭīśvaraḥ । vikrīḍaty asakṛd vicitra-caritaḥ so ayaṃ prabhur mādṛśām ।। sarvadā paricaryāsu prabhor āsakta-cetasaḥ ।
purasthāś ca vrajasthāś cety ucyate anugā dvidhā ।। sucandro maṇḍanaḥ stambaḥ sutambādyāḥ purānugāḥ । eṣāṃ pārṣadavat prāyo rūpālaṅkāraṇādayaḥ ।। dhuvati kila sucandraś cāmaraṃ candra-cārum ।
vidadhati paricaryāḥ sādhavo mādhavasya ।। raktakaḥ patrakaḥ patrī madhukaṇṭho madhuvrataḥ । rasāla-suvilāsāś ca premakando marandakaḥ ।। ānandaś candrahāsaś ca payodo vakulas tathā ।
rasadaḥ śāradādyāś ca vrajasthā anugā matāḥ ।। puraṭa-javā-madhuliṭ-paṭīra-bhāsaḥ । vraja-pati-nandana-kiṅkarān namāmi ।। varair agurubhir jalaṃ racaya vāsitaṃ vārida ।
parāga-paṭalī gavāṃ diśam arundha paurandarīm ।। vrajānugeṣu sarveṣu varīyān raktako mataḥ ।। kharvitoru-śata-parvikā-rucam । rakta-kaṇṭham anuyāmi raktakam ।।
vraja-yuvarājatayā gate prasiddhim । paṭṭimaratā ratir uttamā mamāstu ।। dhūryo dhīraś ca vīraś ca tridhā pāriṣad-ādikaḥ ।। kṛṣṇe asya preyasī-varge dāsādau ca yathāyatham ।
yaḥ prītiṃ tanute bhaktaḥ sa dhūrya iha kīrtyate ।। sarvaḥ prāṇa-samānatāṃ pracinute tad-bhakti-bhājāṃ gaṇaḥ । prītiṃ tat-praṇate khare apy avidadhad yaḥ svāsthyam ālambate ।। āśritya preyasīm asya nātisevāparo api yaḥ ।
tasya prasāda-pātraṃ syān mukhyaṃ dhīraḥ sa ucyate ।। yadukula-kamalārka tvat-prasāda-śriye api । parijana-nikhilāntaḥ-pātinī me yad-ākhyā ।। kṛpāṃ tasya samāśritya prauḍhāṃ nānyam apekṣate ।
atulāṃ yo vahan kṛṣṇe prītiṃ vīraḥ sa ucyate ।। kumāra-makara-dhvajād api na kiñcid āste phalam । priyā pariṣad-agrimāṃ na gaṇayāmi bhāmām api ।। sva eva dhiṣṇye abhiratasya kiṃ tayā ।।
eteṣu tasya dāseṣu trividheṣv āśritādiṣu । nitya-siddhāś ca siddhāś ca sādhakāḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।। anugrahasya samprāptis tasyāṅghri-rajasāṃ tathā । bhuktāvaśiṣṭa-bhaktāder api tad-bhakta-saṅgatiḥ ।
ity ādayo vibhāvāḥ syur eṣv asādhāraṇā matāḥ ।। kṛṣṇasya paśyata kṛpāṃ kṛpādyāḥ kṛpaṇe mayi । dhyeyo asau nidhane hanta dṛśor adhvānam abhyagāt ।। muralī-śṛṅgayoḥ svānaḥ smita-pūrvāvalokanam ।
guṇotkarṣa-śrutiḥ padma-padāṅka-nava-nīradāḥ । tad-aṅga-saurabhādyās tu sarvaiḥ sādhāraṇā matāḥ ।। etasyākṣi-sahasrataḥ surapater aśrūṇi sasrur bhuvi । dūrāt paśyata deva-mātṛkam abhūd vṛndāṭavī-maṇḍalam ।।
sarvataḥ svaniyogānām ādhikyena parigrahaḥ । īrṣyā-lavena cāspṛṣṭā maitrī tat-praṇate jane । tan-niṣṭhādyāḥ śītāḥ syur eṣv asādhāraṇāḥ kriyāḥ ।। akṣodīyān antarāyo vyadhāyi ।।
udbhāsvarāḥ puroktā ye tathāsya suhṛd-ādayaḥ । virāgādyāś ca ye śītāḥ proktāḥ sādhāraṇās tu te ।। śrutadevo acyutaṃ prāptaṃ svagṛhān janako yathā । natvā munīṃś ca saṃhṛṣṭo dhunvan vāso nanarta ha ।।
prema-nāṭya-guruṇāsi pāṭhitaḥ । citrayasy ahaha cāraṇān api ।। atha sāttvikāḥ stambhādyāḥ sāttvikāḥ sarve prītādi-tritaye matāḥ ।। stambham adbhutam asau bhajamānaḥ ।
stambhatāṃ vahati vaiṣṇava-varyaḥ ।। bibhran muhuḥ prema-vibhinnayā dhiyā । prahṛṣṭa-romā nṛpa gadgadākṣaram ।। harṣo dhṛtiś cātra nirvedo atha viṣaṇṇatā ।
dainyaṃ cintā smṛtiḥ śaṅkā matir autsukya-cāpale ।। vitarkāvega-hrī-jāḍya-mohonmādāvahitthikāḥ । bodhaḥ svapnaḥ klamo vyādhir mṛtiś ca vyabhicāriṇaḥ ।। itareṣāṃ madādīnāṃ nātipoṣakatā bhavet ।
yoge trayaḥ syur dhṛty-antā ayoge tu klamādayaḥ । ubhayatra pare śeṣā nirvedādyāḥ satāṃ matāḥ ।। prīty-utphulla-mukhāḥ procur harṣa-gadgadayā girā । pitaraṃ sarva-suhṛdam avitāram ivārbhakāḥ ।।
patito daṇḍa-praṇāma-śata-kāmaḥ । punar utthānaṃ visasmāra ।। aśoṣayan manas tasya mlāpayan mukha-paṅkajam । ādhis tad-virahe deva grīṣme sara ivāṃśumān ।।
ye sarvadā yadupateḥ padayoḥ patanti । dūre muhūrtam api yā na vilokate tam ।। sambhramaḥ prabhutā-jñānāt kampaś cetasi sādaraḥ । anenaikyaṃ gatā prītiḥ sambhrama-prītir ucyate ।
eṣā rase atra kathitā sthāyi-bhāvatayā budhaiḥ ।। āśritādeḥ puraivoktaḥ prakāro rati-janmani । tatra pāriṣadādes tu hetuḥ saṃskāra eva hi । saṃskārodbodhakās tasya darśana-śravaṇādayaḥ ।।
eṣā tu sambhrama-prītiḥ prāpnuvaty uttarottaram । vṛddhiṃ premā tataḥ snehas tato rāga iti tridhā ।। mamādyāmaṅgalaṃ naṣṭaṃ phalavāṃś caiva me bhavaḥ । yan namasye bhagavato yogi-dhyeyāṅghri-paṅkajam ।।
kalinda-nandinī-kula-kadamba-vana-vallabham । kadā namaskariṣāmi gopa-rūpaṃ tam īśvaram ।। hrāsa-śaṅkā-cyutā baddha-mūlā premeyam ucyate । asyānubhāvāḥ kathitās tatra vyasanitādayaḥ ।।
aṇimādi-saukhya-vīcīm avīci-duḥkha-pravāhaṃ vā । naya māṃ vikṛtir na hi me tvat-pada-kamalāvalambasya ।। mayā hṛta-jagat-trayo apy atanu-kaitavaṃ tanvatā । arajyata sa mayy aho dviguṇam eva vairocaniḥ ।।
sāndraś citta-dravaṃ kurvan premā sneha itīryate । kṣaṇikasyāpi neha syād visleṣasya sahiṣṇutā ।। vīkṣya dravac-cittam asusruvat tava । citrā na te dāruka dāru-kalpatā ।।
rajyan-mañjula-kaṇṭha-garbha-luṭhita-stotrākṣaropakramaḥ । stabdho apy abhyadhikāṃ śriyaṃ praṇamatāṃ vṛndād dadhāroddhavaḥ ।। snehaḥ sa rāgo yena syāt sukhaṃ duḥkham api sphuṭam । tat-sambandha-lave apy atra prītiḥ prāṇa-vyayair api ।।
cyutir atiśayinī ca prāya-caryā ca gurvī । viharaṇa-sacivatvād auttareyasya rājñaḥ ।। bāḍavo api kila ṣāḍavo mama । pūrṇa-siddhir api me kuśasthalī ।।
prāya ādya-dvaye premā snehaḥ pāriṣadeṣv asau । parīkṣiti bhaved-rāgo dāruke ca tathoddhave ।। vrajānugeṣv anekeṣu raktaka-pramukheṣu ca । asminn abhyudite bhāvaḥ prāyaḥ syāt sakhya-leśa-bhāk ।।
śuddhāntān militaṃ bāṣpa-ruddha-vāg uddhavo harim । kiñcit-kuñcita-netrāntaḥ svāntena pariṣasvaje ।। ayoga-yogāv etasya prabhedau kathitāv ubhau ।। saṅgābhāvo harer dhīrair ayoga iti kathyate ।
ayoge tan-manaskatvaṃ tad-guṇādy-anusandhayaḥ ।। tat-prāpty-apāya-cintādyāḥ sarveṣāṃ kathitāḥ kriyāḥ । utkaṇṭhitaṃ viyogaś cety ayoge api dvidhocyate ।। tatra utkaṇṭhitam adṛṣṭa-pūrvasya harer didṛkṣotkaṇṭhitaṃ matam ।।
cakāra meghe tad-varṇe bahu-māna-ratiṃ nṛpaḥ । pakṣapātena tan-nāmni mṛge padme ca tad-dṛśi ।। mahyaṃ na na syāt phalam añjasā dṛśaḥ ।। atrāyoga-prasaktānāṃ sarveṣām api sambhave ।
autsukya-dainya-nirveda-cintānāṃ cāpalasya ca । jaḍatonmāda-mohānām api syād atiriktatā ।। hare tvad-ālokanam antareṇa । hā hanta hā hanta kathaṃ nayāmi ।।
vilocana-rasa-cchaṭām anupalabhya vikṣubhyataḥ । kṣaṇārdham api manyate vraja-mahendra varṣa-vrajam ।। nīrandhra-dainyonnati-mukta-kaṇṭham । dākṣiṇya-leśena sakṛn niṣiñca ।।
laghur aghahara kīṭād apy ahaṃ kūṭa-karmā । snapaya kṛpaṇa-bandho mām apāṅga-cchaṭābhiḥ ।। mamābhava-niratayor bhavatu netrayor mandayoḥ । padāmbujanakhāṅkurād api visāri rocis tava ।।
taralamater api yogyatām avīkṣya । hari hari niḥśvasato niśāḥ prayāti ।। mac-cāpalaṃ ca tava vā mama vādhigamyam । mugdhaṃ mukhāmbujam udīkṣitum īkṣaṇābhyām ।।
bhayam api damayitvā bhakta-vṛndāt tṛṣārtā । tava caraṇa-sarojaṃ leḍhum anivcchatīśa ।। nyasta-krīḍanako bālo jaḍavat tan-manastayā । kṛṣṇa-graha-gṛhītātmā na veda jagad īdṛśam ।।
tanuṃ bibhrad bhavyaḥ pratikṛtir ivāste dvija-patiḥ । puraḥ śyāmāmbhode bata vinihitā dṛṣṭir amunā ।। nadati kvacid utkaṇṭho vilajjo nṛtyati kvacit । kvacit tad-bhāvanā-yuktas tanmayo anucakāra ha ।।
kvacid vihasati sphuṭaṃ kvacid amandam ākrandati । harer abhinavoddhura-praṇaya-sīdhum atto muniḥ ।। sa manyamānas tad-anāpti-kātaraḥ । śrutāśrudhāro dvija mūrcchitāpatat ।।
bata vidhūta-cid-ambhasy atra nas tīrtha-varye । kṣipata nanu satīrthāś ceṣṭatāṃ prāṇa-haṃsaḥ ।। atha viyogaḥ viyogo labdha-saṅgena vicchedo danuja-dviṣā ।। kṣataja-puraṃ puruṣottame prayāte ।
viraha-niruddha-manā niruddhavo abhūt ।। aṅgeṣu tāpaḥ kṛśatā jāgaryālamba-śūnyatā । adhṛtir jaḍatā vyādhir unmādo mūrcchitaṃ budhaiḥ । viyoge sambhrama-prīter daśāvasthāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।।
anavasthitir ākhyātā cittasyālamba-śūnyatā । arāgitā tu sarvasminn adhṛtiḥ kathitā budhaiḥ । anye aṣṭau prakaṭārthatvāt tāpādyā na hi lakṣitāḥ ।। ratnākaraś ca baḍavānala-gūḍha-mūrtiḥ ।
taṃ smārayan munipate dahatīha sabhyān ।। bhuja-parighāḥ kṛśatāṃ ca pāṇḍutāṃ ca । sphuṭam iha pāṇḍava-mitra pāṇḍu-pakṣaḥ ।। virahān mura-dviṣaś ciraṃ vidhurāṅge parikhinna-cetasi ।
kṣaṇadāḥ kṣaṇa-dāyitojjhitā bahulāśve bahulās tadābhavan ।। na kila kuṭumbam ihāsti nas trilokyām । kvacid api na vyavatiṣṭhate adya cetaḥ ।। naicikī-nicayam ujjhati dūre ।
raktakas tava padāmbuja-raktaḥ ।। khedānala-vyatikarair ativiklavasya । aṅgāni niṣkriyatayā ca kiloddhavasya ।। calite murabhidi kuśasthalī-purataḥ ।
pavana-vyādhir yathārthākhyaḥ ।। raivate navam avekṣya nīradam । paśya rauti ramate namasyati ।। vraja-bhuvi tathā nāsīn nidrā-lavo api yathā purā ।
satatam adhunā niśceṣṭāṅgās taṭāny adhiśerate ।। pracura-viraha-tāpair dhvanta-hṛt-paṅkajāyām । na kila vasatim ārtāḥ kartum icchanti haṃsāḥ ।। aśivatvān na ghaṭate bhakte kutrāpy asau mṛtiḥ ।
kṣobhakatvād viyogasya jāta-prāyeti kathyate ।। kṛṣṇena saṅgamo yas tu sa yoga iti kīrtyate । yoge api kathitaḥ siddhis tuṣṭiḥ sthitir iti tridhā ।। tatra siddhiḥ utkaṇṭhite hareḥ prāptiḥ siddhir ity abhidhīyate ।।
vaktraṃ citra-vimugdha-hāsa-madhuraṃ bāle vilole dṛśau । mandaṃ mandam aye ka eṣa mathurā-vīthīṃ mitho gāhate ।। rathāt tūrṇam avaplutya so akrūraḥ prema-vihvalaḥ । papāta caraṇopānte daṇḍavad rāma-kṛṣṇayoḥ ।।
tuṣṭiḥ jāte viyoge kaṃsāreḥ samprāptis tuṣṭir ucyate ।। prasanna-dṛṣṭyākhila-tāpa-śoṣaṇam । apaśyamānā vadanaṃ manoharam ।। samakṣam akṣamaḥ prekṣya harim añjali-bandhane ।
dāruko dvārakā-dvāri tatra citra-daśāṃ yayau ।। sthitiḥ saha-vāso mukundena sthitir nigaditā budhaiḥ ।। maṇi-stambhālambī kuru-kula-kathāṃ saṅkalayitā । guroḥ śiṣyo nūnaṃ pada-kamala-saṃvāhana-rataḥ ।।
nijāvasara-śuśrūṣā-vidhāne sāvadhānatā । puras tasya niveśādyā yoge amīṣāṃ kriyā matāḥ ।। kecid asyā rateḥ kṛṣṇa-bhakty-āsvāda-bahirmukhāḥ । bhavatvam eva niścitya na rasāvasthatāṃ jaguḥ ।।
iti tāvad asādhīyo yat purāṇeṣu keṣucit । śrīmad-bhāgavate caiṣa prakaṭo dṛśyate rasaḥ ।। dhasanti nandanti vadanty alaukikāḥ । bhavanti tūṣṇīṃ param etya nirvṛtāḥ ।।
vīryāṇi līlā-tanubhiḥ kṛtāni । protkaṇṭha udgāyati rauti nṛtyati ।। eṣātra bhakta-bhāvānāṃ prāyikī prakriyoditā । kintu kālādi-vaiśiṣṭyāt kvacit syāt sīma-laṅghanam ।।
lālyābhimānināṃ kṛṣṇe syāt prītir gauravottarā । sā vibhāvādibhiḥ puṣṭā gaurava-prītir ucyate ।। tatra ālambanāḥ hariś ca tasya lālyāś ca bhavanty ālambanā iha ।। yadupatir itihāse manda-hāsojjvalāsyaḥ ।
hitam iha nijayāgre ceṣṭayaivātmajān naḥ ।। mahā-gurur mahā-kīrtir mahā-buddhir mahā-balaḥ । rakṣī lālaka ity ādyair guṇair ālambano hariḥ ।। lālyāḥ kila kaniṣṭhatva-putratvādy-abhimāninaḥ ।
kaniṣṭhāḥ sāraṇa-gada-subhadra-pramukhāḥ smṛtāḥ । pradyumna-cārudeṣṇādyāḥ sāmbādyāś ca kumārakāḥ ।। adhika-maṇḍana-veśa-guṇa-śriyaḥ । yadu-kumāra-gaṇāḥ puri remire ।।
tāmbūla-carvitam adanti ca dīyamānam । sāmbādayaḥ kati purā vidadhus tapāṃsi ।। rukmiṇī-nandanas teṣu lālyeṣu pravaro mataḥ ।। sa jayati śambara-damanaḥ sukumāro yadu-kumāra-kula-mauliḥ ।
janayati janeṣu janaka-bhrāntiṃ yaḥ suṣṭhu rūpeṇa ।। sa eṣa paramo gurur garuḍa-go yadūnāṃ patiḥ । purārim api saṅgare guru-ruṣaṃ tiraskurmahe ।। ubhayeṣāṃ sadārādhya-dhiyaiva bhajatām api ।
sevakānām ihaiśvarya-jñānasyaiva pradhānatā ।। lālyānāṃ tu sva-sambandha-sphūrter eva samantataḥ ।। vraja-sthānāṃ paraiśvarya-jñāna-śūnya-dhiyām api । asty eva vallavādhīśa-putratvaiśvarya-vedanam ।।
atha uddīpanāḥ uddīpanās tu vātsalya-smita-prekṣādayo hareḥ ।। agre sānugrahaṃ paśyann agrajaṃ vyagra-mānasaḥ । gadaḥ padāravinde asya vidadhe daṇḍavan-natim ।। anubhāvās tu tasyāgre nīcāsana-niveśanam ।
guror vartmānusāritvaṃ dhuras tasya parigrahaḥ । svairācāra-vimokṣādyāḥ śītā lālyeṣu kīrtitāḥ ।। sukhada-karaka-vārbhir brahmaṇābhyukṣitāṅgaḥ । bhuvam abhi makarāṅko rāṅkavaṃ svīcakāra ।।
dāsaiḥ sādhārāṇāś cānye procyante amīṣu kecana । praṇāmo mauna-bāhulyaṃ saṅkocaṃ praśrayāḍhyatā । nija-prāṇa-vyayenāpi tad-ājñā-paripālanam ।। adho-vadanatā sthairyaṃ kāsa-hāsādi-varjanam ।
tadīyātirahaḥ-keli-vārtādy-uparamādayaḥ ।। dvandve dṛśoḥ padam asau kila niṣprakampā । svinnādya kaṇṭaki-phalaṃ tanur anvakārṣīt ।। atha vyabhicāriṇaḥ anantaroktāḥ sarve atra bhavanti vyabhicāriṇaḥ ।।
dhvanau sthitānāṃ yadu-rājadhanyām । naṭaiś ca hṛṣyadbhir akāri nṛtyam ।। yas tātena vikṛṣya vatsalatayā svotsaṅgam āropitaḥ । prāptā na kṣaṇikāpi lālana-ratiḥ sā yena bālye pituḥ ।।
deha-sambandhitāmānād guru-dhīr atra gauravam । tanmayī lālake prītir gaurava-prītir ucyate ।। sthāyi-bhāvo atra sā caiṣām āmūlāt svayam ucchritā । kañcid viśeṣam āpannā premeti sneha ity api ।
rāga ity ucyate cātra gaurava-prītir eva sā ।। vaktraṃ ca nonnamayati sravad-asra-kīrṇam । dṛṣṭiṃ kṣipaty aghabhidaś caraṇāravinde ।। karād ākṛṣyaiva prasabham abhimanyāv api hate ।
prapede kalyāṇī na hi malinimānaṃ lavam api ।। vimṛjya mayi nikṣipa prasarad-aśru-dhāre dṛśau । nidhehi savidhe pituḥ kathaya vatsa kaḥ sambhramaḥ ।। nipibati cet pitur iṅgitaṃ jhaṣāṅkaḥ ।
viṣam iva tāṃ tu sudhāṃ sa eva sadyaḥ ।। triṣv evāyoga-yogādyā bhedāḥ pūrvavad īritāḥ ।। ḍambaraḥ sa ripur ambarāyitaḥ । kambu-rāja-karam īkṣitāsmahe ।।
na vaṣṭi yogyāṃ ca tathāstra-yogyām । kārām iva dvāravatīm avaiti ।। militaḥ śambara-purato madanaḥ purato vilokayan pitaram । ko aham iti svaṃ pramadān na dhīr adhīr apy asau veda ।।
militam adhiṣṭhita-garuḍaṃ prekṣya yudhiṣṭhira-purān murārātim । ajani mudā yadu-nagare sambhrama-bhūmā kumārāṇām ।। kuñcayann akṣiṇī kiñcid bāṣpa-niṣpandi-pakṣiṇī । vandate pādayor dvandvaṃ pituḥ prati-dinaṃ smaraḥ ।।
utkaṇṭhita-viyogādye yad yad vistāritaṃ na hi । sambhrama-prītivaj jñeyaṃ tat tad evākhilaṃ budhaiḥ ।। iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhau paścima-vibhāge mukhya-bhakti-rasa-pañcaka-nirūpaṇe prīti-bhakti-rasa-laharī dvitīyā । sthāyi-bhāvo vibhāvādyaiḥ sakhyam ātmocitair iha ।
nītaś citte satāṃ puṣṭiṃ rasaḥ preyān udīryate ।। tatra ālambanāḥ hariś ca tad-vayasyāś ca tasminn ālambanā matāḥ ।। tatra hariḥ dvibhujatvādi-bhāg atra prāgvad ālambano hariḥ ।। sphurat-puraṭa-ketakī-kusuma-ramya-paṭṭāmbaraḥ ।
vrajād aghaharo haraty ahaha naḥ sakhīnāṃ manaḥ ।। sakhyenojjvalitais tathā jalajayor āḍhyaṃ caturbhir bhujaiḥ । jagmuḥ pāṇḍu-sutāḥ pramoda-sudhayā naivātma-sambhāvanām ।। suveṣaḥ sarva-sal-lakṣma-lakṣito balināṃ varaḥ ।
vividhādbhuta-bhāṣā-vid vāvadūkaḥ supaṇḍitaḥ ।। vipula-pratibho dakṣaḥ karuṇo vīra-śekharaḥ । vidagdho buddhimān kṣantā rakta-lokaḥ samṛddhimān । sukhī varīyān ity ādyā guṇās tasyeha kīrtitā ।।
rūpa-veṣa-guṇādyais tu samāḥ samyag-ayantritāḥ । viśrambha-sambhṛtātmāno vayasyās tasya kīrtitāḥ ।। bhakti-prapañcam anudañcad-anugraheṇa । vandetarām aghaharasya vayasya-vṛndam ।।
te pura-vraja-sambandhād dvi-vidhāḥ prāya īritāḥ ।। arjuno bhīmasenaś ca duhitā drupadasya ca । śrīdāma-bhūsurādyāś ca sakhāyaḥ pura-saṃśrayāḥ ।। bhuja-parighayoḥ śliṣṭau bhīmārjunau pulakojjvalau ।
tam avaśādhiyaḥ prauḍhānandād arundhata pāṇḍavāḥ ।। śreṣṭhaḥ pura-vayasyeṣu bhagavān vānaradhvajaḥ ।। ramyorur indīvara-sundarābhaḥ । sa rohitākṣaḥ sutarām arājīt ।।
niḥśaṅka-praṇaya-nisṛṣṭa-pūrva-kāyaḥ । gāṇḍīvī smita-vadanāmbujo vyarājīt ।। kṣaṇādarśanato dīnāḥ sadā saha-vihāriṇaḥ । tad-eka-jīvitāḥ proktā vayasyā vraja-vāsinaḥ ।
ataḥ sarva-vayasyeṣu pradhānatvaṃ bhajanty amī ।। priyaṅkaraṇa-vallakī-dala-viṣāṇa-veṇv-aṅkitāḥ । sadā praṇaya-śālinaḥ sahacarā hareḥ pāntu vaḥ ।। hanta śrānta ivāsi nikṣipa sakhe śrīdāma-pāṇau girim ।
doṣṇas te karavāma kāmam adhunā savyasya saṃvāhanam ।। dāsyaṃ gatānāṃ para-daivatena । sākaṃ vijahruḥ kṛta-puṇya-puñjāḥ ।। drutam agha-jaṭharāntaḥ-koṭare prekṣamāṇaḥ ।
kṣaṇam aham avasīdan śūnya-cittas tadāsam ।। suhṛdaś ca sakhāyaś ca tathā priya-sakhāḥ pare । priya-narma-vayasyāś cety uktā goṣṭhe catur-vidhāḥ ।। vātsalya-gandhi-sakhyāṃ tu kiñcit te vayasādhikāḥ ।
sāyudhās tasya duṣṭebhyaḥ sadā rakṣā-parāyaṇāḥ ।। subhadra-maṇḍalībhadra-bhadravardhana-gobhaṭāḥ । yakṣendrabhaṭa-bhadrāṅga-vīrabhadrā mahā-guṇāḥ । vijayo balabhadrādyāḥ suhṛdas tasya kīrtitāḥ ।।
gurvīṃ nārya gadāṃ gṛhāṇa vijaya kṣobhaṃ vṛthā mā kṛthāḥ । garjann eṣa ghano balī na tu balīvardākṛtir dānavaḥ ।। suhṛtsu maṇḍalībhadra-balabhadrau kilottamau ।। pāṭala-paṭala-sad-aṅgo lakuṭa-karaḥ śekharī śikhaṇḍena ।
dyuti-maṇḍalī-mali-nibhāṃ bhāti dadhan maṇḍalībhadraḥ ।। sukhaṃ svapitu naḥ suhṛd vraja-niśānta-madhye niśi । tvam asya visṛjann alaṃ subala sakthinī lālaya ।। kastūrī-kṛta-citrakaṃ pṛthu-hṛdi bhrājiṣṇu guñjā-srajam ।
gambhīra-svanitaṃ pralamba-bhujam ālambe pralamba-dviṣam ।। snapayitum iha sadmany ambayā stambhito asmi । phaṇi-pati-hrada-kacche nādya gaccheḥ kadāpi ।। kaniṣṭha-kalpāḥ sakhyena sambandhāḥ prīti-gandhinā ।
viśāla-vṛṣabhaurjasvi-devaprastha-varūthapāḥ ।। maranda-kusumāpīḍa-maṇibandha-karandhamāḥ । ity-ādayaḥ sakhāyo asya sevā-sakhyaika-rāgiṇaḥ ।। varūthapa vilambitālaka-varūtham utsāraya ।
yad ugra-bhuja-saṅgare gurum agāt klamaṃ naḥ sakhā ।। sarveṣu sakhiṣu śreṣṭho devaprastho ayam īritaḥ ।। pāśā-baddhottuṅga-maulir balīyān । devaprasthaḥ kṛṣṇa-pārśvaṃ pratasthe ।।
dāmnaḥ savya-kareṇa ruddha-hṛdayaṃ śayyā-virājat-tanum । devaprastha itaḥ kṛtī sukhayati premṇā vrajendrātmajam ।। vayas-tulyāḥ priya-sakhā sakhyaṃ kevalam āśritāḥ । śrīdāmā ca sudāmā ca dāmā ca vasudāmakaḥ ।।
kiṅkiṇi-stokakṛṣṇāṃśu-bhadrasena-vilāsinaḥ । puṇḍarīka-viṭaṅkākṣa-kalaviṅkādayo apy amī ।। ramayanti priya-sakhāḥ kelibhir vividhaiḥ sadā । niyuddha-daṇḍa-yuddhādi-kautukair api keśavam ।।
prasārya bhujayor yugaṃ pulaki kaścid āśliṣyati । kṛśāṅgi sukhayanty amī priya-sakhāḥ sakhāyaṃ tava ।। eṣu priya-vayasyeṣu śrīdāmā pravaro mataḥ ।। baddha-spardhaṃ sauhṛdān mādhavena ।
śrīdāmānaṃ dāma-bhājaṃ bhajāmi ।। diṣṭyā dṛṣṭim ito asi hanta niviḍāśleṣaiḥ sakhīn prīṇaya । kiṃ goṣṭhaṃ kim abhīṣṭam ity acirataḥ sarvaṃ viparyasyati ।। priya-narma-vayasyās tu pūrvato apy abhito varāḥ ।
ātyantika-rahasyeṣu yuktā bhāva-viśeṣiṇaḥ । subalārjuna-gandharvās te vasantojjvalādayaḥ ।। śyāmā-kandarpa-lekhaṃ nibhṛtam upaharaty ujjvalaḥ pāṇi-padme । tārā-dāmeti narma-praṇayi-sahacarās tanvi tanvanti sevām ।।
priya-narma-vayasyeṣu prabalau subalārjunau ।। hari-dayitaṃ hāriṇaṃ harid-vasanam । naya-nandita-bāndhavaṃ vande ।। viśāradāyām api mādhavasya ।
saṃjñā-mayī kāpi babhūva vārtā ।। madhu-puṣpa-balibhiḥ prasādhitam । maṇi-hārojjvalam ujjvalaṃ bhaje ।। dūtaḥ sameti sakhi yatra milaty adūre ।
kā vā vṛṣasyati na gopa-vṛṣaṃ kiśorī ।। ujjvalo ayaṃ viśeṣeṇa sadā narmokti-lālasaḥ ।। sumadhura-rasa-rūpo durgamāvāra-pāraḥ । tad iyam aghahara tvām eti sarvādhvanaiva ।।
eteṣu ke api śāstreṣu ke api lokeṣu viśrutāḥ ।। nitya-priyāḥ sura-carāḥ sādhakāś ceti te tridhā । kecid eṣu sthirā jātyā mantrivat tam upāsate ।। taṃ hāsayanti cāpalāḥ kecid vaihāsikopamāḥ ।
kecid ārjava-sāreṇa saralāḥ śīlayanti tam ।। vāmā vakrima-cakreṇa kecid vismāyayanty amum । kecit pragalbhāḥ kurvanti vitaṇḍām amunā । saumyāḥ sūnṛtayā vācā dhanyā dhinvanti taṃ pare ।।
evaṃ vividhayā sarve prakṛtyā madhurā amī । pavitra-maitrī-vaicitrī-cārutām upacinvate ।। uddīpanā vayo-rūpa-śṛṅga-veṇu-darā hareḥ । vinoda-narma-vikrānti-guṇāḥ preṣṭha-janās tathā ।
rāja-devāvatārādi-ceṣṭānukaraṇādayaḥ ।। vayaḥ kaumāra-paugaṇḍa-kaiśoraṃ ceha sammatam । goṣṭhe kaumāra-paugaṇḍe kaiśoraṃ pura-goṣṭhayoḥ ।। tatra kaumāraṃ, yathā kaumāraṃ vatsale vācyaṃ tataḥ saṅkṣipya likhyate ।।
vāme pāṇau masṛṇa-kavalaṃ tat-phalāny aṅgulīṣu । svarge loke miṣati bubhuje yajña-bhug bāla-keliḥ ।। atha paugaṇḍam ādyaṃ madhyaṃ tathā śeṣaṃ paugaṇḍaṃ ca tridhā bhavet ।। adharādeḥ sulauhityaṃ jaṭharasya ca tānavam ।
kambu-grīvodgamādyaṃ ca paugaṇḍe prathame sati ।। kaṇṭhaṃ kambuvad ambujākṣa bhajate rekhā-trayīm ujjvalām । lakṣmīr ādhunikī dhinoti suhṛdām akṣīṇi sā kāpy asau ।। puṣpa-maṇḍana-vaicitrī citrāṇi giri-dhātubhiḥ ।
pīta-paṭṭa-dukūlādyam iha proktaṃ prasādhanam ।। sarvāṭavī-pracāreṇa naicikī-caya-cāraṇam । niyuddha-keli-nṛtyādi-śikṣārambho atra ceṣṭitam ।। guñjāhārī śikhaṇḍa-prakaṭita-mukuṭaḥ pīta-paṭṭāmbara-śrīḥ ।
nṛtyan dor-yuddha-raṅge naṭavad iha sakhīn nandayaty eṣa kṛṣṇaḥ ।। nāsā suśikharā tuṅgā kapolau maṇḍalākṛtī । pārśvādy-aṅgaṃ suvalitaṃ paugaṇḍe sati madhyame ।। nava-maṇi-darpaṇa-darpa-nāśi-gaṇḍaḥ ।
sukhayati suṣṭhu sakhīn sva-śobhayaiva ।। uṣṇīṣaṃ paṭṭa-sūtrottha-pāśenātra taḍit-tviṣā । yaṣṭiḥ śyāmā tri-hastoccā svarṇāgrety ādi-maṇḍanam । bhāṇḍīre krīḍanaṃ śailoddhāraṇādyaṃ ca ceṣṭitam ।।
bibhral-līlāṃ caṭula-camarī-cāru-cūḍojjvala-śrīḥ । paśya krīḍan sukhayati sakhe mitra-vṛndaṃ mukundaḥ ।। paugaṇḍa-madhya evāyaṃ harir dīvyan virājate । mādhuryādbhuta-rūpatvāt kaiśorāgrāṃśa-bhāg iva ।।
veṇī nitamba-lambāgrā līlālaka-latā-dyuti । aṃsayos tuṅgatety ādi paugaṇḍe carame sati ।। cañcad-veṇī-śikhara-śikhayā cumbita-śreṇi-bimbaḥ । nyasyann eva priya-savayasāṃ gokulān nirjihīte ।।
uṣṇīṣe vakrimā līlā-sarasī-ruha-pāṇitā । kāśmīreṇordhva-puṇḍrādyam iha maṇḍanam īritam ।। gaura-śrīr alike kilordhva-tilakaḥ kastūrikā-bindumān । vikrāntaṃ kim uta svabhāva-mṛdulāṃ goṣṭhābalānāṃ tatim ।।
atra bhaṅgī girāṃ narma-sakhaiḥ karṇa-kathā-rasaḥ । eṣu gokula-bālānāṃ śrī-ślāghety-ādi-ceṣṭitam ।। keyaṃ mohanatā-samṛddhir adhunā godhuk-kumārī-gaṇe । pañceṣur jagatāṃ jaye nija-dhurāṃ yatrārpayan mādyati ।।
atha kaiśoram kaiśoraṃ pūrvam evoktaṃ saṅkṣepeṇocyate tataḥ ।। pronmīlad-vana-mālikā-parimala-stome tamāla-tviṣi । śrīdāmā ramaṇīya-roma-kalikākīrṇāṅga-śākhī babhau ।। prāyaḥ kiśora evāyaṃ sarva-bhakteṣu bhāsate ।
tena yauvana-śobhāsya neha kācit prapañcitā ।। alaṅkāram alaṅkṛtvā tavāṅgaṃ paṅkajekṣaṇa । sakhīn kevalam evedaṃ dhāmnā dhīman dhinoti naḥ ।। uṣasi viṣāṇa-vare ruvaty udagram ।
api nivahāḥ samam eva jāgrati sma ।। harim anveṣṭum itaḥ sutāṃ raveḥ । dhvani-dūtaḥ śikhare dhinoti naḥ ।। pāñcālī-patayaḥ śrutvā pāñcajanyasya nisvanam ।
pañcāsya paśya muditāḥ pañcāsya-pratimāṃ yayuḥ ।। kṛta-vara-kavarīkaṃ ratna-tāṭaṅka-karṇam । priya-sakhi subalo abhūd vismitaḥ sa-smitaś ca ।। niyuddha-kanduka-dyūta-vāhya-vāhādi-kelibhiḥ ।
laguḍālaguḍi-krīḍā-saṅgaraiś cāsya toṣaṇam ।। palyaṅkāsana-dolāsu saha-svāpopaveśanam । cāru-citra-parīhāso vihāraḥ salilāśaye ।। yugmatve lāsya-gānādyāḥ sarva-sādhāraṇāḥ kriyāḥ ।।
tvam aṭasi sakhi-goṣṭhyām ātma-vīryaṃ stuvānaḥ । viramita-raṇa-raṅgo niḥsahāṅgaḥ sthito asi ।। yuktāyuktādi-kathanaṃ hita-kṛtye pravartanam । prāyaḥ puraḥsaratvādyāḥ suhṛdām īritāḥ kriyāḥ ।।
tāmbulādy-arpaṇaṃ vaktre tilaka-sthāsaka-kriyā । patrāṅkura-vilekhādi sakhīnāṃ karma kīrtitam ।। nirjitī-karaṇaṃ yuddhe vastre dhṛtvāsya karṣaṇam । puṣpādy-ācchedanaṃ hastāt kṛṣṇena sva-prasādhanam ।
hastāhasti-prasaṅgādyāḥ proktāḥ priya-sakha-kriyāḥ ।। dūtyaṃ vraja-kiśorīṣu tāsāṃ praṇaya-gāmitā । tābhiḥ keli-kalau sākṣāt sakhyuḥ pakṣa-parigrahaḥ ।। asākṣāt sva-sva-yūtheśā-pakṣa-sthāpana-cāturī ।
karṇākarṇi-kathādyāś ca priya-narma-sakha-kriyāḥ ।। vanya-ratnālaṅkārair mādhavasya prasādhanam । puras tauryatrikaṃ tasya gavāṃ sambhālana-kriyāḥ ।। aṅga-saṃvāhanaṃ mālya-gumphanaṃ bījanādayaḥ ।
etāḥ sādhāraṇā dāsair vayasyānāṃ kriyā matāḥ । pūrvokteṣv aparāś cātra jñeyā dhīrair yathocitam ।। śrīdāmāyaṃ drāk pariṣvaktu-kāmaḥ । bāhu-stambhau paśya notkṣeptum īṣṭe ।।
svāty-ambude varṣati ramya-ghoṣe । svedāmbu-muktā-paṭalīṃ prasūte ।। vipula-pulakollāsaṃ svarā pariṣvajate hariḥ । kva subala purā siddha-kṣetre cakatha kiyat-tapaḥ ।।
tadīya-suhṛdas tadā pṛthula-vepathu-vyākulāḥ । nipatya nikaṭa-sthalī-bhuvi suṣuptim ārebhire ।। tasya kṣayārtham iva bāṣpa-jharaṃ kirantī । ābhīra-vīthir abhito harim āvariṣṭa ।।
augryaṃ trāsaṃ tathālasyaṃ varjayitvākhilāḥ pare । rase preyasi bhāva-jñaiḥ kathitā vyabhicāriṇaḥ ।। tatrāyoge madaṃ harṣaṃ garvaṃ nidrāṃ dhṛtiṃ vinā । yoge mṛtiṃ klamaṃ vyādhiṃ vināpasmṛti-dīnate ।।
vallaveśvara-sute samīyuṣi । tad-giraś ca vivaśāṅgatāṃ dadhuḥ ।। vimukta-sambhramā yā syād viśrambhātmā ratir dvayoḥ । prāyaḥ samānayor atra sā sakhya-sthāyi-śabda-bhāk ।।
viśrambho gāḍha-viśvāsa-viśeṣaḥ yantraṇojjhitaḥ । eṣā sakhya-ratir vṛddhiṃ gacchantī praṇayaḥ kramāt । premā snehas tathā rāga iti pañca-bhidoditā ।। mukundo gāndinī-putra tvayā sandiśyatām iti ।
garuḍāṅka guḍākeśas tvāṃ kadā parirapsyate ।। prāptāyāṃ sambhramādīnāṃ yogyatāyām api sphuṭam । tad-gandhenāpy asaṃspṛṣṭā ratiḥ praṇaya ucyate ।। api prathayataḥ parām adhika-pārameṣṭhya-śriyam ।
samaskuruta pāṃśumān śirasi candrakān arjunaḥ ।। mukunda vasatir vane para-gṛhe ca dāsya-kriyā । parantu vavṛdhe tvayi dvi-guṇam eva sakhyāmṛtam ।। anye tad-anurūpāṇi manojñāni mahātmanaḥ ।
gāyanti sma mahārāja sneha-klinna-dhiyaḥ śanaiḥ ।। varṣaty ucchvasiteṣu kṛṣṇa-mudire vyaktaṃ babhūvādbhutam । yā nāsīd udagād dṛśoḥ pathi sadā nīrorudhāvātra sā ।। yā patri-paṅktir akṛpeṇa kṛpī-sutena ।
jātāsya sā kusuma-vṛṣṭir ivotsavāya ।। vana-mālā-racanocitāny araṇye । divasārdhe api babhūva kaumudīva ।। dhanur-vedam adhīyāno madhyamas tvayi pāṇḍavaḥ ।
bāṣpa-saṅkīrṇayā kṛṣṇaḥ girāśleṣaṃ vyajijñapat ।। davasya kavalād api tvam avitātra yeṣām abhūḥ । kathaṃ na viraha-jvarād avasitān sakhīn adya naḥ ।। atrāpi pūrvavat proktās tāpādyās tā daśā daśa ।।
tuṣāre api prauḍhiṃ dinakara-sutā-srotasi gataḥ । balīyān uttāpas tava viraha-janmā jvalayati ।। gabhīrād ābhīrāvali-tanuṣu khedād anudinam । samīrasya ghrānādhvani pṛthulatā kevalam abhūt ।।
bāṣpāmbu-pūreṇa varūthapasya । nirvidya nidrā-madhupī mumoca ।। laghu-bhṛtaṃ sadyaḥ patad-atitarām utpatad api । nirālambaṃ cetaḥ kvacid api vilambaṃ lavam api ।।
kalayati ca kalānāṃ vismṛtau yatna-koṭim । yaduvara virahāt te nārthitāṃ bandhu-vargaḥ ।। sadā viphala-vṛttayo virahitāḥ kila cchāyayā । sphurati suhṛdāṃ gaṇāḥ śikhara-jāta-vṛkṣā iva ।।
viraha-jvara-saṃjvareṇa te jvalitā viślatha-gātra-bandhanā । yaduvīra taṭe viceṣṭate ciram ābhīra-kumāra-maṇḍalī ।। jagad-vyavahṛti-kramaṃ nikhilam eva vismāritāḥ । rudanti mathurā-pate kim api vallavānāṃ gaṇāḥ ।।
prāpya rājyam adhunā madhu-nāthe । gokule tu muhur ākulatābhūt ।। gopāḥ śaila-taṭe tathā śithilita-śvāsāṅkurāḥ śerate । śocanty adya yathā ciraṃ paricaya-snigdhāḥ kuraṅgā api ।।
prokteyaṃ virahāvasthā spaṣṭa-līlānusārataḥ । kṛṣṇena viprayogaḥ syān na jātu vraja-vāsinām ।। vatsair vatsatarībhiś ca sadā krīḍati mādhavaḥ । vṛndāvanāntara-gataḥ sa-rāmo bālakair vṛtaḥ ।।
pāṇḍavaḥ puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ prekṣya cakri-niketane । citrākāraṃ bhajann eva mitrākāram adarśayat ।। bhīmaḥ smayan prema-javākulendriyaḥ । prabṛddha-bāṣpaḥ parirebhire acyutam ।।
priya-saṅgamaṃ vraja-suhṛn-nikarāḥ । pulakāñcitena pariṣaṣvajire ।। dhṛtātmabhir yogibhir apy alabhyaḥ । kiṃ varṇyate diṣṭam ato vrajaukasām ।।
dvayor apy eka-jātīya-bhāva-mādhurya-bhāg asau । preyān kām api puṣṇāti rasaś citta-camatkṛtim ।। prīte ca vatsale cāpi kṛṣṇa-tad-bhaktayoḥ punaḥ । dvayor anyonya-bhāvasya bhinna-jātīyatā bhavet ।।
preyān eva bhavet preyān ataḥ sarva-raseṣv ayam । sakhya-sampṛkta-hṛdayaiḥ sadbhir evānubudhyate ।। iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhau paścima-vibhāge mukhya-bhakti-rasa-pañcaka-nirūpaṇe preyo-bhakti-rasa-laharī tṛtīyā । vibhāvādyais tu vātsalyaṃ sthāyī puṣṭim upāgataḥ ।
eṣa vatsala-nāmātra prokto bhakti-raso budhaiḥ ।। tatra ālambanāḥ kṛṣṇaṃ tasya gurūṃś cātra prāhur ālambanān budhāḥ ।। vicalad-alaka-bhṛṅga-krānta-netrāmbujāntam । vraja-pati-dayitāsīt prasnavotpīḍa-digdhā ।।
śyāmāṅgo ruciraḥ sarva-sal-lakṣaṇa-yuto mṛduḥ । priya-vāk saralo hrīmān vinayī mānya-māna-kṛt । dātety-ādi-guṇo kṛṣṇo vibhāva iti kathyate ।। evaṃ guṇasya cāsyānugrāhyatvād eva kīrtitā ।
prabhāvānāspadatayā vedyasyātra vibhāvatā ।। trayyā copaniṣadbhiś ca sāṅkhya-yogaiś ca sātvataiḥ । upagīyamāna-māhātmyaṃ hariṃ sāmanyatātmajam ।। śaṅke pūtanikādayaḥ kṣiti-ruhau tau vātyayonmūlitau ।
tat-tat-karma duranvayaṃ mama śiśoḥ kenāsya sambhāvyate ।। adhikaṃ-manya-bhāvena śikṣā-kāritayāpi ca । lālakatvādināpy atra vibhāvā guravo matāḥ ।। lālanotkam abhitaḥ kṛpākulam ।
gauravaṃ gaṇam agaṇyam āśraye ।। te tu tasyātra kathitā vraja-rājñī vrajeśvaraḥ । rohiṇī tāś ca vallavyo yāḥ padmaja-hṛtātmajāḥ ।। devakī tat-sapatnyaś ca kuntī cānakadundubhiḥ ।
sāndīpani-mukhāś cānye yathā-pūrvam amī varāḥ । vrajeśvarī-vrajādhīśau śreṣṭhau gurujaneṣv imau ।। putra-sneha-snuta-kuca-yugaṃ jāta-kampaṃ ca subhrūḥ । svinnaṃ vaktraṃ kabara-vigalan-mālatī nirmamantha ।।
sīmānta-dyutir aṅga-bhūṣaṇa-vidhiṃ nāti-prabhūtaṃ śritā । śyāma-śyāma-rucir vicitra-sicayā goṣṭheśvarī pātu vaḥ ।। sa-bāṣpākṣī rakṣā-tilakam alike kalpayati ca । yaśodā mūrteva sphurati suta-vātsalya-paṭalī ।।
nava-bhāṇḍīra-palāśa-cāru-celam । vraja-rājaṃ vara-kūrcam arcayāmi ।। skhalad-aṅghri prasarantam aṅgane । mumude prekṣya sutaṃ vrajādhipaḥ ।।
kaumārādi-vayo-rūpa-veśāḥ śaiśava-cāpalam । jalpita-smita-līlādyāḥ budhair uddīpanāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। tatra kaumāram ādyaṃ madhyaṃ tathā śeṣaṃ kaumāraṃ tri-vidhaṃ matam ।। sthūla-madhyorutāpāṅga-śvetimā svalpa-dantatā ।
pravyakta-mārdavatvaṃ ca kaumāre prathame sati ।। pṛthutara-madhya-kaṭi-rakoru-sīmā । mudam adhikāṃ vraja-nāthayor vyatānīt ।। asmin muhuḥ pada-kṣepa-kṣaṇike rudita-smite ।
