svāṅguṣṭha-pānam uttāna-śayanādyaṃ ca ceṣṭitam ।। pracala-caraṇa-yugmaṃ putram uttāna-suptam । tilam api viratāsīn nekṣituṃ goṣṭha-rājñī ।। atra vyāghra-nakhaṃ kaṇṭhe rakṣā-tilaka-maṅgalam ।
paṭṭa-ḍorī kaṭau haste sūtram ity ādi maṇḍanam ।। śiśuṃ rucira-rocanā-kṛta-tamāla-patra-śriyam । vrajeśa-gṛhiṇī sutaṃ na kila vīkṣya tṛptiṃ yayau ।। dṛk-taṭī-bhāg-alakatānagnatā cchidri-karṇatā ।
kalokti-riṅganādyaṃ ca kaumāre sati madhyame ।। kala-vacanam udañcan nūtana-śrotra-randhram । tanayam amṛta-sindhau prekṣya mātā nyamāṅkṣīt ।। ghrāṇasya śikhare muktā nava-nītaṃ karāmbuje ।
kiṅkiṇy-ādi ca kaṭyādau prasādhanam ihoditam ।। smita-mukham ujjvala-nāsikāgram uktam । tanayam avekṣya nananda nanda-patnī ।। atra kiñcit kṛśaṃ madhyam īṣat-prathima-bhāg uraḥ ।
śiraś ca kāka-pakṣāḍhyaṃ kaumāre carame sati ।। prathimopakrama-śikṣaṇārthi-vakṣāḥ । jananīṃ stambhayati sma divya-ḍimbhaḥ ।। dhaṭī phaṇa-paḍī cātra kiñcid-vanya-vibhūṣaṇam ।
laghu-vetraka-ratnādi maṇḍanaṃ parikīrtitam ।। vatsa-rakṣā vrajābhyarṇe vayasyaiḥ saha khelanam । pāva-śṛṅga-dalādīnāṃ vādanādy atra ceṣṭitam ।। kare ca laguḍīṃ laghuṃ savayasāṃ kulair āvṛtaḥ ।
sutas tava kṛtārthayaty ahaha paśya netrāṇi naḥ ।। atha paugaṇḍam paugaṇḍādi puraivoktaṃ tena saṅkṣipya likhyate ।। dhavalim ayug-apāṅgo maṇḍitaḥ kañcukena । vraja-bhuvi mama vatsaḥ kacca-deśād upaiti ।।
viluṭhad-amala-hāro ramya-romāvali-śrīḥ । tvad-udara-khani-janmā netram uccair dhinoti ।। navyena yauvanenāpi dīvyan goṣṭhendra-nandanaḥ । bhāti kevala-vātsalya-bhājāṃ paugaṇḍa-bhāg iva ।।
sukumāreṇa paugaṇḍa-vayasā saṅgato apy asau । kiśorābhaḥ sadā dāsa-viśeṣāṇāṃ prabhāsate ।। santānikāṃ harati kṛntati mantha-daṇḍam । mātuḥ pramoda-bharam eva haris tanoti ।।
nāyāty eṣa latāntare sphuṭam ito gavyaṃ hariṣyan hariḥ । trasyal-locanam asya śuṣyad-adharaṃ ramyaṃ didṛkṣe mukham ।। anubhāvāḥ śiro-ghrāṇaṃ kareṇāṅgābhimārjanam । āśīrvādo nideśaś ca lālanaṃ pratipālanam ।
hitopadeśa-dānādyā vatsale parikīrtitāḥ ।। jātānurāgā gata-manyavo arbhakān । ghrāṇair avāpuḥ paramāṃ mudaṃ te ।। samagram āghrāya śiraḥ sapiccham ।
aṅgāni putrasya muhur mamārja ।। cumbāśleṣau tathāhvānaṃ nāma-grahaṇa-pūrvakam । upālambhādayaś cātra mitraiḥ sādhāraṇāḥ kriyāḥ ।। atha sāttvikāḥ navātra sāttvikāḥ stanya-srāvaḥ stambhādayaś ca te ।।
utthāpya dorbhiḥ parirabhya nirbharam । matvā paraṃ brahma sutān apāyayan ।। akhila-surabhi-reṇūn kṣālayadbhir yaśodā । tava navam abhiṣekaṃ dugdha-pūraiḥ karoti ।।
kalayitum api nālaṃ bāṣpa-pura-plutākṣī । dadhatam acalam āsīd vyākulā gokuleśā ।। atha vyabhicāriṇaḥ tatrāpasmāra-sahitāḥ prītoktāḥ vyabhicāriṇaḥ ।। yaśodāpi mahābhāgā naṣṭa-labdha-prajā satī ।
pariṣvajāṅkam āropya mumocāśru-kalāṃ muhuḥ ।। naladendīvara-candana-śriyam । vahati sparśa-mahotsavas tava ।। sambhramādi-cyutā yā syād anukampe anukampituḥ ।
ratiḥ saivātra vātsalyaṃ sthāyī bhāvo nigadyate ।। yaśodādes tu vātsalya-ratiḥ prauḍhā nisargataḥ । premavat snehavad bhāti kadācit kila rāgavat ।। nandaḥ sva-putram ādāya pretyāgatam udāra-dhīḥ ।
mūrdhny upāghrāya paramāṃ mudaṃ lebhe kurūdvaha ।। bhūyaḥ prasrava-varṣiṇī dviguṇitotkaṇṭhā pradoṣodaye । govindasya muhur vrajendra-gṛhiṇī panthānam ālokate ।। stūyamānam asi mukta-sambhramā ।
prasnutā kuru-bhuvi nyavīviśat ।। bhūyobhir vasudeva-nandanatayāpy udghūṣyamāṇe janaiḥ । premā vallava-nāthayor atitarām ullāsam evāyayau ।। kālindī ca vilocanābja-janitair jātāñjana-śyāmalaiḥ ।
vṛttāsi vraja-rājñi tat-suta-mukha-prekṣāṃ sphuṭaṃ vāñchasi ।। bhavantam avalokate yadi mukunda goṣṭheśvarī । sthitā yadi na tatra te vadana-padmam udvīkṣyate ।। sampādayiṣyati kadā nayanotsavaṃ naḥ ।
ūrvī tvarā jayati devaka-nandinīnām ।। mama sandiśa gāndinī-putra । didṛkṣate tvāṃ hare kuntī ।। yaśodā varṇyamānāni putrasya caritāṇi ca ।
śṛṇvaty aśrūṇy asrākṣīt sneha-snuta-payodharā ।। paśya srasta-tanuḥ kaṭhora-luṭhanair dehe vraṇaṃ kurvatī । krośantī karayor yugena kurute kaṣṭād uras-tāḍanam ।। bahūnām api sad-bhāve viyoge atra tu kecana ।
cintā viṣāda-nirveda-jāḍya-dainyāni cāpalam । unmāda-mohāv ity ādyā atyudrekaṃ vrajanty amī ।। dvandvaṃ locanayoś cirād avicala-vyābhugna-tāraṃ sthitam । nūnaṃ vallava-rājñi putra-virahodghūrṇābhir ākramyase ।।
nava-taruṇimārambhonmṛṣṭaṃ na ramyam alokayam । śirasi kuliśaṃ hanta kṣiptaṃ śvaphalka-sutena me ।। yayā na hi hareḥ śiraḥ snuta-kucāgram āghrāyate । sa luñcati na cañcalaḥ surabhi-gandhi yāsāṃ dadhi ।।
goṣṭhe karāmbhoruha-maṇḍano abhūt । daṇḍākṛtis te jananī babhūva ।। tvāṃ radais tṛṇam udasya yaśodā । matsaraṃ tyaja mamānaya vatsam ।।
vrajapatir iti brūte mugdho ayam atra mudā janaḥ । kaṭhina-hṛdayo goṣṭhe svairī praviśya sukhīyati ।। sa babhrāmābhyarṇe bhaṇata tam udantaṃ madhukarāḥ । bhavantaṃ pṛcchantī diśi diśi yaśodā vicarati ।।
prasāraya dṛśaṃ manāk tava sutaḥ puro vartate । sa śocati tava prasūṃ yadu-kulendra nandaḥ pitā ।। vilocanābhīṣṭa-vilokanaṃ harim । devyaḥ kṣaṇād ānakadundubhi-priyāḥ ।।
tāḥ putram aṅkam āropya sneha-snuta-payodharāḥ । harṣa-vihvalitātmānaḥ siṣicur netrajair jalaiḥ ।। paripatadbhir asau payasāṃ jharaiḥ । sva-tanayaṃ praṇayād abhiṣiñcati ।।
vinihita-nayaneyaṃ tvan-mukhendor mukunda । tava muhur atiharṣād varṣati kṣīra-dhārām ।। svīkurvate rasam imaṃ nāṭya-jñā api kecana ।। sphuṭaṃ camatkāritayā vatsalaṃ ca rasaṃ viduḥ ।
sthāyī vatsalatāsyeha putrādy-ālambanaṃ matam ।। apratītau hari-rateḥ prītasya syād apuṣṭatā । preyasas tu tirobhāvo vatsalaysāsya na kṣatiḥ ।। eṣā rasa-trayī proktā prītādiḥ paramādbhutā ।
tatra keṣucid apy asyāḥ saṅkulatvam udīryate ।। saṅkarṣaṇasya sakhyas tu prīti-vātsalya-saṅgatam । yudhiṣṭhirasya vātsalyaṃ prītyā sakhyena cānvitam ।। āhuka-prabhṛtīnāṃ tu prītir vātsalya-miśritā ।
jarad-ābhīrikādīnāṃ vātsalyaṃ sakhya-miśritam ।। mādreya-nāradādīnāṃ sakhyaṃ prītyā karambitam । rudra-tārkṣyoddhavādīnāṃ prītiḥ sakhyena miśritā ।। aniruddhāpi-naptṝṇām evaṃ kecid babhāṣire ।
evaṃ keṣucid anyeṣu vijñeyaṃ bhāva-miśraṇam ।। iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhau paścima-vibhāge mukhya-bhakti-rasa-pañcaka-nirūpaṇe vatsala-bhakti-rasa-laharī caturthī । ātmocitair vibhāvādyaiḥ puṣṭiṃ nītā satāṃ hṛdi । madhurākhyo bhaved bhakti-raso asau madhurā ratiḥ ।।
nivṛttānupayogitvād durūhatvād ayaṃ rasaḥ । rahasyatvāc ca saṃkṣipya vitatāṇgo vilikhyate ।। tatra ālambanāḥ asmin ālambanaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ priyās tasya tu subhruvaḥ ।। tatra kṛṣṇaḥ asamānordhva-saundarya-līlā-vaidigdhī-sampadām ।
āśrayatvena madhure harir ālambano mataḥ ।। śreṇī-śyāmala-komalair upanayann aṅgair anaṅgotsavam । śṛṅgāraḥ sakhi mūrtimān iva madhau mugdho hariḥ krīḍati ।। praṇaya-taraṅga-karambitās taraṅgāḥ ।
praṇamata tāḥ paramādbhutāḥ kiśorīḥ ।। preyasīṣu harer āsu pravarā vārṣabhānavī ।। vadana-damita-rākārohiṇī-kānta-kīrtiḥ । madhurima-madhu-pātrī rājate paśya rādhā ।।
śrotrasyānta-taṭīm api sphuṭam anādhāya sthitodyan-mukhī । maitrī-gauravato apy asau śata-guṇāṃ mat-prītim evādadhe ।। kaṃsārir api saṃsāra-vāsanābaddha-śṛṅkhalām । rādhām ādhāya hṛdaye tatyāja vraja-sundarīḥ ।।
atha uddīpanāḥ । uddīpanā iha proktā muralī-nisvanādayaḥ ।। gṛha-pati-caritaṃ ca dāruṇaṃ kim api । śiva śiva muralī murārāteḥ ।।
atha anubhāvāḥ anubhāvās tu kathitā dṛg-natekṣā-smitādayaḥ ।। rādhāyāḥ smita-candrikā-suradhunī-pure nipīyāmṛtam । krāntvā sapta jaganti samprati vayaṃ sarvordhvam adhyāsmahe ।। vācaḥ sa-gadgada-padāḥ sakhi kampi vakṣaḥ ।
cetaḥ sudhāṃśu-vadane taralīkaroti ।। atha vyabhicāriṇaḥ ālasyaugrye vinā sarve vijñeyā vyabhicāriṇaḥ ।। mā siñca sāndra-makaranda-rasena vāyo । nālambituṃ katham api kṣamate adya jīvaḥ ।।
kuvalaya-dala-lakṣmī-laṅgimāḥ svāṅga-bhāsaḥ । kavalayati dhṛtiṃ me kṣmādharāraṇya-dhūrtaḥ ।। atha sthāyī sthāyī bhāvo bhavaty atra pūrvoktā madhurā ratiḥ ।। kaṅkelli-koraka-karambita-karṇa-pūraḥ ।
vaṃśīraveṇa sakhi mām avaśīkaroti ।। rādhā-mādhavayor eva kvāpi bhāvaiḥ kadāpy asau । sajātīya-vijātīyair naiva vicchidyate ratiḥ ।। dṛśor agre candrāvalir upari śailasya danujaḥ ।
anta-śrīr lolā taḍid iva mukundasya valate ।। brahmiṣṭha-śvasanaḥ śama-stuti-kathā prāleyam āsiñcati । rādhāyās tad api praphullam abhajan mlāniṃ na bhāvāmbujam ।। sa vipralambha-sambhoga-bhedena dvi-vidho mataḥ ।।
sa pūrva-rāgo mānaś ca pravāsādi-mayas tathā । vipralambho bahu-vidho vidvadbhir iha kathyate ।। tatra pūrva-rāgaḥ prāg-asaṅgatayor bhāvaḥ pūrva-rāgo bhaved dvayoḥ ।। vrajantyā dṛṣṭo yo nava-jaladhara-śyāmala-tanuḥ ।
mano me vyālolaṃ kvacana gṛha-kṛtyo na lagate ।। yathā vinidrā yac cittā rukmiṇī kamalekṣaṇā । tathāham api tac-citto nidrāṃ ca na labhe niśi । vedāhaṃ rukmiṇyā dveṣān mamodvāho nivāritaḥ ।।
atha mānaḥ । mānaḥ prasiddha evātra ।। vigalita-nijotkarṣād īṛsyā-vaśena gatānyataḥ । mukhara-nikhare līnā dīnāpy uvāca rahaḥ sakhīm ।।
atha pravāsaḥ pravāsaḥ saṅga-vicyutiḥ ।। aśrānta-locana-jala-snapitānanāyāḥ । nidrā-lavo api kuta eva saroruhākṣyāḥ ।। bhagavān api govindaḥ kandarpa-śara-pīḍitaḥ ।
na bhuṅkte na svapiti ca cintayan vo hy aharniśam ।। atha sambhogaḥ dvayor militayor bhogaḥ sambhoga iti kīrtyate ।। parirambha-kauśala-vikāśi-bhāvayā । niravāhayac chikhi-śikhaṇḍa-śekharaḥ ।।
śrīmad-bhāgavatādy-arha-śāstra-darśitayā dṛśā । iyam āviṣkṛtā mukhya-pañca-bhakti-rasā mayā ।। gopāla-rūpa-śobhāṃ dadhad api raghunātha-bhāva-vistārī । tuṣyatu sanātanātmā paścima-bhāge rasāmbu-nidheḥ ।।
iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhau paścima-vibhāge madhurākhya-bhakti-rasa-laharī caturthī । iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhau mukhya-bhakti-rasa-nirūpakaḥ paścima-vibhāgaḥ samāptaḥ । bhakti-bhareṇa prītiṃ kalayann urarīkṛta-vrajāsaṅgaḥ । tanutāṃ sanātanātmā bhagavān mayi sarvadā tuṣṭim ।।
rasāmṛtābdher bhāge atra turīye tūttārābhidhe । rasaḥ sapta-vidho gauṇo maitrī-vaira-sthitir mithaḥ ।। rasābhāsāś ca tenātra laharyo nava kīrtitāḥ । prāg atrāniyatādhārāḥ kadācit kvāpy uditvarāḥ ।।
gauṇā bhakti-rasāḥ sapta lekhyā hāsyādayaḥ kramāt ।। bhaktānāṃ pañcadhoktānām eṣāṃ madhyata eva hi । kvāpy ekaḥ kvāpy anekaś ca gauṇeṣv ālambano mataḥ ।। vakṣyamāṇair vibhāvādyaiḥ puṣṭiṃ hāsa-ratir gatā ।
hāsya-bhakti-raso nāma budhair eṣa nigadyate ।। asminn ālambanaḥ kṛṣṇas tathānyo api tad-anvayī । vṛddhāḥ śiśu-mukhāḥ prāyaḥ proktā dhīrais tad-āśrayāḥ । vibhāvanādi-vaiśiṣṭyāt pravarāś ca kvacin matāḥ ।।
mātar neṣyati māṃ pidhāya kapaṭād ādhārikāyām asau । hāsyaṃ tasya niruddhato apy atitarāṃ vyaktaṃ tadāsīn muneḥ ।। atha tad-anvayī yac ceṣṭā kṛṣṇa-viṣayā proktaḥ so atra tad-anvayī ।। niśamya jaratī-giraṃ vivṛta-komalauṣṭhe sthite ।
harau jahasur uddhuraṃ kim api suṣṭhu goṣṭhārbhakāḥ ।। tathyaṃ hanta cirāyur eṣa bhavitā kiṃ dhenu-koṭīśvaraḥ । drāg āvirbhavad-uddhura-smitam idaṃ vaktraṃ tvayā rudhyate ।। uddīpanā hares tādṛg-vāg-veṣa-caritādayaḥ ।
anubhāvās tu nāsauṣṭha-gaṇḍa-niṣpandanādayaḥ ।। harṣālasyāvahitthādyā vijñeyā vyabhicāriṇaḥ । sā hāsa-ratir evātra sthāyi-bhāvatayoditā ।। ṣoḍhā hāsa-ratiḥ syāt smita-hasite vihasitāvahasite ca ।
apahasitātihasitake jyeṣṭhādīnāṃ kramād dve dve ।। vibhāvanādi-vaicitryād uttamasyāpi kutracit । bhaved vihasitādyaṃ ca bhāvajñair iti bhaṇyate ।। tatra smitam smitaṃ tv alakṣya-daśanaṃ netra-gaṇḍa-vikāśa-kṛt ।।
pradhāvati javena māṃ subala maṅkṣu rakṣāṃ kuru । vikasvara-mukhāmbujaṃ kulam abhūn munīnāṃ divi ।। hasitam tad eva dara-saṃlakṣya-dantāgraṃ hasitaṃ bhavet ।। paśyety acyuta-jalpa-viśvasitayā saṃrambha-rajyad-dṛśā ।
putre prāṅgataḥ sakhī-kulam abhūd dantāṃśu-dhautādharam ।। vihasitam sa-svanaṃ dṛṣṭa-daśanaṃ bhaved vihasitaṃ tu tat ।। sa-niḥśvasita-ḍambaraṃ jaṭilayātra nidrāyate । kṛtaṃ hasitam utsvanaṃ kapaṭa-suptayā vṛddhayā ।।
avahasitam tac cāvahasitaṃ phulla-nāsaṃ kuñcita-locanam ।। prātaḥ putra balasya vā kim asitaṃ vāsas tvayāṅge dhṛtam । dūtī saṅkucad-īkṣaṇāvahasitaṃ jātā na roddhuṃ kṣamā ।। apahasitam tac cāpahasitaṃ sāśru-locanaṃ kampitāṃsakam ।।
yad abhrāṇy uddaṇḍo daśana-rucibhiḥ pāṇḍarayati । jaratyāḥ prastobhān naṭati tad anaiṣīd dṛśam asau ।। atihasitam sahasra-tālaṃ kṣiptāṅgaṃ tac cātihasitaṃ viduḥ ।। tvām udvoḍhum asau balī-mukha-varo māṃ sādhayaty utsukaḥ ।
ity uccair mukharā-girā vijahasuḥ sottālikā bālikāḥ ।। yasya hāsaḥ sa cet kvāpi sākṣān naiva nibadhyate । tathāpy eṣa vibhāvādi-sāmarthyād upalabhyate ।। tvaṃ jīryad-duli-dṛṣṭir oṣṭha-tulitāṅgārā mṛdaṅgodarī ।
puṇyena vraja-subhruvāṃ tava dhṛtiṃ hartuṃ na vaṃśī kṣamā ।। eṣa hāsya-rasas tatra kaiśikī-vṛtti-vistṛtau । śṛṅgārādi-rasodbhedo bahudhaiva prapañcitaḥ ।। iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhāv uttara-vibhāge hāsya-bhakti-rasa-nirūpaṇe adbhuta-bhakti-rasa-laharī prathamā ।।
ātmocitair vibhāvādyaiḥ svādyatvaṃ bhakta-cetasi । sā vismaya-ratir nītād- bhuto-bhakti-raso bhavet ।। bhaktaḥ sarva-vidho apy atra ghaṭate vismayāśrayaḥ । lokottara-kriyā-hetur viṣayas tatra keśavaḥ ।।
tasya ceṣṭā-viśeṣādyās tasminn uddīpanā matāḥ । kriyās tu netra-vistāra-stambhāśru-pulakādayaḥ ।। āvega-harṣa-jāḍyādyās tatra syur vyabhicāriṇaḥ । sthāyī syād vismaya-ratiḥ sā lokottara-karmataḥ ।
sākṣād anumitaṃ ceti tac ca dvividham ucyate ।। tatra sākṣāt, yathā sākṣād aindriyakaṃ dṛṣṭa-śruta-saṅkīrtitādikam ।। mandireṣu yugapan nikhileṣu । spandanojjhita-tanur munir āsīt ।।
citraṃ bataitad ekena vapuṣā yugapat pṛthak । gṛheṣu dvy-aṣṭa-sāhasraṃ striya eka udāvahat ।। govardhanaḥ śikhara-ruddha-ghanaḥ kva cāyam । khelann iva sphurati hanta kim indra-jālam ।।
pratyekam acchinadamuni śara-trayeṇa । sphārekṣaṇaḥ kṣitipatiḥ pulakī tadāsīt ।। vatsāś ceti vadan kṛto asmi vivaśaḥ stambha-śriyā paśyata । stūyante jagad-aṇḍavadbhir abhitas te hanta padmāsanaiḥ ।।
bhāṇḍīraṃ punar atulya vilokayantaḥ । unmuktāṃ manasi camatkriyām avāpuḥ ।। apriyādeḥ kriyā kuryān nālaukiky api vismayam । asādhāraṇy api manāk karoty eva priyasya sā ।।
priyāt priyasya kim uta sarva-lokottarottarā । ity atra vismaye proktā raty-anugraha-mādhurī ।। iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhāv uttara-vibhāge gauṇa-bhakti-rasa-nirūpaṇe adbhuta-bhakti-rasa-laharī dvitīyā ।। saivotsāha-ratiḥ sthāyī vibhāvādyair nijocitaḥ ।
ānīyamānā svādyatvaṃ vīra-bhakti-raso bhavet ।। yuddha-dāna-dayā-dharmaiś caturdhā-vīra ucyate । ālambana iha prokta eṣa eva caturvidhaḥ ।। utsāhas tv eṣa bhaktānāṃ sarveṣām eva sambhavet ।।
paritoṣāya kṛṣṇasya dadhad utsāham āhave । sakhā bandhu-viśeṣo vā yuddha-vīra ihocyate ।। pratiyoddhā mukundo vā tasmin vā prekṣake sthite । tadīyecchāveśenātra bhaved anyaḥ suhṛd-varaḥ ।।
caṭulaṃ tvām abhibhūya mādhava । yadi na tvaṃ samarāt parāñcasi ।। kālindī-puline vayasya-nikarair ālokyamānas tadā । śrīdāmnaś ca bakī-dviṣaś ca samarāṭopaḥ paṭīyān abhūt ।।
tathādya laguḍaṃ kramād bhramayati sma dāmā kṛtī । samṛddha-pulako yathā laguḍa-pañjarāntaḥ-sthitam ।। prāyaḥ prakṛta-śūrāṇāṃ sva-pakṣair api karhicit । yuddha-keli-samutsāho jāyate paramādbhutaḥ ।।
tathā ca hari-vaṃśe tathā gāṇḍīva-dhanvānaṃ vikrīḍan madhusūdanaḥ । jigāya bharata-śreṣṭhaṃ kuntyāḥ pramukhato vibhuḥ ।। iti । katthitāsphoṭa-vispardhā-vikramāstra-grahādayaḥ । pratiyodha-sthitāḥ santo bhavanty uddīpanā iha ।। jitvā dāmodara yudhi vṛthā mā kṛthāḥ katthitāni ।
mandradhvāno naṭati nikaṭe stokakṛṣṇaḥ kalāpī ।। katthitādyāḥ sva-saṃsthāś ced anubhāvāḥ prakīrtitāḥ । tathaivāhopuruṣikā kṣveḍitākrośa-valganam ।। asahāye api yuddhecchā samarād apalāyanam ।
bhītābhaya-pradānādyā vijñeyāś cāpare budhaiḥ ।। māṃ keśisūdana vidann api bhadrasenam । divyārgalā pratibhaṭas trapate bhujo me ।। nibadhnaty ullāsād bhuja-samara-caryā-samucitam ।
sudāmnaḥ sotkaṇṭhaṃ jayati muhur āhopuruṣikā ।। catuṣṭaye api vīrāṇāṃ nikhilā eva sāttvikāḥ । garvāvega-dhṛti-vrīḍā-mati-harṣāvahitthikāḥ । amarṣotsukatāsūyā-smṛty-ādyā vyabhicāriṇaḥ ।।
yuddhotsāha-ratis tasmin sthāyi-bhāvatayoditā । yā svaśakti-sahāyādyair āhāryā sahajāpi vā । jigīṣā stheyasī yuddhe sā yuddhotsāha īryate ।। āhūyamānaḥ puruṣottamena ।
prodyamya daṇḍaṃ bhramayāñcakāra ।। mā tvaṃ bhaiṣīḥ kṣudra re bhadrasena । śrīdāmāhaṃ kṛṣṇam evāhvayeya ।। payodhim iva mandaraḥ kṛta-mukunda-pakṣa-grahaḥ ।
hareḥ pramadam ekakaḥ samiti bhadraseno vyadhāt ।। bhaja bhaṅgaṃ na hi saṅgarāditaḥ । sa-virūpaṃ vibruvan hariṃ yayau ।। dāmodarasya vijayāya kṛtī sudāmā ।
jāto maṇiḥ sujaṭito vara-hāṭakena ।। suhṛd eva pratibhaṭo vīre kṛṣṇasya na tvariḥ । sa bhakta-kṣobha-kāritvād raudre tv ālambano rase । rāgābhāvo dṛg-ādīnāṃ raudrād asya vibhedakaḥ ।।
dvi-vidho dāna-vīraḥ syād ekas tatra bahu-pradaḥ । upasthita-durāpārtha-tyāgī cāpara ucyate ।। sahasā dīyate yena svayaṃ sarvasvam apy uta । dāmodarasya saukhyāya procyate sa bahu-pradaḥ ।।
sampradānasya vīkṣādyā asminn uddīpanā matāḥ । vāñchitādhika-dātṛtvaṃ smita-pūrvābhibhāṣaṇam ।। sthairya-dākṣiṇya-dhairyādyā anubhāvā ihoditāḥ । vitarkautsukya-harṣādyā vijñeyā vyabhicāriṇaḥ ।।
dānotsāha-ratis tv atra sthāyi-bhāvatayoditā । pragāḍhā stheyasī ditsā dānotsāha itīryate ।। dvidhā bahu-prado apy eṣa vidvadbhir iha kathyate । syād ābhyudayikas tv ekaḥ paras tat-sampradānakaḥ ।।
kṛṣṇasyābhyudayārthaṃ tu yena sarvasvam arpyate । arthibhyo brāhmaṇādibhyaḥ sa ābhyudāyiko bhavet ।। vyatarad amala-cetāḥ sañcayaṃ naicikīnām । iti nijagadur uccair bhūsurā yena tṛptāḥ ।।
jñātaye haraye svīyam ahaṃtā-mamatāspadam । sarvasvaṃ dīyate yena sa syāt tat-sampradānakaḥ ।। tad-dānaṃ prīti-pūjābhyāṃ bhaved ity uditaṃ dvidhā ।। tatra prīti-dānam prīti-dānaṃ tu tasmai yad dadyād bandhv-ādi-rūpiṇe ।।
śreṇiṃ māṇikya-bhājaṃ gaja-ratha-turagān karburān karbureṇa । deyaṃ kutrāpy adṛṣṭvā makha-sadasi tadā vyākulaḥ pāṇḍavo abhūt ।। pujā-dānaṃ pujā-dānaṃ tu tasmai yad vipra-rūpāya dīyate ।। bhavanta āmnāya-vidhāna-kovidāḥ ।
dāsyāmy amuṣmai kṣitim īpsitāṃ mune ।। lakṣmī-payodharotsaṅga-kuṅkumāruṇito hareḥ । balinaiva sa yenāsya bhikṣā-pātrīkṛtaḥ karaḥ ।। upasthita-durāpārtha-tyagy asau yena neṣyate ।
hariṇā dīyamāno api sārṣṭy-ādis tuṣyatā varaḥ ।। pūrvato atra viparyasta-kārakatvaṃ dvayor bhavet । asminn uddīpanāḥ kṛṣṇa-kṛpālāpa-smitādayaḥ ।। anubhāvās tad-utkarṣa-varṇana-draḍhimādayaḥ ।
atra sañcāritā bhūmnā dhṛter eva samīkṣyate ।। tyāgotsāha-ratir dhīraiḥ sthāyī bhāva ihoditaḥ । tyāgecchā tādṛśī prauḍhā tyāgotsāha itīryate ।। tvāṃ prāptavān deva-munīndra-guhyam ।
svāmin kṛtārtho asmi varaṃ na yāce ।। kiṃ vānyad arpita-bhayaṃ bhruva unnayais te । kīrtanya-tīrtha-yaśasaḥ kuśalā rasa-jñāḥ ।। ayam eva bhavann uccaiḥ prauḍha-bhāva-viśeṣa-bhāk ।
dhuryādīnāṃ tṛtīyasya vīrasya padavīṃ vrajet ।। kṛpārdra-hṛdayatvena khaṇḍaśo deham arpayan । kṛṣṇāyācchanna-kṛpāya dayā-vīra ihocyate ।। uddīpanā iha proktās tad-ārti-vyañjanādayaḥ ।
nija-prāṇa-vyayenāpi vipanna-trāṇa-śīlatā ।। āśvāsanoktayaḥ sthairyam ity ādyās tatra vikriyāḥ । autsukyam atiharṣādyā jñeyāḥ sañcāriṇo budhaiḥ ।। dayotsāha-ratis tv atra sthāyi-bhāva udīryate ।
dayodreka-bhṛd utsāho dayotsāha ihoditaḥ ।। yenārdhaṃ kapaṭa-dvijāya vapuṣaḥ kaṃsa-dviṣe ditsatā । sollāsaṃ krakacena dāritam abhūt patnī-sutābhyāṃ śivaḥ ।। hareś cet tattva-vijñānaṃ naivāsya ghaṭate dayā ।
tad-abhāve tv asau dāna-vīre antar-bhavati sphuṭam ।। vaiṣṇavatvād ratiḥ kṛṣṇe kriyate anena sarvadā । kṛtātra dvija-rūpe ca bhaktis tenāsya bhaktatā ।। antar-bhāvaṃ vadanto asya dāna-vīre dayātmanaḥ ।
vopadevādayo dhīrā vīram ācakṣate tridhā ।। kṛṣṇaika-toṣaṇe dharme yaḥ sadā pariniṣṭhitaḥ । prāyeṇa dhīra-śāntas tu dharma-vīraḥ sa ucyate ।। uddīpanā iha proktāḥ sac-chāstra-śravaṇādayaḥ ।
anubhāvā nayāstikya-sahiṣṇutva-yamādayaḥ ।। dharmotsāha-ratir dhīraiḥ sthāyī bhāva ihocyate । dharmaikābhiniveśas tu dharmotsāho mataḥ satām ।। puram abhi puru-hūte nityam evopahūte ।
suciram araci śacyāḥ savya-hastāṅka-śāyī ।। yajñaḥ pūjā-viśeṣo asya bhujādy-aṅgāni vaiṣṇavaḥ । dhyātvendrādy-āśrayatvena yad eṣv āhutir arpyate ।। ayaṃ tu sākṣāt tasyaiva nideśāt kurute makhān ।
yudhiṣṭhiro ambudhiḥ premṇāṃ mahā-bhāgavatottamaḥ ।। dānādi-trividhaṃ vīraṃ varṇayantaḥ parisphuṭam । dharma-vīraṃ na manyante katicid dhanikādayaḥ ।। iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhāv uttara-vibhāge vīra-bhakti-rasa-nirūpaṇe adbhuta-bhakti-rasa-laharī tṛtīyā ।।
ātmocitair vibhāvādyair nītā puṣṭiṃ satāṃ hṛdi । bhavec choka-ratir bhakti-raso hi karuṇābhidhaḥ ।। avyucchinna-mahānando apy eṣa prema-viśeṣataḥ । aniṣṭāpteḥ padatayā vedyaḥ kṛṣṇo asya ca priyaḥ ।।
tathānavāpta-tad-bhakti-saukhyaś ca sva-priyo janaḥ । ity asya viṣayatvena jñeyā ālambanās tridhā ।। tat-tad-vedī ca tad-bhakta āśrayatvena ca tridhā । so apy aucityena vijñeyaḥ prāyaḥ śāntādi-varjitaḥ ।
tat-karma-guṇa-rūpādyā bhavaty uddīpanā iha ।। anubhāvā mukhe śoṣo vilāpaḥ srasta-gātratā । śvāsa-krośana-bhūpāta-ghātoras tāḍanādayaḥ ।। atrāṣṭau sāttvikā jāḍya-nirveda-glāni-dīnatāḥ ।
cintā-viṣāda-autsukya-cāpalonmāda-mṛtyavaḥ । ālasyāpasmṛti-vyādhi-mohādyā vyabhicāriṇaḥ ।। hṛdi śokatayāṃśena gatā pariṇatiṃ ratiḥ । uktā śoka-ratiḥ saiva sthāyī bhāva ihocyate ।।
ālokya tat-priya-sakhāḥ paśupā bhṛśārtāḥ । duḥkhānuśoka-bhayam ūḍha-dhiyo nipetuḥ ।। skhalad-aśiśira-bāṣpa-stoma-dhautottarīyā । viṣam agatim avasthāṃ goṣṭha-rājasya rājñī ।।
kṛṣṇa-priyāṇām ākarṣe śaṅkha-cūḍena nirmite । nīlāmbarasya vaktrendur nīlimānaṃ muhur dadhe ।। svayambhū-cūḍāgrair lulita-śikharāḥ pāda-nakharāḥ । sa devarṣir muktān api tanu-bhṛtaḥ śocati bhṛśam ।।
sāndrānanda-sudhābdhir eṣa yuvayor nābhūd dṛśāṃ gocaraḥ । govindasya padāravinda-yugala-proddāma-kānti-cchaṭām ।। ratiṃ vināpi ghaṭate hāsyāder udgamaḥ kvacit । kadācid api śokasya nāsya sambhāvanā bhavet ।।
rater bhūmnā kraśimnā ca śoko bhūyān kṛśaś ca saḥ । ratyā sahāvinā-bhāvāt kāpy etasya viśiṣṭatā ।। kṛṣṇaiśvaryādy-avijñānaṃ kṛtaṃ naiṣām avidyayā । kintu premottara-rasa-viśeṣeṇaiva tat kṛtam ।।
ataḥ prādurbhavan śoko labdhāpy udbhaṭatāṃ muhuḥ । durūhām eva tanute gatiṃ saukhyasya kām api ।। iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhāv uttara-vibhāge gauṇa-bhakti-rasa-nirūpaṇe karuṇa-bhakti-rasa-laharī caturthī ।। nītā krodha-ratiḥ puṣṭiṃ vibhāvādyair nijocitaiḥ ।
hṛdi bhakta-janasyāsau raudra-bhakti-raso bhavet ।। kṛṣṇo hito ahitaś ceti krodhasya viṣayas tridhā । kṛṣṇe sakhī-jaraty-ādyāḥ krodhasyāśrayatāṃ gatāḥ । bhaktāḥ sarva-vidhā eva hite caivāhite tathā ।।
tatra kṛṣṇe sakhyāḥ krodhaḥ sakhī-krodhe bhavet sakhyāḥ kṛṣṇād atyāhite sati ।। nāyaṃ vañcana-sañcaya-praṇayinaṃ hāsaṃ tathāpy ujjhati । hā medhāvini rādhike tava kathaṃ premā garīyān abhūt ।। tatra jaratyāḥ krodhaḥ krodho jaratyā vadhv-ādi-sambandhe prekṣite harau ।।
tavorasi nirīkṣyate bata na neti kiṃ jalpasi । vrajeśvara-sutena me suta-gṛhe agnir utthāpitaḥ ।। govardhanaṃ mahā-mallaṃ vinānyeṣāṃ vrajaukasām । sarveṣām eva govinde ratiḥ prauḍhā virājate ।।
atha hitaḥ hitas tridhānavahitaḥ sāhasī cerṣyur ity api ।। kṛṣṇa-pālana-kartāpi tat-karmābhiniveśataḥ । kvacit tatra pramatto yaḥ prokto anavahito atra saḥ ।। vṛthaiva dhik paṇḍita-māninī tvam ।
baddhaḥ suto asau sakhi bambhramīti ।। atha sāhasī yaḥ prerako bhaya-sthāne sāhasī sa nigadyate ।। tālānāṃ vipinam iti sphuṭaṃ niśamya । ḍimbhānāṃ vraja-pati-gehinī dadarśa ।।
atha īrṣyuḥ īrṣyur māna-dhanā proktā prauḍherṣyākrānta-mānasā ।। dūraṃ prayāhi savidhe tava jājjvalīmi । nirmañchitāgra-caraṇāpy aruṇānanāsi ।। atha ahitaḥ ahitaḥ syād dvidhā svasya hareś ceti prabhedataḥ ।।
tatra svasyāhitaḥ ahitaḥ svasya sa syād yaḥ kṛṣṇa-sambandha-bādhakaḥ ।। mā maryādām yadu-kula-bhuvām bhindhire gāndineyaḥ । vitrastānāṃ parivavalire vallavīnāṃ vilāpāḥ ।। atha harer ahitaḥ ahitas tu hares tasya vairi-pakṣo nigadyate ।।
sphurac-caraṇa-paṅkaje apy avamatiṃ vyanakty atra yaḥ । trir asya mukuṭopari sphuṭam udīrya savyaṃ padam ।। solluṇṭha-hāsa-vakrokti-kaṭākṣānādarādayaḥ । kṛṣṇāhita-hitasthāḥ syur amī uddīpanā iha ।।
hasta-nispeṣaṇaṃ danta-ghaṭṭanaṃ rakta-netratā । daṣṭauṣṭhatātibhrū-kuṭī bhujāsphālana-tāḍanāḥ ।। tuṣṇīkatā natāsyatvaṃ niśvāso bhugna-dṛṣṭitā । bhartsanaṃ mūrdha-vidhūtir dṛg-ante pāṭala-cchaviḥ ।।
bhrū-bhedādhara-kampādyā anubhāvā ihoditāḥ । atra stambhādayaḥ sarve prākaṭyaṃ yānti sāttvikāḥ ।। āvego jaḍatā garvo nirvedo moha-cāpale । asūyaugryaṃ tathāmarṣa-śramādyā vyabhicāriṇaḥ ।।
atra krodha-ratiḥ sthāyī sa tu krodhas tridhā mataḥ । kopo manyus tathā roṣas tatra kopas tu śatru-gaḥ ।। manyur bandhuṣu te pūjya-sama-nyūnās tridhoditāḥ । roṣas tu dayite strīṇām ato vyabhicaraty asau ।।
hasta-peṣādayaḥ kope manyau tuṣṇīkatādayaḥ । dṛg-anta-pāṭalatvādyā roṣe tu kathitāḥ kriyāḥ ।। mṛdhe magadha-bhūpatau kim api vaktram ākrośati । dahad-iṅgala-pravala-piṅgalāṃ lāṅgalī ।।
dhāvantyāṃ bhaya-bhāji vistṛta-bhujo rundhe puraḥ paddhatim । mātaś caṇḍi mayā śikhaṇḍa-mukuṭād ātmābhirakṣyaḥ katham ।। tava girā jaṭile niṭile ca me । duhitaraṃ duhitur mama pāmari ।।
hāraś cakāsti hari-kaṇṭha-taṭī-cariṣṇuḥ । kuṭena māṃ tad api vañcayate vadhūṭī ।। asmin na tādṛśo manyau vartate raty-anugrahaḥ । udāharaṇa-mātrāya tathāpy eṣa nidarśitaḥ ।।
krodhāśrayāṇāṃ śatrūṇāṃ caidyādīnāṃ svabhāvataḥ । krodho rati-vinābhāvān na bhakti-rasatāṃ vrajet ।। iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhāv uttara-vibhāge gauṇa-bhakti-rasa-nirūpaṇe raudra-bhakti-rasa-laharī pañcamī ।। vakṣyamāṇair vibhāvādyaiḥ puṣṭiṃ bhaya-ratir gatā ।
bhayānakābhidho bhakti-raso dhīrair udīryate ।। kṛṣṇaś ca dāruṇāś ceti tasminn ālambanā dvidhā । anukampyeṣu sāgassu kṛṣṇas tasya ca bandhuṣu ।। dāruṇāḥ snehataḥ śaśvat-tad-aniṣṭhāpti-darśiṣu ।
darśanāc chravaṇāc ceti smaraṇāc ca prakīrtitāḥ ।। viśvasya prakṛtiṃ bhajasva na manāg apy asti mantuṃ tava । pṛthvī pratyuta yuddha-kautuka-mayī sevaiva me nirmitā ।। laghu-haram iti kārṣīr mā sma dīnāya manyum ।
aśaraṇam atimūḍhaṃ rakṣa rakṣa prasīda ।। gopendra gopaya balād uparudhya bālam । śṛṅgāṇi laṅghayati paśya turaṅga-daityaḥ ।। gokulaṃ kila viśantam uddhuram ।
śuṣyad-āsya-jalajā vrajeśvarī ।। tanum iyam adhunāpi smaryamāṇā dhunoti । vapur atipuruṣaṃ yā ghoram āviścakāra ।। vibhāvasya bhrū-kuṭy-ādyās tasminn uddīpanā matāḥ ।
mukha-śoṣaṇam ucchvāsaḥ parāvṛtya vilokanam ।। sva-saṅgopanam udghūrṇā śaraṇānveṣaṇaṃ tathā । krośanādyāḥ kriyāś cātra sāttvikāś cāśru-varjitāḥ ।। iha santrāsa-maraṇa-cāpalāvega-dīnatāḥ ।
viṣāda-mohāpasmāra-śaṅkādyā vyabhicāriṇaḥ ।। asmin bhagna-ratiḥ sthāyī bhāvaḥ syād aparādhataḥ । bhīṣaṇebhyaś ca tatra syād bahudhaivāparādhitā ।। taj-jā bhīr nāparatra syād anugrāhya-janān vinā ।
ākṛtyā ye prakṛtyā ye ye prabhāveṇa bhīṣaṇāḥ ।। etad-ālambanā bhītiḥ kevala-prema-śāliṣu । nārī-bālādiṣu tathā prāyeṇātropajāyate ।। ākṛtyā pūtanādyāḥ syuḥ prakṛtyā duṣṭa-bhū-bhujaḥ ।
bhīṣaṇās tu prabhāveṇa surendra-giriśādayaḥ ।। sadā bhagavato bhītiṃ gatā ātyantikīm api । kaṃsādyā rati-śūnyatvād atra nālambanā matāḥ ।। iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhāv uttara-vibhāge gauṇa-bhakti-rasa-nirūpaṇe bhayānaka-bhakti-rasa-laharī ṣaṣṭhī ।।
puṣṭiṃ nija-vibhāvādyair jugupsā-ratir āgatā । asau bhakti-raso dhīrair bībhatsākhya itīryate ।। asminn āśrita-śāntādyā dhīrair ālambanā matāḥ ।। kurvan pūrvam aśeṣa-ṣiḍga-nagarī sāmrājya-caryām abhūt ।
dṛṣṭe strī-vadane vikūṇita-mukho viṣṭabhya niṣṭhīvati ।। atra niṣṭhīvanaṃ vaktra-kūṇanaṃ ghrāṇa-saṃvṛtiḥ । dhāvanaṃ kampa-pulaka-prasvedādyāś ca vikriyāḥ ।। iha glāni-śramonmāda-moha-nirveda-dīnatāḥ ।
viṣāda-cāpalāvega-jāḍyādyo vyabhicāriṇaḥ ।। jugupsā-ratir atra syāt sthāyī sā ca vivekajā । prāyikī ceti kathitā jugupsā dvi-vidhā budhaiḥ ।। jāta-kṛṣṇa-rater bhakta-viśeṣasya tu kasyacit ।
vivekotthā tu dehādau jugupsā syād vivekajā ।। piśita-vimiśrita-visra-gandha-bhāji । bhagavati hanta rater lave apy udīrṇe ।। amedhya-pūty-anubhavāt sarveṣām eva sarvataḥ ।
yā prāyo jāyate seyaṃ jugupsā prāyikī matā ।। vasann eṣa klinno jaḍa-tanur ahaṃ mātur udare । tad asmin kaṃsāre kuru mayi kṛpā-sāgara kṛpām ।। srasta-vyādhita-yūtha-gūtha-ghaṭanā-nirdhūta-netrāyuṣi ।
kṣiptās te smṛtim ākalayya naraka-dhvaṃsinn iha prāṇimaḥ ।। labdha-kṛṣṇa-rater eva suṣṭhu pūtaṃ manaḥ sadā । kṣubhyaty ahṛdy aleśe api tato asyāṃ raty-anugrahaḥ ।। hāsyādīnāṃ rasatvaṃ yad gauṇatvenāpi kīrtitam ।
prācāṃ matānusāreṇa tad vijñeyaṃ manīṣibhiḥ ।। amī pañcaiva śāntādyā harer bhakti-rasā matāḥ । eṣu hāsyādayaḥ prāyo bibhrati vyabhicāritām ।। iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhāv uttara-vibhāge gauṇa-bhakti-rasa-nirūpaṇe bībhatsa-bhakti-rasa-laharī saptamī ।।
athāmīṣāṃ krameṇaiva śāntādīnāṃ parasparam । mitratvaṃ śātravatvaṃ ca rasānām abhidhīyate ।। śāntasya prīta-bībhatsa-dharma-vīrāḥ suhṛd-varāḥ । adbhutaś caiṣa prītādiṣu catuḥṣv api ।।
dviṣann asya śucir yuddhavīro raudro bhayānakaḥ ।। suhṛt-prītasya bībhatsaḥ śānto vīra-dvayaṃ tathā । vairī śucir yuddha-vīro raudraś caika-vibhāvakaḥ ।। preyasas tu śucir hāsyo yuddha-vīraḥ suhṛd-varāḥ ।
dviṣo vatsala-bībhatsa-raudrā bhīṣmaś ca pūrvavat ।। vatsalasya suhṛd-dhāsyaḥ karuṇo bhīṣma-bhit tathā । śatruḥ śucir yuddha-vīraḥ prīto raudraś ca pūrvavat ।। śucer hāsyas tathā preyān suhṛd asya prakīrtitaḥ ।
dviṣo vatsala-bībhatsa-śānta-raudra-bhayānakāḥ । prāhur eke asya suhṛdaṃ vīra-yugmaṃ pare ripum ।। mitraṃ hāsyasya bībhatsaḥ śuciḥ preyān savatsalaḥ । pratipakṣas tu karuṇas tathā prokto bhayānakaḥ ।।
adbhutasya suhṛd vīraḥ pañca śāntādayas tathā । pratipakṣo bhaved asya raudro bībhatsa eva ca ।। vīrasya tv adbhuto hāsyaḥ preyān prītis tathā suhṛt । bhayānako vipakṣo asya kasyacic chānta eva ca ।।
karuṇasya suhṛd-raudro vatsalaś ca vilokyate । vairī hāsyo asya sambhoga-śṛṅgāraś cādbhutas tathā ।। raudrasya karuṇaḥ prokto vīraś cāpi suhṛd-varaḥ । pratipakṣas tu hāsye asya śṛṅgāro bhīṣaṇo api ca ।।
bhayānakasya bībhatsaḥ karuṇaś ca suhṛd-varaḥ । dviṣantu vīra-śṛṅgāra-hāsya-raudrāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।। bībhatsasya bhavec chānto hāsyaḥ prītis tathā suhṛt । śatruḥ śucis tathā preyān jñeyā yuktyā pare ca te ।।
tatra suhṛt-kṛtyam kathitebhyaḥ pare ye syus te taṭasthāḥ satāṃ matāḥ ।। suhṛdā miśraṇāṃ samyag āsvādaṃ kurute rasam ।। dvayos tu miśraṇe sāmyaṃ duḥśakaṃ syāt tulā-dhṛtam । tasmād aṅgāṅgi-bhāvena melanaṃ viduṣāṃ matam ।।
bhaven mukhyo atha vā gauṇo raso aṅgī kila yatra yaḥ । kartavyaṃ tatra tasyāṅgaṃ suhṛd eva raso budhaiḥ ।। athāṅgitvaṃ prathamato mukhyānām iha likhyate । aṅgatāṃ yatra suhṛdo mukhyā gauṇāś ca bibhrati ।।
jīva-sphuliṅga-vahner mahaso ghana-cit-svarūpasya । tasya padāmbuja-yugalaṃ kiṃ vā saṃvāhayiṣyāmi ।। atra mukhye aṅgini mukhyasyāṅgatā । pṛthu-kutupe kutukī rataḥ śarīre ।
sukha-vapuṣaḥ smaraṇe api mantharo asmi ।। atra mukhya eva gauṇasya । prīty-utsikta-manāḥ kadāham asakṛd-dustarka-caryāspadam । seviṣye cala-cāru-cāmara-marut-sañcāra cāturyataḥ ।।
atra mukhya eva mukhyasya gauṇayoś ca । niravadyaḥ pratipadya-mādhurīm । prabhumindīvara-sundaraṃ bhaje ।। atra mukhye mukhyasya ।
smaran prabhu-pādāmbhojaṃ naṭann aṭati vaiṣṇavaḥ । yas tu dṛṣṭyā padminīnām api suṣṭhu hṛṇīyate ।। atra mukhye gauṇasya । na tṛpyati na sarvataḥ sukha-maye samādhāv api ।
prabho tava padārcane param upaiti tṛṣṇāṃ manaḥ ।। atra mukhye mukhyasya gauṇayoś ca । dhanyānāṃ kila mūrdhanyāḥ subalāmur vrajābalāḥ । adharaṃ piñcha-cūḍasya calāś culūkayanti yāḥ ।।
atra mukhye mukhyasya । vitarkayasi māṃ yathā na hi tathāsmi kiṃ bhūriṇā । dadarśa subalo balad-vikaca-dṛṣṭir asyānanam ।। atra mukhye gauṇasya ।
praviśati subalo ayaṃ rādhikā-veṣa-gūḍhaḥ । smita-vikaśita-gaṇḍaṃ svīyam āsyaṃ vṛṇoti ।। atra mukhye mukhya-gauṇayoḥ । nirātapatraḥ kāntāre santataṃ mukta-pādukaḥ ।
vatsān avati vatso me hanta santapyate manaḥ ।। atra mukhye gauṇasya । vinyasyāpasasāra tasya kaṇikāṃ nidrāṇa-ḍimbhānane । smerāṃ nikṣipatī sadā bhavatu vaḥ kṣemāya goṣṭheśvarī ।।
atrāpi mukhye gauṇasya । savye doṣṇi vikāśi-gaṇḍa-phalakā līlāsya-bhaṅgī-śate । pātu prasnava-sicyamāna-sicayā viśvaṃ vrajādhīśvarī ।। atrāpi mukhye catūrṇāṃ gauṇānām ।
kevale vatsale nāsti mukhyasya khalu sauhṛdam । ato atra vatsale tasya natarāṃ likhitāṅgatā ।। vinyasya mañju-bhuja-mūrdhni bhujaṃ mukundaḥ । sandeśam arpayati tanvi mad-artham eva ।।
atra mukhye mukhyasya । kuru praṇaya-nirbharaṃ mama kṛśāṅgi kaṇṭha-graham । kṛtaṃ smitam abhijñayā guru-puras tadā rādhayā ।। atra mukhye gauṇasya ।
smara-smerām ārād dṛśam asakalām arpayati ca । ibhāri-kṣveḍābhir vṛṣa-danujam udyojayati ca ।। atra mukhye mukhya-gauṇayoḥ । hāsyādīnāṃ tu gauṇānāṃ yad-udāharaṇaṃ kṛtam ।
tenaiṣām aṅgitā vyaktā mukhyānāṃ ca tathāṅgatā । tathāpy alpa-viśeṣāya kiñcid eva vilikhyate ।। prasabhaṃ pīta-paṭāñcale dhṛte । harir utphulla-kapolam ānanam ।।
atra gauṇe aṅgini mukhyasyāṅgatā । māṃ yoddhuṃ milasi puraḥ kathaṃ viśāla । śrīdāmā gaṇayati re tvam atra ko asi ।। atrāpi gauṇe aṅgini mukhyasya ।
śiśupālaṃ samare jighāṃsubhiḥ । jagṛhe pāṇḍu-sutair varāyudham ।। atra gauṇe mukhya-gauṇayoḥ । yaṣṭyā durbalayā vijitya purataḥ solluṇṭham udgāyataḥ ।
kṛṣṇaḥ phulla-kapolakaḥ pulakavān visphāra-dṛṣṭir babhau ।। atra gauṇe mukhyasya gauṇayoś ca । evam anyasya gauṇasya jñeyā kavibhir aṅgitā । tathā ca mukhya-gauṇānāṃ rasānām aṅgatāpi ca ।।
so aṅgī sarvātigo yaḥ syān mukhyo gauṇo athavā rasaḥ । sa evāṅgaṃ bhaved aṅgi-poṣī sañcāritāṃ vrajan ।। eka eva bhavet sthāyī raso mukhyatamo hi yaḥ । rasās tad-anuyāyitvād anye syur vyabhicāriṇaḥ ।।
rasānāṃ samavetānāṃ yasya rūpaṃ bhaved bahu । sa mantavyo rasaḥ sthāyī śeṣāḥ saṅcāriṇo matāḥ ।। stokād vibhāvanāj jātaḥ samprāpya vyabhicāritām । puṣṇan nija-prabhuṃ mukhyaṃ gauṇas tatraiva līyate ।।
prodyan vibhāvanotkarṣāt puṣṭiṃ mukhyena lambhitaḥ । kuñcatā nija-nāthena gauṇo apy aṅgitvam aśnute ।। mukhyas tv aṅgatvam āsādya puṣṇann indram upendravat । gauṇam evāṅginaṃ kṛtvā nigūḍha-nija-vaibhavaḥ ।।
anādi-vāsanodbhāsa-vāsite bhakta-cetasi । bhāty eva na tu līnaḥ syād eṣa sañcāri-gauṇavat ।। aṅgī mukhyaḥ svam atrāṅgair bhāvais tair abhivardhayan । sajātīyair vijātīyaiḥ svatantraḥ san virājate ।।
yasya mukhyasya yo bhakto bhaven nitya-nijāśrayaḥ । aṅgī sa eva tatra syān mukhyo apy anyo aṅgatāṃ vrajet ।। āsvādodreka-hetutvam aṅgasyāṅgatvam aṅgini । tad vinā tasya sampāto vaiphalyāyaiva kalpate ।।
yathā mṛṣṭa-rasālāyāṃ yavasādeḥ kathañcana । tac-carvaṇe bhaved eva satṛṇābhyavahāritā ।। janayaty eva vairasyaṃ rasānāṃ vairiṇā yutiḥ । sumṛṣṭa-pānakādīnāṃ kṣāra-tiktādinā yathā ।।
kālo bhūyān hā samādhi-vratena । koṇenākṣṇaḥ sāci-savyasya naikṣi ।। tatra śāntasyojjvalena vairasyam । sura-muni-vandita-pādam indireśam ।
prabhum īkṣitaṃ mano me ।। tatra prītasyojjvalenaiva । dorbhyām argala-dīrghābhyāṃ sakhe parirabhasva mām । śiraḥ kṛṣṇa tavāghrāya vihariṣye tatas tvayā ।।
atra preyaso vatsalena । sātvatās tu bhagavantam uśanti । vyāji-hīrṣatu kathaṃ mama jihvā ।। atra vatsalasya prītena ।
taḍid-vilāsa-taralā nava-yauvana-sampadaḥ । adyaiva dūti tena tvaṃ mayā ramaya mādhavam ।। atrojjvalasya śāntena । ciraṃ jīveti saṃyujya kācid āśīrbhir acyutam ।
kailāsa-sthā vilāsena kāmukī pariṣaṣvaje ।। atra śucer vatsalena । śuceḥ sambandha-gandho api kathañcid yadi vatsale । kvacid bhavet tataḥ suṣṭhu vairasyāyaiva kalpate ।।
piśitāsṛṅ-mayī nāhaṃ satyam asmi tavocitā । svāpāṅga-biddhāṃ śyāmāṅga kṛpayāṅgī-kuruṣva mām ।। atra śucer bībhatsena । evam anyāpi vijñeyā prājñai rasa-virodhitā ।
prāyeṇeyaṃ rasābhāsa-kakṣāyāṃ paryavasyati ।। dvāyor ekatarasyeha bādhyatvenopavarṇane । smaryamāṇatayāpy uktau sāmyena vacane api ca ।। rasāntareṇa vyavadhau taṭa-sthena priyeṇa vā ।
viṣayāśraya-bhede ca gauṇena dviṣatā saha । ity ādiṣu na vairasyaṃ vairiṇo janayed yutiḥ ।। bālāsau viṣayeṣu dhitsati tataḥ pratyāharantī manaḥ । mugdheyaṃ kila tasya paśya hṛdayān niṣkrāntim ākāṅkṣati ।।
bādhyatvam atra śāntasya śucer utkarṣa-varṇanāt ।। vrajasya hāsodgama-saṃvidhātā । karoti hā naḥ paridevanāni ।। viśrānta-ṣoḍaśa-kalā nirvikalpā nirāvṛtiḥ ।
sukhātmā bhavatī rādhe brahma-vidyeva rājate ।। rādhā śāntir ivonnidraṃ nirnimeṣekṣaṇaṃ ca mām । kurvatī dhyāna-lagnaṃ ca vāsayaty adri-kandare ।। draṣṭuṃ paraṃ brahma kutas tatākṣī ।
rambhe samāviśya bhidā smareṇa ।। atrādbhutena vyavadhiḥ । māṃsāsthi-rakta-kṛmi-viṭ-kapha-pitta-vātam । yā te padābja-makarandam ajighratī strī ।।
tatrāsmākaṃ yad-avadhi sakhe dṛṣṭir eṣā niviṣṭā । smāraṃ smāraṃ mukha-kuṭilatā-kāriṇīyaṃ hṛṇīyā ।। ubhayatra śuci-bībhatsayoḥ । sthala-bhuvi sambhṛta-sāṃyugīna-līlam ।
pulaka-kulaṃ dviṣatāṃ tu kālimānam ।। atra vīra-bhayānakayoḥ । viṣayāśraya-bhede api mukhyena dviṣatā saha । saṅgatiḥ kila mukhyasya vairasyāyaiva jāyate ।।
vimocayārgalābandhaṃ vilambaṃ tāta nācara । yāmi kāśya-gṛhaṃ yūnā manaḥ śyāmena me hṛtam ।। atra śuceḥ prītena । rukmiṇī-kuca-kāśmīra-paṅkiloraḥ-sthalaṃ kadā ।
sadānandaṃ paraṃ brahma dṛṣṭyā seviṣyate mayā ।। atra śāntasya śucinā । anurakta-dhiyo bhaktāḥ kecana jñāna-vartmani । śāntasyāśraya-bhinnatve vairasyaṃ nānumanvate ।।
bhṛtyayor nāyakasyeva nisarga-dveṣiṇor api । aṅgayor aṅginaḥ puṣṭyai bhaved ekatra saṅgatiḥ ।। gariṣṭho ayaṃ keśī girivad iti me vellati manaḥ । khalaṃ kṣundan kuryāṃ vrajam atitarāṃ śālinam aham ।।
atra vidviṣau vīrabhayānakau vatsalaṃ puṣṇītaḥ । yathā kamprā svedini cūrṇa-kuntala-taṭe ity ādi ।। tatra hāsya-karuṇau vatsalam eva puṣṇītaḥ । mitho vairāv api dvau yau bhāvau dharma-sutādiṣu ।
kālādi-bhedat prākaṭyaṃ tau vindantau na duṣyataḥ ।। adhirūḍhe mahā-bhāve viruddhair virasāḥ yutiḥ । na syād ity ujjvale rādhā-kṛṣṇayor darśitaṃ purā ।। kvāpy acintya-mahā-śaktau mahā-puruṣa-śekhare ।
rasāvali-samāveśaḥ svādāyaivopajāyate ।। gaṇḍaunnatyaṃ khaleśāḥ pralayam ṛṣigaṇā dhyāna-muṣṇāsram ambāḥ । lāsyaṃ dāsāḥ kaṭākṣaṃ yayur asita-dṛśaḥ prekṣya raṅge mukundam ।। thūtkārī dadhni visre praṇayiṣu vivṛta-prauḍhir indre aruṇākṣaḥ ।
āsāre sphāra-dṛṣṭir yuvatiṣu pulakī bibhrad adriṃ vibhur vaḥ ।। iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhāv uttara-vibhāge rasānāṃ maitrī-vaira-sthiti-nāmnī laharī aṣṭamī ।। pūrvam evānuśiṣṭena vikalā rasa-lakṣaṇā । rasā eva rasābhāsā rasa-jñair anukīrtitāḥ ।।
syus tridhoparasāś cānu-rasāś cāparasāś ca te । uttamā madhyamāḥ proktāḥ kaniṣṭhāś cety amī kramāt ।। prāptaiḥ sthāyi-vibhāvānu-bhāvādyais tu virūpatām । śāntādayo rasā eva dvādaśoparasā matāḥ ।।
brahma-bhāvāt para-brahmaṇy advaitādhikya-yogataḥ । tathā bībhatsa-bhūmādeḥ śānto hy uparaso bhavet ।। vijñāna-suṣamādhaute samādhau yad udañcati । sukhaṃ dṛṣṭe tad evādya purāṇa-puruṣe tvayi ।।
taṃ tam eva kalayāmi bhavantam । tvāṃ vinā kim api nāparam asti ।। kṛṣṇasyāgre atidhārṣṭyena tad-bhakteṣv avahelayā । svābhīṣṭa-devatānyatra paramotkarṣa-vīkṣayā ।
maryādātikramādyaiś ca prītoparasatā matā ।। avadhīryamāṇa-naṭano apy anargalaḥ । caṭulo baṭu-vyavṛṇutātmano ratim ।। ekasminn eva sakhyena hari-mitrādy-avajñayā ।
yuddha-bhūmādinā cāpi preyānuparaso bhavet ।। chalito narma-girā stutiṃ cakāra । hariṇā daṇḍavad agrataḥ papāta ।। sāmarthyādhikyābhijñānāl lālanādy-aprayatnataḥ ।
karuṇasyātirekādes turyāś coparaso bhavet ।। unmāthaṃ sapadi tavātmajād apaśyam । drāghiṣṭhām api samitiṃ prapadyamāne ।। atha śṛṅgāroparasaḥ । tatra sthāyi-vairūpyam
dvayor ekatarasyaiva ratir yā khalu dṛśyate । yān ekatra tathaikasya sthāyinaḥ sā virūpatā । vibhāvasyaiva vairūpyaṃ sthāyiny atropacaryate ।। saṅgopitaś ca sahajo api dṛśos taraṅgaḥ ।
ahnāya kāpi gaitri aṅkuritām ayāsīt ।। atyantābhāva evātra rateḥ khalu vivakṣitaḥ । etasyāḥ prāg-abhāve tu śucir noparaso bhavet ।। agre dharaṇyāṃ sakhi kāma-pālam ।
bhinnādya sādhvi smarato dvidhāsi ।। kecit tu nāyakasyāpi sarvathā tulya-rāgataḥ । nāyikāsv apy anekāsu vadanty uparasaṃ śucim ।। vaidagdhyaujjvalya-viraho vibhāvasya virūpatā ।
latā-paśu-pulindīṣu vṛddhāsv api sa vartate ।। madhu-mathanena kaṭākṣitātha mṛdvī । ratim iha pallavitāṃ hṛdi vyanakti ।। pataṅga-kanyā-puline adya dhanyāḥ ।
sānaṅga-raṅgāṃ dṛśam arpayanti ।। kālindī-puline paśya pulindī pulakācitā । harer dṛk-cāpalaṃ vīkṣya sahajaṃ yā vighūrṇate ।। bilva-yugma-racitonnata-stanī ।
smerayaty aghaharaṃ jaraty asau ।। sthāyino atra virūpatvam eka-rāgatayāpi cet । ghaṭetāsau vibhāvasya virūpatve apy udāhṛtiḥ ।। śucitvaujjvalya-vaidigdhyāt suveśatvāc ca kathyate ।
śṛṅgārasya vibhāvatvam anyatrābhāsatā tataḥ ।। samayānāṃ vyatikrāntir grāmyatvaṃ dhṛṣṭāpi ca । vairūpyam anubhāvāder manīṣibhir udīritam ।। samayāḥ khaṇḍitādīnāṃ priye roṣoditādayaḥ ।
puṃsaḥ smitādayaś cātra priyayā tāḍanādiṣu । eteṣām anyathā-bhāvaḥ samayānāṃ vyatikramaḥ ।। kāntā-nakhāndhito apy adya parihṛtya hare hriyam । kailāsa-vāsinīṃ dāsīṃ kṛpā-dṛṣṭyā bhajasva mām ।।
bāla-śabdādy-upanyāso virasokti-prapañcanam । kaṭī-kaṇḍūtir ity ādyaṃ grāmyatvaṃ kathitaṃ budhaiḥ ।। kiṃ naḥ phaṇi-kiśorīṇāṃ tvaṃ puṣkara-sadāṃ sadā । muralī-dhvaninā nīvīṃ gopa-bāla vilumpasi ।।
atha dhṛṣṭatā prakaṭa-prārthanādiḥ syāt sambhogādes tu dhṛṣṭatā ।। kānta kailāsa-kuñjo ayaṃ ramyāhaṃ nava-yauvanā । tvaṃ vidagdho asi govinda kiṃ vā vācyam ataḥ param ।। evam eva tu gauṇānāṃ hāsādīnām api svayam ।
vijñeyoparasatvasya manīṣibhir udāhṛtiḥ ।। bhaktādibhir vibhāvādyaiḥ kṛṣṇa-sambandha-varjitaiḥ । rasā hāsyādayaḥ sapta śāntaś cānurasā matāḥ ।। markaṭī bhrū-kuṭībhis tathoddhuram ।
hāsa-ḍambara-karambitānanam ।। vedānta-tantre śuka-maṇḍalasya । romāñcitāṅgaś ca surarṣir āsīt ।। evam evātra vijñeyā vīrāder apy udāhṛtiḥ ।।
aṣṭāv amī taṭastheṣu prākaṭyaṃ yadi bibhrati । kṛṣṇādibhir vibhāvādyair gatair anubhavādhvani ।। kṛṣṇa-tat-pratipakṣaś ced viṣayāśrayatāṃ gatāḥ । hāsādīnāṃ tadā te atra prājñair aparasā matāḥ ।।
palāyamānam udvīkṣya capalāyata-locanam । kṛṣṇam ārāj jarāsandhaḥ solluṇṭham ahasīn muhuḥ ।। evam anye api vijñeyās te adbhutāparasādayaḥ । uttamās tu rasābhāsāḥ kaiścid rasatayoditāḥ ।।
bhāvāḥ sarve tad-ābhāsā rasābhāsāś ca kecana । amī prokta-rasābhijñaiḥ sarve api rasanād rasāḥ ।। bhāratādyāś catasras tu rasāvasthāna-sūcikāḥ । vṛttayo nāṭya-mātṛtvād uktā nāṭaka-lakṣaṇe ।।
granthasya gaurava-bhayād asyā bhakti-rasa-śriyaḥ । samāhṛtiḥ samāsena mayā seyaṃ vinirmitā ।। gopāla-rūpa-śobhāṃ dadhad api raghunātha-bhāva-visārī । tuṣyatu sanātano asminn uttara-bhāge rasāmṛtāmbhodheḥ ।।
iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhāv uttara-vibhāge rasābhāsa-laharī navamī ।। iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhau gauṇa-bhakti-rasa-nirūpaṇo nāma caturtho vibhāgaḥ samāptaḥ । rāmāṅga-śatru-gaṇite śāke gokulam adhiṣṭhitenāyam । bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhur viṭaṅkitaḥ kṣudra-rūpeṇa ।।
samāpto ayaṃ śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhuḥ ।।
